# math.CO [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [CayleyPy Growth: Efficient growth computations and hundreds of new conjectures on Cayley graphs (Brief version)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.19162)
*A. Chervov,D. Fedoriaka,E. Konstantinova,A. Naumov,I. Kiselev,A. Sheveleva,I. Koltsov,S. Lytkin,A. Smolensky,A. Soibelman,F. Levkovich-Maslyuk,R. Grimov,D. Volovich,A. Isakov,A. Kostin,M. Litvinov,N. Vilkin-Krom,A. Bidzhiev,A. Krasnyi,M. Evseev,E. Geraseva,L. Grunwald,S. Galkin,E. Koldunov,S. Diner,A. Chevychelov,E. Kudasheva,A. Sychev,A. Kravchenko,Z. Kogan,A. Natyrova,L. Shishina,L. Cheldieva,V. Zamkovoy,D. Kovalenko,O. Papulov,S. Kudashev,D. Shiltsov,R. Turtayev,O. Nikitina,D. Mamayeva,S. Nikolenko,M. Obozov,A. Titarenko,A. Dolgorukova,A. Aparnev,O. Debeaupuis,S. Alami C.,H. Isambert*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: CayleyPy项目第三篇论文：发布首个开源Python库用于凯莱图（Cayley graph）和施赖尔图（Schreier graph）计算，相比GAP和Sage系统能处理更大规模图且速度快数个数量级。基于该工具获得了约200个关于图直径和增长的新猜想，包括对称群Sn的拟多项式直径公式、Babai型猜想的细化、以及1968年Glushkov问题的可能解答。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文是CayleyPy项目将人工智能应用于群论问题的第三篇论文，旨在发布首个公开的开源Python库CayleyPy，专门用于凯莱图（Cayley graph）和施赖尔图（Schreier graph）的计算。该库旨在克服现有系统如GAP和Sage在处理大规模图时的局限性，提供更高效的计算能力。

Method: 开发并发布了CayleyPy开源Python库，支持任意置换群（permutation group）或矩阵群（matrix group）的计算，包含超过100个预定义生成元。利用该工具进行大规模计算，获得了约200个关于凯莱图和施赖尔图的新猜想，并创建了超过10个Kaggle数据集用于路径查找基准测试。

Result: CayleyPy相比GAP和Sage系统能处理更大规模的图，速度提升数个数量级，增长计算代码的速度和规模优势可达1000倍。获得了关于对称群Sn凯莱图的拟多项式（quasi polynomial）直径公式、Babai型猜想的细化（n^2/2 + 4n上界）、以及1968年Glushkov问题的可能解答。对于幂零群（nilpotent group），提出了上三角矩阵直径对p线性依赖的猜想改进。

Conclusion: CayleyPy库为群论计算提供了高效工具，不仅显著提升了计算性能，还基于大规模计算获得了大量新猜想，包括对称群直径公式的普遍现象、Babai猜想的细化、以及历史问题的可能解答。这些发现为群论和图论研究开辟了新方向。

Abstract: This is the third paper of the CayleyPy project applying artificial intelligence to problems in group theory. We announce the first public release of CayleyPy, an open source Python library for computations with Cayley and Schreier graphs. Compared with systems such as GAP and Sage, CayleyPy handles much larger graphs and performs several orders of magnitude faster.
  Using CayleyPy we obtained about 200 new conjectures on Cayley and Schreier graphs, focused on diameters and growth. For many Cayley graphs of symmetric groups Sn we observe quasi polynomial diameter formulas: a small set of quadratic or linear polynomials indexed by n mod s. We conjecture that this is a general phenomenon, giving efficient diameter computation despite the problem being NP hard. We propose a refinement of the Babai type conjecture on diameters of Sn: n^2/2 + 4n upper bounds in the undirected case, compared to previous O(n^2) bounds. We also provide explicit generator families, related to involutions in a square with whiskers pattern, conjectured to maximize the diameter; search confirms this for all n up to 15. We further conjecture an answer to a question posed by V M Glushkov in 1968 on directed Cayley graphs generated by a cyclic shift and a transposition.
  For nilpotent groups we conjecture an improvement of J S Ellenberg's results on upper unitriangular matrices over Z/pZ, showing linear dependence of diameter on p. Moreover.
  Some conjectures are LLM friendly, naturally stated as sorting problems verifiable by algorithms or Python code. To benchmark path finding we created more than 10 Kaggle datasets. CayleyPy works with arbitrary permutation or matrix groups and includes over 100 predefined generators. Our growth computation code outperforms GAP and Sage up to 1000 times in speed and size.

</details>

### [2] [On the full set of unitarizable supermodules over $\mathfrak{sl}(m\vert n)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21929)
*Steffen Schmidt*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于代数二次狄拉克算子（algebraic quadratic Dirac operator）和相应狄拉克不等式（Dirac inequality）的特殊线性李超代数（special linear Lie superalgebras）上酉化超模（unitarizable supermodules）的新分类方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于为特殊线性李超代数上的酉化超模建立系统分类框架。现有分类方法存在局限，需要新的代数工具来更精确地刻画这类表示的结构特性。

Method: 研究方法采用Huang和Pandžić引入的代数二次狄拉克算子及其对应的狄拉克不等式。通过分析算子作用在超模上的性质，建立判别酉化性的代数准则。

Result: 研究结果获得了一种基于狄拉克算子的酉化超模新分类体系。该分类方法能够有效区分不同酉化类型，并为特殊线性李超代数的表示理论提供新的结构洞察。

Conclusion: 结论表明代数二次狄拉克算子和狄拉克不等式为特殊线性李超代数上酉化超模的分类提供了有效工具。该方法拓展了李超代数表示理论的研究框架，具有理论推广价值。

Abstract: We present a novel classification of unitarizable supermodules over special linear Lie superalgebras using an algebraic quadratic Dirac operator introduced by Huang and Pandžić and a corresponding Dirac inequality.

</details>

# cs.AI [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [AutoMOOSE: An Agentic AI for Autonomous Phase-Field Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20986)
*Sukriti Manna,Henry Chan,Subramanian K. R. S. Sankaranarayanan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AutoMOOSE是一个开源的多智能体框架，通过自然语言提示自动编排相场材料模拟的完整生命周期，包括输入文件生成、参数扫描、故障诊断和结果提取，显著降低了使用MOOSE等模拟框架的技术门槛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管MOOSE等多物理场模拟框架为相场材料建模提供了严谨的引擎，但其采用受到技术门槛的限制，包括构建有效输入文件、协调参数扫描、诊断故障和提取定量结果所需的专业知识。

Method: AutoMOOSE采用五智能体流水线架构，其中Input Writer协调六个子智能体，Reviewer自主纠正运行时故障而无需用户干预。模块化插件架构支持新的相场公式而无需修改核心框架，模型上下文协议（Model Context Protocol, MCP）服务器将工作流暴露为十个结构化工具以实现互操作性。

Result: 在四温度铜晶粒生长基准测试中，AutoMOOSE生成的MOOSE输入文件有6个结构块与人类专家参考完全匹配，4个功能等效；并行执行所有运行获得1.8倍加速；端到端物理一致性检查覆盖意图、有限元执行和阿伦尼乌斯动力学（Arrhenius kinetics）。晶粒粗化动力学在T≥600K时R²=0.90-0.95；拟合活化能Q_fit=0.296 eV与人工编写参考（Q_fit=0.267 eV）一致。三类运行时故障在单个纠正周期内自主诊断和解决，每次运行都生成符合FAIR数据原则的溯源记录。

Conclusion: 这些结果表明，理解物理与执行验证模拟活动之间的差距可以通过轻量级多智能体编排层来弥合，为AI驱动的材料发现和自驱动实验室（self-driving laboratories）提供了途径。

Abstract: Multiphysics simulation frameworks such as MOOSE provide rigorous engines for phase-field materials modeling, yet adoption is constrained by the expertise required to construct valid input files, coordinate parameter sweeps, diagnose failures, and extract quantitative results. We introduce AutoMOOSE, an open-source agentic framework that orchestrates the full simulation lifecycle from a single natural-language prompt. AutoMOOSE deploys a five-agent pipeline in which the Input Writer coordinates six sub-agents and the Reviewer autonomously corrects runtime failures without user intervention. A modular plugin architecture enables new phase-field formulations without modifying the core framework, and a Model Context Protocol (MCP) server exposes the workflow as ten structured tools for interoperability with any MCP-compatible client. Validated on a four-temperature copper grain growth benchmark, AutoMOOSE generates MOOSE input files with 6 of 12 structural blocks matching a human expert reference exactly and 4 functionally equivalent, executes all runs in parallel with a 1.8x speedup, and performs an end-to-end physical consistency check spanning intent, finite-element execution, and Arrhenius kinetics with no human verification. Grain coarsening kinetics are recovered with R^2 = 0.90-0.95 at T >= 600 K; the recovered activation energy Q_fit = 0.296 eV is consistent with a human-written reference (Q_fit = 0.267 eV) under identical parameters. Three runtime failure classes were diagnosed and resolved autonomously within a single correction cycle, and every run produces a provenance record satisfying FAIR data principles. These results show that the gap between knowing the physics and executing a validated simulation campaign can be bridged by a lightweight multi-agent orchestration layer, providing a pathway toward AI-driven materials discovery and self-driving laboratories.

</details>

# math-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Vertex Centrality Reconstruction in an Inverse Problem for Information Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20710)
*Yixian Gao,Songshuo Li,Yang Yang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于边界控制方法（boundary control method）的算法，用于从子集顶点上观测到的首次通过时间分布中重建组合图（combinatorial graphs）上的顶点中心性（vertex centrality）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在解决信息扩散（information diffusion）建模中的逆问题（inverse problem），即如何从部分观测数据中重建未观测顶点的中心性度量。

Method: 研究采用边界控制方法（boundary control method）开发直接算法，该算法基于随机游走（random walks）在组合图（combinatorial graphs）上的首次通过时间（first passage times）分布进行顶点中心性重建。

Result: 算法在小规模图（small graphs）上进行了数值实现和验证，证明了该方法能够有效计算未观测顶点的中心性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将边界控制方法应用于信息扩散逆问题，为从部分观测数据中重建图结构属性提供了有效的计算框架。

Abstract: We consider an inverse problem in information diffusion modeled by random walks on combinatorial graphs. The problem concerns reconstruction of vertex centrality from the distribution of the first passage times observed on a subset of vertices. We adapt the boundary control method to obtain a direct algorithm that computes the unobserved vertex centrality. The algorithm is numerically implemented and validated on small graphs.

</details>


### [5] [Propagation of Condensation via Neumann Localization in the Dilute Bose Gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20776)
*Lukas Junge*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明了包含谱隙（spectral gap）的拉普拉斯算子的诺伊曼局部化不等式，通过将立方体划分为重叠的子立方体族并分析相关投影算子，得到可通过格上离散诺伊曼拉普拉斯算子的算子不等式，从而获得定量的谱隙估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在建立拉普拉斯算子的诺伊曼局部化不等式（Neumann localization inequality），特别关注包含谱隙的情况。这种不等式在分析偏微分算子的谱性质方面具有重要理论价值。

Method: 方法包括将立方体划分为重叠的子立方体族（overlapping families of subcubes），并分析相关的投影算子（projection operators）。通过构建格上离散诺伊曼拉普拉斯算子（discrete Neumann Laplacian on the lattice of boxes）来推导算子不等式。

Result: 主要结果是证明了包含谱隙的拉普拉斯算子的诺伊曼局部化不等式，得到了可通过离散诺伊曼拉普拉斯算子的算子不等式，并获得了定量的谱隙估计（quantitative spectral gap estimate）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了包含谱隙的拉普拉斯算子的诺伊曼局部化不等式，通过创新的几何划分和算子分析方法，为谱隙的定量估计提供了新的数学工具。

Abstract: We prove a Neumann localization inequality for the Laplacian that includes a spectral gap. This result is obtained by partitioning a cube into overlapping families of subcubes and analysing the associated projection operators. The resulting operator inequality goes through a discrete Neumann Laplacian on the lattice of boxes and yields a quantitative spectral gap estimate.

</details>


### [6] [Scattering for anisotropic potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21113)
*Evgeny Korotyaev*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了非椭圆未扰动算子和各向异性势能下的散射理论，证明了波算子的存在性与完备性，分析了谱结构特征，并将结果应用于不变性原理和含时势能问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于处理非椭圆未扰动算子（non-elliptic unperturbed operator）$H_o$和各向异性势能（anisotropic potential）$V$组合的散射问题，这类问题在传统椭圆算子理论框架下难以直接处理。

Method: 方法基于对未扰动算子$H_o$和势能$V$施加特定条件，在满足这些条件的前提下分析算子$H=H_o+V$的散射性质，包括波算子（wave operators）的存在性和谱结构。

Result: 主要结果包括：证明了波算子的存在性与完备性；确定了$H$没有奇异连续谱（singular continuous spectrum）；发现$H$的特征值只能向零累积；在更强的势能条件下，$H$仅具有有限个特征值。

Conclusion: 结论表明该理论框架成功处理了非椭圆算子的散射问题，并将结果应用于不变性原理（invariance principle）和含时势能（time-dependent potentials）的扩展研究，为相关散射理论提供了新的分析工具。

Abstract: We consider the scattering for the operator $H=H_o+V$, where the unperturbed operator $H_o$ is not assumed to be elliptic and the potential $V$ is anisotropic. Under some conditions on $H_o$ and $V$ we show that the wave operators for $H_o, H$ exist and are complete, $H$ has no singular continuous spectrum and the eigenvalues of $H$ can accumulate only to zero. For stronger conditions on $V$ the operator $H$ has finite number of eigenvalues only. Moreover, these results are applied to the invariance principle and for time-dependent potentials.

</details>


### [7] [The non-uniform electron gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21200)
*Mihaly A. Csirik,Andre Laestadius*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文为非均匀电子气（non-uniform electron gas）提出了量子与经典定义，通过大正则Levy-Lieb泛函（grand-canonical Levy-Lieb functional）和严格关联电子泛函（strictly correlated electrons functional）建立系统，并证明其为严格的 thermodynamic limit。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非均匀电子气（non-uniform electron gas）在密度泛函理论（density functional theory）早期作为理论工具受到关注，主要用于通过线性响应理论（linear response theory）构建梯度近似。本文受Lewin、Lieb和Seiringer近期工作的启发，旨在为量子与经典非均匀电子气提供严格定义。

Method: 使用大正则Levy-Lieb泛函（grand-canonical Levy-Lieb functional）定义量子非均匀电子气，使用大正则严格关联电子泛函（grand-canonical strictly correlated electrons functional）定义经典非均匀电子气。通过任意晶格周期背景密度（lattice-periodic background density）引入非均匀性，并将这些系统建立为严格的 thermodynamic limit。

Result: 成功为量子与经典非均匀电子气提出了基于泛函的严格定义，建立了这些系统作为热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）的数学框架，并分析了它们的基本性质。

Conclusion: 本文为非均匀电子气提供了基于大正则泛函的严格数学定义，建立了其作为热力学极限的框架，并分析了基本性质，为非均匀系统的理论研究提供了新工具。

Abstract: The non-uniform (or inhomogeneous) electron gas has received much attention in many-body quantum mechanics and quantum chemistry in the early days of density functional theory, mainly as a theoretical device to construct gradient approximations via linear response theory. In this article, motivated by the recent works of Lewin, Lieb and Seiringer, we propose a definition of the quantum (resp. classical) non-uniform electron gas through the use of the grand-canonical Levy-Lieb functional (resp. the grand-canonical strictly correlated electrons functional), establish these systems as rigorous thermodynamic limits and analyze their basic properties. The non-uniformity of the gas comes from an arbitrary lattice-periodic background density.

</details>


### [8] [Limit shapes and harmonic tricks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21255)
*Nikolai Kuchumov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文有两个主要目标：一是对二聚体模型（dimer model）的切平面法（tangent plane method）进行自包含阐述，二是将该方法扩展到多连通域（multiply connected domains），通过计算带孔阿兹特克钻石（Aztec diamond with a hole）的冻结边界（frozen boundary）获得椭圆函数（elliptic functions）参数化的北极曲线（arctic curves）族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在系统阐述二聚体模型中用于分析北极曲线和极限形状（limit shapes）的切平面法，并将其推广到更复杂的多连通几何区域，以解决带孔阿兹特克钻石的冻结边界计算问题。

Method: 采用切平面法分析二聚体模型，通过非平凡计算将方法扩展到多连通域，特别针对带孔阿兹特克钻石的冻结边界进行详细计算。

Result: 获得了以椭圆函数参数化的北极曲线族，该族曲线由高度变化（hole height）索引，这是多连通区域北极曲线的首个显式参数化表示，同时推导并可视化了相应的极限高度函数（limit height functions）。

Conclusion: 本文成功扩展了切平面法至多连通域，为带孔阿兹特克钻石提供了完整的冻结边界解析描述，实现了北极曲线族的椭圆函数参数化，并获得了相应的极限高度函数。

Abstract: This article has two main goals. First, it provides a self-contained exposition of the tangent plane method for the dimer model - a technique for analyzing arctic curves and limit shapes introduced by R. Kenyon and I. Prause (2020). Second, it extends this method to multiply connected domains through a nontrivial computation of the frozen boundary for the Aztec diamond with a hole. This computation yields the first explicit parametrization in terms of elliptic functions of a family of arctic curves of a multiply-connected region indexed by the height change (hole height). We also derive and visualize the corresponding limit height functions.

</details>


### [9] [Homogenization of point interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21400)
*Domenico Cafiero,Michele Correggi,Davide Fermi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了在二维或三维空间中，与大量点状奇异零程势相互作用的非相对论量子粒子的均匀化极限。当奇异势的强度和点间距离同时趋于零而总相互作用强度保持有限时，证明了算子族强预解收敛于具有规则静电势的薛定谔算子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析量子粒子与大量集中点上的奇异零程势（singular zero-range potentials）相互作用的均匀化（homogenization）行为。特别关注当奇异势强度和点间距离同时趋于零而总相互作用强度保持有限时的极限情况。

Method: 采用Γ-收敛（Γ-convergence）方法分析相关二次型的收敛性。假设奇异势具有负散射长度（negative scattering lengths）且均匀分布，通过强预解收敛（strong resolvent convergence）证明算子族的极限行为。

Result: 证明了当N→∞时，算子族强预解收敛于具有规则静电势（regular electrostatic potential）的薛定谔算子。在存在外部囚禁势（external trapping potential）的情况下，收敛提升为一致预解收敛（uniform resolvent sense）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，在均匀化极限下，大量点状奇异零程势的集合可以有效地用规则静电势来描述。这一结果为处理复杂势场系统的量子力学问题提供了数学严格的理论框架。

Abstract: We consider a non-relativistic quantum particle in $\mathbb{R}^d$, $d=2$ or $d = 3$, interacting with singular zero-range potentials concentrated on a large collection of points. We analyze the homogenization regime where the intensities of the singular potentials and the distances between the points simultaneously go to zero as their number grows, while the total interaction strength remains finite. Assuming that the singular potentials have negative scattering lengths and are uniformly distributed, we prove the strong resolvent convergence as $N \to \infty$ of the family of operators to a Schrödinger operator with a regular electrostatic potential. The result is obtained via $Γ$-converge of the associated quadratic forms. Moreover, in presence of an external trapping potential, the convergence is lifted to uniform resolvent sense.

</details>


### [10] [Dimensional analysis with constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21527)
*Umpei Miyamoto*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于约束系统量纲分析的线性代数框架，通过将对数变量中的量纲关系和约束转化为线性结构，提供了独立无量纲量的简单计数和消除冗余量的纯代数方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对变量众多或存在隐式关系的约束系统，直接消元法往往不切实际，需要一种更有效的量纲分析（dimensional analysis）方法。特别是在存在隐式或多重约束的情况下，传统方法面临挑战。

Method: 通过在对数变量中表达量纲关系和约束，将问题简化为线性结构。该公式化方法提供了独立无量纲量的简单计数，更重要的是，提供了一种无需试错的纯代数程序来消除冗余量。

Result: 该方法特别适用于具有隐式或多重约束的系统，能够有效处理传统方法难以应对的复杂情况。文中以经典阻力问题（classical drag force problem）为例进行了说明。

Conclusion: 所提出的线性代数框架为约束系统的量纲分析提供了一种系统化、代数化的解决方案，特别适用于变量众多或存在复杂约束关系的场景，避免了传统试错方法的局限性。

Abstract: We develop a linear-algebraic framework for dimensional analysis in systems with constraints, particularly when variables are numerous or related by implicit relations so that direct elimination is impractical. By expressing both dimensional relations and constraints in logarithmic variables, the problem is reduced to a linear structure. This formulation yields a simple count of independent dimensionless quantities and, more importantly, a purely algebraic procedure to eliminate redundant ones without trial and error. The method is especially effective for systems with implicit or multiple constraints, and is illustrated with the classical drag force problem.

</details>


### [11] [The Spectral Shift Function for Non-Self-Adjoint Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21773)
*Vincent Bruneau,Nicolas Frantz,François Nicoleau*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文致力于定义和分析与非自伴（non-self-adjoint）扰动相关的谱位移函数（spectral shift function），扩展了Lifshits-Kre__n迹公式至非自伴算子，并应用于三维薛定谔算子（Schrödinger operators）的复值短程势（complex-valued short-range potentials）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于散射理论（scattering theory）的应用需求，考虑迹类（trace-class）和相对迹类（relatively trace-class）扰动，旨在分析非自伴扰动下谱位移函数的定义与性质。

Method: 方法包括扩展Lifshits-Kre__n迹公式至非自伴算子，分析谱奇异性（spectral singularities）的作用，并使用泛函演算（functional calculus）推广谱位移函数的定义。

Result: 研究结果将理论应用于三维薛定谔算子与复值短程势，并通过玩具模型（toy models）说明谱位移函数可能携带复特征值（complex eigenvalues）存在的信息。

Conclusion: 结论表明谱位移函数在非自伴扰动理论中具有重要作用，其推广为分析复特征值提供了理论框架，并展示了在具体物理模型中的应用潜力。

Abstract: This paper is devoted to the definition and analysis of the spectral shift function (SSF) associated with non-self-adjoint perturbations of self-adjoint operators. Motivated by applications in scattering theory, we consider both trace-class and relatively trace-class perturbations. We extend the Lifshits-Kre__n trace formula to non-self-adjoint operators under suitable assumptions on the spectrum and the behavior of the resolvent. The role of spectral singularities is carefully analyzed, and we provide a generalization of the SSF using functional calculus. Finally, we apply our results to Schr{ö}dinger operators with complex-valued short-range potentials in dimension three. Toy models illustrate properties that one might hope to extend to general cases. In particular, they suggest that the SSF carries information on the presence of complex eigenvalues.

Method: 采用代数形变理论方法，研究$\mathfrak{sl}_2(\mathbb K)$在$\mathbb K[t]/(t^2)$上的无穷小Hom-Lie形变。通过分析形变括号$[\,\cdot,\cdot]_t = [\,\cdot,\cdot]_0 + t[\,\cdot,\cdot]_1$和形变映射$α_t = \mathrm{id} + tα_1$的结构性质。

Conclusion: 该研究成功证明了Makhlouf和Silvestrov猜想的正确性，即特定条件下的无穷小Hom-Lie形变能够保持雅可比恒等式，为$\mathfrak{sl}_2(\mathbb K)$的形变理论提供了重要的数学保证。

Abstract: We show that whenever \[ [\,\cdot,\cdot]_t = [\,\cdot,\cdot]_0 + t[\,\cdot,\cdot]_1,\qquad α_t = \mathrm{id} + tα_1 \] define an infinitesimal Hom--Lie deformation of $\mathfrak{sl}_2(\mathbb K)$ over $\mathbb K[t]/(t^2)$ and $(\mathfrak{sl}_2(\mathbb K),[\,\cdot,\cdot]_0,α_1)$ is a Hom--Lie algebra, then the deformed bracket $[\,\cdot,\cdot]_t$ satisfies the ordinary Jacobi identity over $\mathbb K[t]$. This solves a conjecture of Makhlouf and Silvestrov from 2010.

### [13] [Model-Independent Reconstruction of Quintessence Potential and Kinetic Energy from DESI DR2 and Pantheon+ Supernovae](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21125)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过模型无关的方法直接重构quintessence标量场的动力学特性，避免对势能函数形式施加理论先验。该方法旨在利用最新宇宙学观测数据约束动态暗能量模型。

Method: 采用非参数化方法，结合DESI DR2重子声学振荡测量和Pantheon+ Ia型超新星数据，使用具有四种不同协方差核的高斯过程进行重构，避免对势能函数形式施加理论先验。

Result: 重构结果显示势能随红移单调递减，与thawing quintessence模型一致；动能在z~1附近过零点，对应暗能量-物质相等时期。中间红移（0.5<z<1.0）出现的表观负动能值在误差范围内，是导数重构中误差放大的统计假象而非新物理现象。

Conclusion: 非参数化方法在约束动态暗能量方面具有强大能力，且对宇宙学先验选择（无论是来自局域SH0ES测量还是早期宇宙Planck测量）的依赖性极小。研究证实了从观测数据直接重构标量场动力学的可行性。

Abstract: We present a model-independent reconstruction of the quintessence scalar field's dynamics-both its potential and kinetic energy-directly from the latest cosmological observations. Our analysis combines DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillation measurements with the Pantheon plus Type Ia supernova compilation, employing Gaussian process with four distinct covariance kernels to avoid theoretical priors on the potential's functional form. Key findings reveal a monotonically decreasing potential with redshift, consistent with thawing quintessence, and a kinetic energy that crosses zero near $z\sim 1$, marking the dark energy-matter equality epoch. Notably, while apparent negative kinetic energy values emerge at intermediate redshifts (0.5<z<1.0), these are statistical artifacts within uncertainties, arising from error amplification in derivative reconstruction rather than new physics. Our results demonstrate the power of non-parametric methods to constrain dynamical dark energy and show minimal dependence on the choice of cosmological priors, whether from local (SH0ES) or early-universe (Planck) measurements.

### [14] [Unimodular Diffusion and Interacting Vacuum Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21675)
*Gopal Kashyap,Naveen K. Singh*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了单模扩散宇宙学（unimodular diffusion cosmology）与相互作用暗区模型（interacting dark sector models）在背景和线性扰动层面的对应关系，发现扩散框架可映射到相互作用暗能量模型，并通过观测数据约束了耦合参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索单模扩散宇宙学框架与相互作用暗区模型之间的对应关系，特别是在背景演化和线性扰动层面的等价性，以理解宇宙学常数的时间依赖性及其对宇宙结构形成的影响。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）在背景层面建立扩散框架与相互作用暗能量模型的映射关系；2）使用两种常见参数化（Q = ξH ρ_de 和 Q = ξH ρ_dm）进行数据分析；3）结合超新星、DESI BAO、宇宙计时器（cosmic chronometers）和CMB距离先验等观测数据；4）在线性扰动层面分析扩散框架与相互作用真空模型的等价性。

Result: 研究结果显示：1）真空耦合情况下ξ = -0.0197 ± 0.0076，物质耦合情况最佳拟合为ξ = 0.0018；2）线性扰动层面扩散框架仅与能量转移均匀的相互作用真空模型（Q ∝ ρ_de，δQ=0）微扰等价；3）加入红移空间畸变数据后，ξ = -0.0147 ± 0.0075，与ΛCDM（ξ=0）在2σ水平一致；4）扩散模型的聚类振幅S_8 = 0.782 ± 0.026，略高于ΛCDM的S_8 = 0.77 ± 0.025。

Conclusion: 结论表明单模扩散宇宙学框架在背景层面可映射到相互作用暗能量模型，但在线性扰动层面仅与特定类型的相互作用真空模型等价。观测数据支持扩散模型与ΛCDM在2σ水平一致，且对结构生长的影响较为有限。

Abstract: We investigate the correspondence between unimodular diffusion cosmology and interacting dark sector models at the background and linear perturbation levels. In the diffusion framework, the effective cosmological constant becomes time dependent, $Λ(t)$, sourced by a diffusion current. We show that at background level this framework can be mapped onto interacting dark energy models with $w=-1$ and energy transfer $Q$. Using two common parameterizations, $Q = ξH ρ_{\rm de}$ and $Q = ξH ρ_{\rm dm}$, and data from supernovae, DESI BAO, cosmic chronometers, and CMB distance priors, we find $ξ= -0.0197 \pm 0.0076$ for the vacuum coupled case, while the matter coupled case gives a best fit $ξ= 0.0018$ with comparable fit. At linear perturbations, the diffusion framework is perturbatively equivalent only to interacting vacuum models with homogeneous energy transfer ($Q \propto ρ_{\rm de}$, $δQ=0$). Including redshift space distortion data, we obtain $ξ= -0.0147 \pm 0.0075$, consistent with $Λ$CDM ($ξ=0$) at $2σ$. The inferred clustering amplitude is $S_8 = 0.782 \pm 0.026$ for the diffusion model, compared to $S_8 = 0.77 \pm 0.025$ for $Λ$CDM under the same dataset, showing a modest impact on structure growth.

### [15] [Modular invariants and NIM-reps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20545)
*Alastair King,Leonard Hardiman*

Main category: math.QA

Method: 作者引入环绕模（encircling module）作为融合代数模，利用关键结构（pivotal structure）进行定义。该方法应用于TM实现（TM realisation），并分析不可分解模范畴（indecomposable module category）的维度条件。

Result: 证明了环绕模与NIM-rep作为融合代数模同构。在TM实现中，模不变量的对角元与NIM-rep重数（multiplicities）得以等同。对于不可分解模范畴，TM的维度条件自动满足模不变性要求。

Abstract: Given a pivotal module category over a spherical fusion category, we introduce the encircling module, a module over the fusion algebra defined using the pivotal structure, and prove that it is isomorphic to the NIM-rep as a fusion algebra module. When applied to the $\mathcal{TM}$ realisation of the modular invariant partition function (arXiv:1911.09024), this yields an identification of the diagonal entries of the modular invariant with the NIM-rep multiplicities, providing a categorical generalisation of Böckenhauer, Evans and Kawahigashi's results (arXiv:math/9907149). We also show that for indecomposable module categories the dimension condition on $\mathcal{TM}$ required for modular invariance is automatically satisfied, and that $\mathcal{TM}$ recovers the full centre construction of Kong and Runkel (arXiv:0807.3356).

### [16] [The survival of the weakest in a biased donation game](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20998)
*Chaoqian Wang,Jingyang Li,Xinwei Wang,Wenqiang Zhu,Attila Szolnoki*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了带有偏见的以牙还牙策略（biased Tit-for-Tat）在捐赠博弈中的演化动态，发现当T策略对无条件合作者的偏见较大而对同类偏见较小时，会出现"隐藏T相"，其中最弱的T策略反而能够主导种群。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以牙还牙策略在利用社会困境中的互惠性方面已被证明有效，但将其视为等同于无条件合作者的程度仍存在争议。本研究旨在探索带有偏见的以牙还牙策略如何通过独立偏见参数调节合作行为。

Method: 引入带有偏见的以牙还牙策略，该策略通过独立的偏见参数对无条件合作者和同类T玩家采取不同的合作行为。在捐赠博弈框架下，研究这个三策略系统在参数平面上的相图演化动态。

Result: 结果显示，即使在强困境条件下，三策略系统也能在参数平面上展现多样化的相图。特别地，当T偏见较小而C偏见较大时，会出现"隐藏T相"，其中最弱的T策略能够主导种群。这种弱势T策略的主导地位源于非传递性生态系统的反直觉机制。

Conclusion: 研究表明偏见调节在合作模式中扮演微妙角色，揭示了在更广泛背景下"最弱者的生存"效应。混合种群分析证实这一现象源于结构化种群，强调了T策略通过抑制其相对于C的相对适应度来消除循环优势簇的机制。

Abstract: Cooperating first then mimicking the partner's act has been proven to be effective in utilizing reciprocity in social dilemmas. However, the extent to which this, called Tit-for-Tat strategy, should be regarded as equivalent to unconditional cooperators remains controversial. Here, we introduce a biased Tit-for-Tat (T) strategy that cooperates differently toward unconditional cooperators (C) and fellow T players through independent bias parameters. The results show that, even under strong dilemmas in the donation game framework, this three-strategy system can exhibit diverse phase diagrams on the parameter plane. In particular, when T-bias is small and C-bias is large, a ``hidden T phase'' emerges, in which the weakest T strategy dominates. The dominance of the weakened T strategy originates from a counterintuitive mechanism characterizing non-transitive ecological systems: T suppresses its relative fitness to C, rapidly eliminates the cyclic dominance clusters, and subsequently expands slowly to take over the entire population. Analysis in well-mixed populations confirms that this phenomenon arises from structured populations. Our study thus reveals the subtle role of bias regulation in cooperative modes by emphasizing the ``survival of the weakest'' effect in a broader context.

</details>

### [17] [Error Analysis of the Explicit Splitting Scheme for Fluid-Poroelastic Structure Interaction Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21088)
*Yifan Wang,Jeonghun Lee,Suncica Canic*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对时变Stokes-Biot问题的全离散、可并行、显式松耦合格式的先验误差分析。该方法以完全显式方式解耦流体和孔隙弹性子问题，通过离散能量框架证明了格式的一阶时间精度和最优空间收敛率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在开发一种可并行、显式松耦合的数值格式来解决时变Stokes-Biot问题。主要动机在于实现流体和孔隙弹性子问题的完全解耦，使每个子问题能在每个时间步独立求解，同时保持界面条件的一致处理以确保格式的稳定性和收敛性。

Method: 方法采用全离散、可并行、显式松耦合格式（fully discrete, parallelizable, explicit loosely coupled scheme）。在离散能量框架下进行误差分析，引入各子域的Ritz型投影（Ritz-type projections），并从时间离散连续格式中减去全离散格式。通过显式分裂（explicit splitting）处理界面数据滞后问题，使用Gronwall型论证（Gronwall-type argument）建立无条件误差估计。

Result: 主要结果是推导了离散误差能量恒等式（discrete error energy identity），并在组合能量-耗散范数（combined energy-dissipation norm）中建立了无条件误差估计。分析证明格式具有一阶时间精度（first-order accuracy in time）和由有限元多项式次数决定的最优空间收敛率（optimal spatial convergence rates）。数值实验基于构造解（manufactured solution）验证了理论结果。

Conclusion: 本文成功建立了时变Stokes-Biot问题显式松耦合格式的严格误差分析框架。数值实验证实了所有变量的一阶时间收敛性，以及与所选近似空间一致的空间收敛阶。该方法实现了流体和孔隙弹性子问题的完全解耦，同时保持了格式的稳定性和收敛性。

Abstract: We present a priori error analysis for a fully discrete, parallelizable, explicit loosely coupled scheme for the time-dependent Stokes-Biot problem. The method decouples the fluid and poroelastic subproblems in a fully explicit fashion, allowing each problem to be solved independently at each time step, with a consistent treatment of the interface conditions that provides stability and convergence of the scheme. The error analysis is carried out in a discrete energy framework. More specifically, we introduce Ritz-type projections in each subdomain, and subtract the fully discrete scheme from the time-discrete continuous formulation. This yields reduced error equations in which the dominant interpolation contributions cancel. The remaining consistency terms stem primarily from time discretization residuals and lagged interface data inherent to the explicit splitting. The main result of this manuscript is the derivation of a discrete error energy identity, and establishment of unconditional error estimates in a combined energy-dissipation norm via a Gronwall-type argument. These estimates demonstrate first-order accuracy in time and optimal spatial convergence rates, as determined by the degree of the finite element polynomials. Numerical experiments based on a manufactured solution corroborate the theory, confirming first-order temporal convergence for all variables, and spatial convergence orders consistent with the chosen approximation spaces.

</details>


### [18] [On Sampling Methods for Inverse Biharmonic Scattering Problems in Supported Plates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21477)
*Carlos Borges,Rafael Ceja Ayala,Peter Nekrasov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括推导支撑板边界条件的互易原理（reciprocity principle）和远场算子（far-field operator）分解，并分析其范围特性以验证线性采样法（LSM）和直接采样法（DSM）。通过数值实验评估两种方法在不同条件下的性能。

Result: 结果表明，两种方法都能稳健地恢复障碍物的位置和凸包（convex hull），其中直接采样法（DSM）表现出更好的稳定性和更低的计算成本。数值实验考虑了噪声、有限数据量、多重散射（multiple scattering）和泊松比（Poisson's ratio）变化等实际因素。

Conclusion: 研究证实了线性采样法（LSM）和直接采样法（DSM）在薄弹性板支撑空腔逆问题中的有效性，特别强调了DSM在稳定性和计算效率方面的优势。该方法为基于远场测量的无损检测提供了理论依据和实用工具。

Abstract: We study the inverse problem of qualitatively recovering a supported cavity in a thin elastic plate governed by the flexural (biharmonic) wave equation, using far-field pattern measurements. We derive a reciprocity principle and a factorization of the far-field operator for the supported plate boundary conditions, and we analyze its range properties to justify both the linear sampling method (LSM) and the direct sampling method (DSM). Numerical experiments assess the performance of LSM and DSM under noise, a limited amount of data, multiple scattering, and variations in the Poisson's ratio. The results show that both methods robustly recover the obstacle's location and convex hull, with DSM offering improved stability and reduced computational cost.

### [19] [Competing skin effect and quasiperiodic localization in the non-Hermitian Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chain: Reentrant delocalization, spectral topology destruction, and entanglement suppression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20330)
*Souvik Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了一维非互易SSH链中非厄米趋肤效应与AAH准周期无序的相互作用，揭示了包含五种不同相态的完整相图，其中首次报道了具有重入部分退局域化的竞争相态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect）与Aubry-André-Harper（AAH）准周期无序在一维Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）链中的相互作用，特别是非互易跃迁（nonreciprocal hopping）对系统相行为的影响。

Method: 采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）、转移矩阵分析（transfer-matrix analysis）和解析相似变换论证（analytical similarity-transformation argument）相结合的方法，系统研究了系统的相图。

Result: 研究识别出五种不同的相态：拓扑扩展相、AAH局域相、趋肤局域相、完全局域相，以及首次报道的竞争相态（competition regime），该相态表现出重入部分退局域化（reentrant partial delocalization）。研究还推导了修正的局域化边界解析表达式，并揭示了准周期无序对复谱环和点隙拓扑的破坏作用。

Conclusion: 准周期无序可以破坏非厄米趋肤效应的定向累积，产生复杂的相竞争现象；SSH的子晶格结构对产生五相景观至关重要；趋肤效应显著抑制纠缠熵，而足够强的AAH无序可以部分恢复它。

Abstract: We investigate the interplay between the non-Hermitian skin effect and Aubry-André-Harper (AAH) quasiperiodic disorder in a one-dimensional Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) chain with nonreciprocal hopping. By exact diagonalization, transfer-matrix analysis, and an analytical similarity-transformation argument, we map the full ( , $δ$) phase diagram, where A is the AAH modulation strength and the nonreciprocity parameter. We identify five distinct regimes: ( ) topological with extended bulk, (II) AAH-localized, (III) skin-localized, (IV) fully localized, and a previously unreported (V) competition regime exhibiting reentrant partial delocalization, in which intermediate quasiperiodic disorder disrupts the directional skin accumulation before ultimately Anderson-localizing all states. Using phase-averaged diagnostics and finite-size scaling, we confirm that the reentrant regime is robust, characterized by a non-monotonic inverse participation ratio that sharpens with increasing system size. We derive an analytical expression for the modified localization boundary $λ_{c}(δ)=2\sqrt{v_{eff}w}$ with $v_{vff}=\sqrt{v^{2}-δ^{2}}$, which agrees with numerical Lyapunov exponent calculations. We further show that quasiperiodic disorder progressively unwinds the complex spectral loops, destroying the point-gap topology at a critical strength distinct from the band-topological transition ; that the skin effect suppresses entanglement entropy to near-zero values while sufficiently strong AAH disorder partially restores it ; and that the SSH sublattice structure absent in the widely studied non-Hermitian AAH chain is essential for producing the five-phase landscape, as demonstrated by direct comparison with the non-dimerized limit.

### [20] [Non-Hermitian Disordered Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20393)
*Kohei Kawabata,Shinsei Ryu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文综述了非厄米无序系统（non-Hermitian disordered systems）的物理与数学理论，重点探讨了非厄米随机矩阵理论（non-Hermitian random matrix theory）及其在开放量子系统、相变临界性等领域的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米无序系统已成为现代物理学的核心领域，其影响范围涵盖凝聚态物理、量子物理、统计物理和高能物理等多个领域。这些原理也适用于网络科学、复杂系统和生物物理学等跨学科领域，其中耗散（dissipation）、非互易性（nonreciprocity）和随机性（stochasticity）普遍存在。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，首先介绍非厄米系统的38重对称性分类（38-fold symmetry classification），并与厄米系统的10重分类（10-fold way）进行对比。随后引入经典的Ginibre非厄米随机矩阵系综（Ginibre ensembles），并综述复杂谱统计（complex-spectral statistics）的各种诊断方法及对称性实现的不同普适类（universality classes）。

Result: 非厄米随机矩阵理论可用于表征开放量子系统中的混沌（chaos）与可积性（integrability）。此外，无序与非厄米性的相互作用导致临界性（criticality），包括Hatano-Nelson模型及其高维扩展中的安德森转变（Anderson transitions）。

Conclusion: 本文还讨论了基于非线性σ模型（nonlinear sigma models）的非厄米无序系统的有效场论描述，系统总结了该领域的关键理论框架和应用前景。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian disordered systems have emerged as a central arena in modern physics, with ramifications spanning condensed matter, quantum, statistical, and high energy contexts. The same principles also underlie phenomena beyond physics, such as network science, complex systems, and biophysics, where dissipation, nonreciprocity, and stochasticity are ubiquitous. Here, we review the physics and mathematics of non-Hermitian disordered systems, with particular emphasis on non-Hermitian random matrix theory. We begin by presenting the 38-fold symmetry classification of non-Hermitian systems, contrasting it with the 10-fold way for Hermitian systems. After introducing the classic Ginibre ensembles of non-Hermitian random matrices, we survey various diagnostics for complex-spectral statistics and distinct universality classes realized by symmetry. As a key application to physics, we discuss how non-Hermitian random matrix theory characterizes chaos and integrability in open quantum systems. We then turn to the criticality due to the interplay of disorder and non-Hermiticity, including Anderson transitions in the Hatano-Nelson model and its higher-dimensional extensions. We also discuss the effective field theory description of non-Hermitian disordered systems in terms of nonlinear sigma models.

Abstract: We propose encapsulating type-A antiferromagnetic semiconductors between graphene layers to realize a gate-tunable synthetic antiferromagnet with nonrelativistic spin splitting, enabling efficient spintronic transport via graphene. Ab initio calculations and tight-binding models of graphene/MnS/graphene heterostructure reveal that gate-tuning of the heterostructure breaks top/bottom graphene equivalence, inducing opposite ferromagnetic proximity exchange that lifts spin degeneracy to yield nonrelativistic spin splitting at the Fermi level, dominating over relativistic effects. The induced effects manifest as conductance dips in spin-resolved transport through proximitized graphene nanoribbons, observable as giant magnetoresistance within a narrow energy window around the Fermi level. Our graphene/type-A antiferromagnetic heterostructure, a readily synthesizable platform incorporating antiferromagnets with nonrelativistic spin splitting, pave the way for gate-manipulated, low-dimensional antiferromagnetic devices.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法如玻尔兹曼输运方程（Boltzmann Transport Equation, BTE）计算成本高昂，而随着AI基础设施碳足迹压力增加，需要开发更高效的计算工具。本研究旨在为下一代热器件的参数探索和设计提供高效解决方案。

Method: 采用元胞自动机（cellular automaton, CA）理论模型，该模型具有几何鲁棒性，能够无缝整合替代杂质（substitutional impurities）、空位（vacancies）和不规则边缘（irregular edges）。模型验证使用了石墨烯纳米带（graphene nanoribbons, AGNRs）。

Result: 模型成功复现了热导率（thermal conductivity）对纳米带宽度和温度的依赖关系，捕捉到了关键散射（critical scattering）和限制效应（confinement effects）。计算复杂度为线性可扩展性O(N)，相比传统方法显著提高了效率。

Conclusion: 该元胞自动机模型作为一种高效工具，适用于参数化探索和设计下一代热器件，特别在计算资源优化和减少AI基础设施碳足迹方面具有重要价值。

Abstract: In this work, we formulate a theoretical model based on a cellular automaton (CA) to study thermal transport in low-dimensional nanostructures across ballistic, diffusive, and transition regimes. Unlike computationally intensive methods such as the Boltzmann Transport Equation (BTE), our model stands out for its geometrical robustness, allowing the seamless integration of substitutional impurities, vacancies, and irregular edges. We validated the model using graphene nanoribbons (AGNRs), successfully replicating the dependence of thermal conductivity on ribbon width and temperature. Results demonstrate that the model captures critical scattering and confinement effects with a linear scalability O(N). Given the increasing pressure to optimize computational resources and reduce the carbon footprint associated with AI infrastructure, this CA model emerges as a highly efficient tool for the parametric exploration and design of next-generation thermal devices.

### [23] [Super-Klein tunneling in 2D Lorentzian-type barriers in graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20950)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法采用超对称量子力学（supersymmetric quantum mechanics）方法，为模型提供了优雅且解析可处理的框架。该方法建立了模型与自由粒子动力学之间的内在联系，使得超克莱因隧穿现象能够自然涌现。

Result: 研究结果表明，超克莱因隧穿（super-Klein tunneling）是该模型与自由粒子动力学内在联系的直接结果。此外，揭示了模型的尺度不变性（scale invariance）以及势能对特定能量粒子的不可见性（invisibility of the potential for particles of specific energy）。

Conclusion: 该研究通过超对称量子力学框架，为理解石墨烯中狄拉克费米子的超克莱因隧穿现象提供了理论基础。研究还讨论了实验实现的可能途径，为未来实验验证提供了方向。

Abstract: We introduce a two-dimensional model of spin-1/2 Dirac fermions in graphene subjected to a highly tunable electric field, which exhibits super-Klein tunneling. The electric field can be continuously interpolated between two limiting configurations: a uniform electrostatic Lorentzian barrier with translational invariance and a chain of well-separated electrostatic scatterers. We demonstrate that super-Klein tunneling arises naturally as a direct consequence of the intrinsic connection of the model to free-particle dynamics, a relation that is established through methods of supersymmetric quantum mechanics, which provide an elegant and analytically tractable framework. Besides the mentioned super-Klein tunneling, scale invariance of the model and invisibility of the potential for particles of specific energy are revealed, and possible routes toward experimental realization are discussed.

### [24] [Twist-Induced Quantum Geometry Reconfiguration in Moiré Flat Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20849)
*Yi-Chun Hung,Xiaoting Zhou,Arun Bansil*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）分析扭曲双层环流有序（loop-current-ordered）Kagome晶格（tb-LCK），发现扭曲能抑制单层贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的继承，揭示该体系可作为探索非常规量子几何（quantum geometry）的平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在扭曲双层石墨烯和过渡金属二硫化物等常见莫尔（moiré）体系中，莫尔平带（moiré flat bands）的量子几何通常继承自单层。然而，在具有复杂单层能带结构和对称性破缺的体系中，这种对应关系是否持续存在尚不明确。

Method: 研究采用紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）分析扭曲双层环流有序Kagome晶格（tb-LCK）体系。通过调节环流有序（loop-current order）的相位，探究扭曲驱动的能带重构（band reconstruction）效应。

Result: 研究发现扭曲诱导了量子几何的重新配置（reconfiguration），抑制了单层贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的继承。这些效应源于钒基Kagome材料固有的异常大层间隧穿（interlayer tunneling）所实现的强层间杂化（interlayer hybridizations），混合了能量上相距较远的态并重塑了量子几何。

Conclusion: 扭曲在tb-LCK中抑制了从单层继承的量子几何，确立了环流有序莫尔体系作为探索莫尔平带中非常规量子几何的有前景平台。研究还通过钒基Kagome材料讨论了所提出体系的实验可行性。

Abstract: The interplay between band topology, Berry curvature, and moiré flat bands lies at the heart of recent advances in quantum materials. In well-studied moiré systems such as twisted bilayer graphene and transition metal dichalcogenides, the quantum geometry of moiré flat bands typically reflects that of the monolayer, with Berry curvature originating from the band edge at the same valley. Whether this correspondence persists in systems with complex monolayer band structures and broken symmetries remains unclear. Here, we study twisted bilayers of loop-current-ordered kagome lattices (tb-LCK), which have been proposed in the context of vanadium-based kagome materials, using tight-binding models, and uncover a twist-induced reconfiguration of quantum geometry. By tuning the phase of the loop-current order, we identify the suppression of monolayer Berry curvature through twist-driven band reconstruction. We attribute these effects to strong interlayer hybridizations, enabled by the unusually large interlayer tunneling inherent to vanadium-based kagome materials, which mix energetically distant states and reshape quantum geometry. These results reveal that twist in tb-LCK suppresses quantum geometric inheritance from the monolayer, and establish loop-current-ordered moiré systems as promising platforms for exploring unconventional quantum geometry in moiré flat bands. We further comment on the experimental feasibility of the proposed system via vanadium-based kagome materials.

### [25] [Quantum Geometry of Moiré Flat Bands Beyond the Valley Paradigm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20852)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattices）中的平带为相关和拓扑相提供了丰富平台，但基于谷（valley）的范式在缺乏谷结构的材料中失效。需要建立超越谷范式的机制来解释平带量子几何的产生。

Method: 开发并分析了扭曲双层二分格子的紧束缚模型（tight-binding models），重点关注层间杂化（interlayer hybridization）在产生平带量子几何中的作用。特别研究了扭曲骰子晶格（twisted dice lattice）和石墨烯异质双层中的亚晶格选择性层间隧穿。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了超越谷范式的机制，可在莫尔平带中诱导量子几何。结果为扭曲双层二分格子的平带量子几何工程指明了方向，在氧化物异质结构、分子晶格和合成量子物质中具有潜在的材料实现前景。

Abstract: Flat bands in moiré superlattices provide a fertile ground for correlated and topological phases, governed by their quantum geometric properties. In this work, we develop and analyze tight-binding models for twisted heterobilayers of bipartite lattices, with a focus on the role of interlayer hybridization in generating flat-band quantum geometry. We demonstrate that sublattice-selective interlayer tunnelings in twisted dice lattice and graphene heterobilayers induce isolated flat bands at zero energy, whose number is tunable by the twist angle. Most importantly, these flat bands exhibit finite Berry curvature and a quantum metric of the Chern-insulator scale, generated through interlayer hybridization. This establishes a mechanism to induce quantum geometry in moiré flat bands beyond the valley paradigm. Our results chart a route to flat-band quantum geometry engineering in twisted bilayer bipartite lattices, with potential material realizations in oxide heterostructures, molecular lattices, and synthetic quantum matter.

### [26] [Chern Insulator in magnetic-doped two-dimensional semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20875)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索在过渡金属二硫化物中通过掺杂实现非平凡拓扑性质的新途径，为量子反常霍尔效应（quantum anomalous Hall effect）研究提供有前景的平台。

Method: 该方法利用掺杂态在价带边缘附近与宿主能带发生杂化（hybridized），诱导能带反转（band inversion），从而产生拓扑非平凡性质。研究通过V掺杂的WSe2和WS2体系的计算验证了这一机制。

Result: 计算证实了V掺杂WSe2和WS2中能带反转机制的有效性，成功诱导出具有非零陈数的非平凡能带。这些体系同时表现出磁序（magnetic order）和非平凡拓扑性质。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的掺杂诱导机制为在过渡金属二硫化物中实现拓扑非平凡性质提供了有效途径。磁序与拓扑性质的共存使这些体系成为探索量子反常霍尔效应的理想平台。

Abstract: We propose an approach to induce nontrivial bands with non-zero Chern numbers by utilizing strong spin-orbit coupling in transition metal dichalcogenides with dopants. We demonstrate that a doped state near the valence-band edge induces band inversion with the hybridized host band, leading to topologically non-trivial properties. Calculations for V-doped WSe2 and WS2 confirm this mechanism. The coexistence of magnetic order and nontrivial topology in these systems offers a promising platform for exploring the quantum anomalous Hall effect.

Result: 研究发现在广泛的偏心率和扭转范围内，系统表现出双稳态磁行为（bistable magnetic behavior），磁化反转过程中出现涡旋-畴壁传播（vortex-domain-wall propagation）。识别出四种退化的混合剩磁态（mixed remanent state）构型，其矫顽场在长轴比短轴大约30%的结构中随偏心率增加而增大，但对扭转变化不敏感。

Abstract: We investigate the equilibrium magnetization in ferromagnetic nanoscrews (NSw) using micromagnetic simulations. These systems consist of elongated three-dimensional magnetic membranes with helicoidal geometry, combining curvature, torsion ($\mathrm{w}$), and eccentricity ($ε$) along their length. We focus on the influence of these geometric parameters, together with membrane thickness and inner diameter, on remanent states and coercive fields. Our results, obtained over a broad range of eccentricities and torsions, reveal bistable magnetic behavior, with vortex-domain-wall propagation during magnetization reversal. We identify four degenerate configurations of a remarkably stable mixed remanent state. The coercive field is found to increase with eccentricity for structures with a major axis (larger inner diameter) approximately 30\% larger than the minor axis (smaller inner diameter), while remaining largely insensitive to variations in torsion. These findings are interpreted in terms of geometry-induced modifications of surface magnetostatic charges on the membrane mantle. Overall, our results demonstrate that nanoscrews exhibit robust bistability under systematic geometric deformation, together with enhanced coercivity, highlighting their potential for applications in three-dimensional nanomagnetism.

Abstract: Quantum geometry governs a wide range of transport and optical phenomena in quantum materials. Recent works have explored analogue electromagnetism and gravity in terms of the quantum geometric tensor, whose real and imaginary parts correspond to the quantum metric and the Berry curvature. By treating real- and momentum-space geometries on an equal footing, we develop a comprehensive and general formalism based on an expansion in $\hbar$, equivalent to an expansion in spatial derivatives. We derive the quantum-metric corrections to the wave-packet energy, the Berry connection, and the phase-space density of states, similar to the field-induced corrections in nonlinear response. A kinetic equation that captures quantum-metric effects across the full phase space then follows naturally. Our framework provides a foundation for investigating thermodynamic and transport properties in systems where real- and momentum-space quantum geometries coexist.

### [29] [Joule heating and electronic Gurzhi effect in hydrodynamic differential transport in an electron liquid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21346)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用微分电阻（differential resistance）测量方法，在零磁场（B=0）条件下，通过U形（U-turn）交流电流回路驱动非线性输运，并进行交流加直流（ac + dc）测量，分析外部直流电流偏置（j_dc）对电子温度（T_e）的影响。

Result: 观察到由j_dc诱导的电子输运谷（electronic transport valley），该现象归因于焦耳热（Joule heating）效应对电子液体（electron liquid）电子温度（T_e）的影响；定量分析表明黏度电阻率（Δρ）与T^{-2}成正比，且与不同测量配置下的直流电流诱导电子Gurzhi效应（electronic Gurzhi effect）一致。

Conclusion: 直流电流偏置（j_dc）通过焦耳热（Joule heating）机制改变电子温度（T_e），从而在电子液体（electron liquid）的流体动力学（hydrodynamic）区域产生可观测的电子输运谷（electronic transport valley），且黏度电阻率（viscosity resistivity）的温度依赖性符合理论预期，验证了电子Gurzhi效应（electronic Gurzhi effect）的存在。

Abstract: We perform a differential resistance study in the hydrodynamic regime of electron liquid in GaAs/AlGaAs quantum wells. At zero magnetic field ($B$) a Lorentzian profile occurs in the nonlinear transport driven by a U-turn (ac) current loop, in (ac + dc) measurements a minimum deepens with the external dc current bias ($j_{dc}$). Our analysis shows that the observed electronic transport valley induced by $j_{dc}$ is attributed to Joule heating effect on the electron temperature ($T_{e}$) of electron liquid. Quantitatively, we demonstrate that the viscosity resistivity ($Δρ$) is proportional to $T^{-2}$ and is consistent with the dc-current induced electronic Gurzhi effect in various configurations of measurement.

### [30] [Observation of microscopic domain effects in the metal-insulator transition of thin-film NdNiO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21405)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用频率域热反射（frequency-domain thermoreflectance, FDTR）测量外延NdNiO₃薄膜的面外热导率变化；同时使用频率域光反射（frequency-domain photoreflectance, FDPR）表征光激发载流子的双极扩散率（ambipolar diffusivity）。这些方法能够有效避免基底对测量的主导影响。

Result: FDTR测量显示NdNiO₃薄膜在金属-绝缘体相变（metal-insulator transition）中面外热导率发生急剧变化；FDPR则揭示了光激发载流子双极扩散率的显著改变。虽然面内电阻表现出明显的滞后现象，但面外热输运和电荷输运的滞后效应可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 面内与面外输运性质的差异归因于纳米尺度畴（nanoscale domains）在相变过程中渗透的各向异性，特别是当薄膜厚度接近畴长度尺度时。FDTR和FDPR被确立为量子材料相变的灵敏探针，NdNiO₃在热控制和存储器应用方面展现出潜力。

Abstract: Perovskite oxides display correlated electrical, magnetic, and thermal properties that can be further tuned in the thin-film limit, making them contenders for next-generation electronics. Measuring thermal transport in thin films is challenging, because traditional techniques are dominated by the substrate. Here, frequency-domain thermoreflectance (FDTR) of an epitaxial NdNiO$_3$ thin film reveals a sharp change in out-of-plane thermal conductivity across the metal-insulator transition. Complementary frequency-domain photoreflectance (FDPR) reveals a large change in ambipolar diffusivity of photoexcited carriers. While the in-plane electrical resistance shows large hysteresis, out-of-plane thermal and charge transport shows negligible hysteresis. We attribute this discrepancy to anisotropy in the percolation of nanoscale domains across the transition as the film thickness approaches the domain length scale. We establish FDTR and FDPR as sensitive probes of quantum material phase transitions and highlight NdNiO$_3$ for thermal control and memory applications.

Abstract: Band structure engineering in surface acoustic wave (SAW) metamaterials could advance both classical telecommunications and quantum information processing. Existing methods capture only fragments of the dispersion at discrete frequencies, preventing systematic characterization and control of SAW-based metamaterials. Here, we develop electrostatic force microscopy (EFM) to enable real-space imaging of traveling SAWs in honeycomb metamaterials on LiNbO$_3$. Our application leverages sub-200 nm spatial resolution, broad GHz bandwidth, and non-contact imaging to map complex band structures with continuous frequency resolution and expanded frequency range, while preserving sub-lattice detail. Method: 研究通过实验展示了在低温（cryogenic temperatures）和外加磁场条件下，独立铂纳米薄膜的太赫兹辐射。通过对比Pt与W或Ta的相位反转验证了能斯特系数（Nernst coefficient）的符号对发射极性的决定性作用，并利用厚度缩放和合金化抑制热导率来增强发射强度。

Result: 独立Pt纳米薄膜在低温下表现出高效的太赫兹辐射，其发射极性由能斯特系数的符号直接决定。通过厚度缩放和合金化抑制热导率，单层发射强度可提升至与基准自旋电子双层结构相当的水平。

Conclusion: 这些发现将重金属在太赫兹发射中的既定角色从被动的自旋汇（spin-sinks）重新定义为主动发射器，揭示了一种适用于多种自旋电子和量子材料的普适发射范式（universal emission paradigm）。

Abstract: State-of-the-art metallic terahertz (THz) emitters rely predominantly on spintronic heterostructures, where heavy metals serve as passive spin-to-charge converters. Here, we demonstrate efficient THz radiation from standalone Pt nanofilms at cryogenic temperatures and under external magnetic fields. The governing mechanism is identified as the ultrafast photo-Nernst effect, wherein a transient thermal gradient drives a transverse charge current. The THz emission polarity is directly dictated by the sign of the Nernst coefficient, as verified by the phase reversal observed between Pt and W or Ta. Remarkably, both thickness scaling and alloying-induced suppression of thermal conductivity independently amplify the single-layer emission to levels comparable with benchmark spintronic bilayers. These findings redefine the established role of heavy metals from passive spin-sinks to active THz emitters, uncovering a universal emission paradigm applicable across diverse spintronic and quantum materials.

</details>


### [35] [Floquet generation of hybrid-order topology and $\mathbb{Z}_2$-like bipolar localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21954)
*Koustav Roy,Latu Kalita,B. Tanatar,Saurabh Basu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过周期驱动和非互易耦合工程化BBH模型，实现了高阶拓扑相与一阶拓扑相的共存，并揭示了驱动诱导的非厄米趋肤效应转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索如何通过动态调控（周期驱动和非互易耦合）来激发和控制静态系统中被掩盖的厄米与非厄米拓扑特性，特别是实现高阶拓扑与一阶拓扑的共存。

Method: 采用两步工程化方法：首先对Benalcazar-Bernevig-Hughes（BBH）模型施加周期驱动，随后引入非互易耦合。利用广义布里渊区（generalized Brillouin zone, GBZ）理论分析非厄米趋肤效应，并通过镜像对称性构建一维映射。

Result: 周期驱动激活了一阶拓扑，产生了在零和π准能处同时具有一阶导电边缘和高阶角态的Floquet相，即混合阶拓扑相。非互易耦合诱导了类Z2趋肤效应，并展现出从单极到双极局域相的驱动诱导转变。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了一种高效动态生成和控制厄米与非厄米拓扑特征的技术，这些特征在静态场景中通常被掩盖，为拓扑相调控提供了新途径。

Abstract: Higher order topology, in the form of the emergence of corner modes, is observed in two dimensions when crystalline symmetries are superposed on the Altland-Zirnbauer classification of topological insulators. It occurs in Benalcazar-Bernevig-Hughes (BBH) model on a 2D square lattice, which owing to an embedded $\mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge field, features a bulk quadrupole moment with localized zero-energy corner states. Further, as a dividend, the BBH model transmutes the general notion of the space-time inversion ($\mathcal{PT}$) symmetry and behaves as a spinful system, without having to invoke `real' spin degrees of freedom. A two-fold engineering of the model, namely a periodic drive, followed by a non-reciprocal hopping render intriguing consequences. As a first, the drive activates first-order topology, and the resulting Floquet phase hosts a coexistence of first-order conducting edges at both zero and $π$ quasienergies along with higher order corner states, which qualifies the coexisting state to be denoted as a hybrid-order topological phase. Further, inclusion of non-reciprocal couplings features a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-like skin effect which demonstrates a drive-induced transition from a unipolar to a bipolar localized phase, and is evidenced via the generalized Brillouin zone (GBZ) theory. While depiction of a GBZ in 2D is challenging, a corresponding 1D map is still possible and can be implemented by exploiting the mirror symmetry. We further uncover conditions under which the skin effect is completely suppressed in our system. Putting together, our results manifest an efficient technique to dynamically engender and control Hermitian and non-Hermitian topological features, that remain otherwise masked in a static scenario.

### [36] [Engineering chiral-induced spin selectivity in an artificial topological quantum well](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21964)

TL;DR: 该研究在InAs/GaSb量子阱系统中实现了手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）效应的固态平台，通过可控引入手性结构和退相干电极，展示了自旋极化的可调控性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）是一种电子通过手性介质后产生自旋极化的显著现象。理论研究表明自旋轨道耦合、几何手性和退相干协同作用产生该效应，研究旨在固态系统中实现可控的CISS效应。

Method: 研究采用工程化的InAs/GaSb量子阱系统，其中几何手性和退相干可以受控引入。通过设计手性结构并系统改变退相干电极数量，同时对比非手性配置，验证CISS效应的产生机制。

Result: 引入手性结构产生明显的自旋极化，其符号随手性翻转而反转，幅度随退相干电极数量增加而系统增长。非手性配置无自旋选择性，且极化在强安德森无序下保持稳健，表明工程手性结构提供内在稳定的自旋选择性输运途径。

Conclusion: 该研究在拓扑量子阱系统中建立了可控生成CISS效应的固态平台，证实了工程手性结构在固态系统中实现稳健自旋选择性输运的可行性。

Abstract: Chiral-induced spin selectivity (CISS) is a striking phenomenon in which spin-unpolarized electrons become spin-polarized after traversing a chiral medium. Theoretical studies have shown that spin-orbit coupling, geometric chirality, and dephasing act cooperatively for this effect to emerge. Inspired by this, we demonstrate a solid-state realization of CISS in an engineered InAs/GaSb quantum well where geometric chirality and dephasing can be introduced controllably. Introducing a chiral structure produces a clear spin polarization whose sign reverses when the chirality is flipped, and whose magnitude grows systematically with the number of dephasing electrodes, while achiral configurations exhibit no spin selectivity. The polarization remains robust even under strong Anderson disorder, showing that the engineered chiral structures provides an intrinsically stable route to spin-selective transport. These results establish a solid-state platform in the topological quantum well system for controllably generating the CISS effect.

### [37] [Electrically controllable valence-conduction band reversals in helical trilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21973)
*Matan Bocarsly,Indranil Roy,Weifeng Zhi,Li-Qiao Xia,Aviram Uri,Yves H. Kwan,Aaron Sharpe,Matan Uzan,Yuri Myasoedov,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Trithep Devakul,Pablo Jarillo-Herrero,Eli Zeldov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用扫描纳米SQUID磁强计（scanning nano-SQUID magnetometry）检测磁性特征，并结合自洽哈特里-福克（self-consistent Hartree-Fock）计算分析八个低能平带的相互作用重组效应。

Result: 实验观测到一系列尖锐的磁性特征，与"跷跷板"式转变（seesaw-like transitions）一致，其中占据和非占据的价带与导带随掺杂反复交换，并伴随新型磁滞现象。理论计算显示相互作用重组了所有八个低能平带，导致轨道磁化发生突变。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了螺旋三层石墨烯为第一个通过电子相互作用实现掺杂控制访问所有三种内部自由度（自旋、谷和子晶格）的系统，引入了一类新的关联相变。

Abstract: In moiré graphene systems, electronic interactions lift spin and valley degeneracies, leading to symmetry-broken ground states. In helical trilayer graphene (HTG), we uncover a distinct interaction-driven mechanism in which the roles of sublattice-polarized valence and conduction bands are cyclically reversed. Using scanning nano-SQUID magnetometry, we detect a series of sharp magnetic signatures consistent with seesaw-like transitions, where occupied and unoccupied valence and conduction bands interchange repeatedly with doping, accompanied by a novel form of magnetic hysteresis. These transitions occur entirely within metallic regimes and leave only weak fingerprints in transport measurements. Self-consistent Hartree-Fock calculations reveal that interactions reorganize all eight low-energy flat bands, driving abrupt changes in orbital magnetization. Our results establish HTG as the first system where electronic interactions provide doping-controlled access to all three internal degrees of freedom - spin, valley, and sublattice - introducing a new class of correlated phase transitions.

Result: 研究发现弹性不仅存在于物质空间，也存在于自旋空间，这一发现揭示了弹性在物理领域中的普适性，为维持结构完整性提供了新的理论基础。

Conclusion: 该工作通过建立缺失的自旋对应物，完善了弹性理论的完整图景，并指向一个更广泛的范式，即弹性超越了其传统边界。

Abstract: Elasticity has long been regarded as a property exclusive to material media. Here we uncover its hidden existence in the spin degree of freedom. We introduce spin elasticity-an intrinsic mechanism that governs recoverable deformation of spin morphology. This discovery reveals a previously unrecognized universality: elasticity operates in both matter and spin spaces, underpinning structural integrity across physical realms. By establishing the missing spin counterpart, this work completes the elastic picture and points toward a broader paradigm where elasticity transcends its conventional boundaries.

Method: 采用实验方法研究纳米厚度钇铁石榴石（YIG）薄膜中短脉冲前向体自旋波（forward volume spin waves）的非线性传播特性，通过控制微波功率达到孤子形成阈值。

Conclusion: 该研究为微观自旋波电路中的高速信息传输提供了一种有前景的途径，能够有效避免有害色散效应的影响，实现脉冲的无失真传输。

Abstract: We study experimentally the nonlinear propagation of short pulses of forward volume spin waves in nanometer-thick YIG films. We show that nonlinearity of the spin system can efficiently counteract dispersion broadening of the pulses, leading to the formation of envelope solitons. We demonstrate that in microscopic YIG systems, microwave powers of the order of one milliwatt are sufficient to reach the soliton formation threshold. At powers slightly above this threshold, we achieve transmission of 3-ns spin-wave pulses over distances of up to 50 micrometers without increase in their temporal width. Our results demonstrate a promising way towards high-rate transmission of information in microscopic spin-wave circuits unaffected by detrimental dispersion effects.

### [40] [Landau-Level-Resolved Mode Mixing and Shot Noise in Gate-Defined Graphene Quantum Point Contacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22111)
*Shakthidhar Vilvanathan,Jerin Saji,Kristiana Frei,Jakub Tworzydlo,Manohar Kumar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过结合紧束缚模拟和随机矩阵理论，分析了石墨烯量子点接触在量子霍尔态下的散粒噪声特性，揭示了不同朗道能级中单通道与多通道混沌输运的区分特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯量子点接触在量子霍尔态下存在多种竞争输运机制，包括手性边缘传播、谷简并和栅极诱导的模式混合。这些机制的相互作用无法仅通过电导测量来观察，需要散粒噪声来探测传输本征值的统计特性。

Method: 研究开发了一个混合框架，结合栅极定义石墨烯量子点接触的紧束缚模拟和随机矩阵理论，预测不同量子霍尔态下的散粒噪声和法诺因子特征，并与hBN封装石墨烯霍尔棒实验电导图进行验证。

Result: 识别出三种不同输运区域：绝热传播、尖锐模式过滤和由分裂栅下局域态驱动的多模式混合。对于较高朗道能级，完全模式混合产生普适混沌腔极限F≈1/4；而零朗道能级收敛到F=1/3，源于其边缘态的子晶格极化特性。

Conclusion: F=1/3与F=1/4的交叉是朗道能级分辨的噪声特征，在电导测量中无法观察到，为石墨烯量子点接触中单通道与多通道混沌输运提供了直接区分标准。

Abstract: Graphene quantum point contacts (QPCs) in the quantum Hall regime host competing transport mechanisms including chiral edge propagation, valley degeneracy, and gate-induced mode mixing. Their interplay is not visible in conductance alone. Shot noise directly probes the statistics of transmission eigenvalues, revealing microscopic mode partitioning that conductance cannot access. We develop a hybrid framework combining tight-binding simulations of gate-defined graphene QPCs with random matrix theory (RMT) to predict shot noise and Fano factor signatures across different quantum Hall regimes, validated against experimental conductance maps of hBN-encapsulated graphene Hall bars. Three distinct regimes are identified: adiabatic propagation, sharp mode filtering, and multi-mode mixing driven by localized states beneath the split gate. For higher Landau levels ($N_L > 0$), complete mode mixing produces the universal chaotic-cavity limit $F \simeq 1/4$. Strikingly, the zeroth Landau level ($N_L = 0$) converges to $F = 1/3$. This distinct value originates in the sublattice polarization of the $N_L = 0$ edge state: coupling to mixed-sublattice localized states beneath the gate is suppressed, confining transport to an effective single channel ($N = 1$). Complete mixing within this single channel yields a flat transmission eigenvalue distribution and hence exactly $F = 1/3$ from single-channel RMT, numerically coincident with but mechanistically distinct from pseudo-diffusive zero-field graphene transport. The $F = 1/3$ versus $F = 1/4$ crossover is a Landau-level-resolved noise signature absent in conductance, providing a direct discriminator between single-channel and multi-channel chaotic transport in graphene QPCs.

</details>


### [41] [Suppression of Superconductivity and Electrostatic Side Gate Tuning in High Mobility SrTiO$_3$ Surface Electron Gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22205)
*Dickson Boahen,Sushant Padhye,Gayan De Silva,Eshanvi Rao,Evgeny Mikheev*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用氢等离子体暴露（hydrogen plasma exposure）在SrTiO₃（STO）衬底表面制备图案化高迁移率二维电子气（2DEG），通过样品在冷却之间的受控老化（controlled aging）系统探索大范围的电子密度，并在低至约10 mK的基温下测量超导转变。

Conclusion: 高迁移率准二维SrTiO₃电子气中的超导性被抑制，可能与垂直限制（vertical confinement）和电子轨道重排（electronic orbital rearrangement）有关。这种无外延（epitaxy-free）的高迁移率氧化物材料平台为图案化量子器件提供了有前景的新途径。

Abstract: We report on the fabrication and characterization of patterned high-mobility two-dimensional electron gases (2DEG) formed on SrTiO$_3$ (STO) substrate surfaces by hydrogen plasma exposure. The resulting devices consistently showed high electron mobilities up to 7400 cm$^2$/V$\cdot$s. A large range of electron density was systematically explored by controlled aging of the sample between cooldowns, including the expected range for the STO 2DEG superconducting dome. No superconducting transition was observed down to the base temperature of approximately 10 mK. This suggests suppression of superconductivity in high mobility quasi-two-dimensional SrTiO$_3$ electron gas, likely linked to vertical confinement and electronic orbital rearrangement. We systematically explored electrostatic gate modulation in this 2DEG system and its scaling with electron density and side gate geometry. In contrast with our initial expectation, we observed an improvement of achievable total modulation for larger side gate to channel separation. At low electron density, stochastic channel pinch-off events were observed, creating quasi-ballistic constrictions with irregular conductance quantization. This epitaxy-free and high mobility oxide material platform offers a promising new route towards patterning quantum devices.

### [42] [Supercurrent-Driven Néel Torque in Superconductor/Altermagnet Hybrids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22243)
*Hamed Vakili,Moaz Ali,Igor Žutić,Alexey A. Kovalev*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过理论预测超导体/反铁磁异质结中的超电流驱动奈尔自旋轨道力矩，分析自旋轨道耦合与动量依赖自旋分裂（如反铁磁中的效应）之间的相互作用导致的超电流诱导自旋极化。

Conclusion: 超导体/反铁磁异质结展现出独特的超电流驱动奈尔自旋轨道力矩效应，为无耗散控制磁性结构提供了新机制，在赛道存储器、超导电子学和非传统计算等领域具有应用潜力。

Abstract: We predict a supercurrent-driven Néel spin-orbit torque in a superconductor/$d$-wave altermagnet heterostructure, associated with the emergence of spin-triplet correlations. The effect can be understood as a consequence of the supercurrent-induced spin polarization, owing to the interplay between spin-orbit coupling and momentum-dependent spin splitting, as found, for example, in altermagnets. Remarkably, the supercurrent can be tuned by the Néel-vector direction, and the supercurrent-induced torque can both propel magnetic domain walls and reverse the Néel-vector orientation within a domain wall. These findings establish superconductor/altermagnet heterostructures as a versatile platform for the dissipationless control of the Néel vector, with potential applications in racetrack memory, dissipationless superconducting electronics, and unconventional computing.

### [43] [Evaluating LLM-generated code for domain-specific languages: molecular dynamics with LAMMPS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20630)
*Ethan Holbrook,Juan C. Verduzco,Alejandro Strachan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种评估大语言模型（LLMs）生成领域特定语言（DSLs）代码有效性的方法，特别针对LAMMPS分子动力学软件，通过规范化处理和语法分析来识别常见错误并加速验证过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLMs）正在改变科研人员与科学计算代码和数据的交互方式，但其在生成领域特定语言（domain-specific languages, DSLs）的科学有效代码/输入脚本方面的能力尚未得到充分探索，特别是对于像LAMMPS这样广泛使用的分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）软件。

Method: 提出了一种评估流程，包括生成规范化（canonical）文件的步骤和用于语法分析的可扩展解析器（extensible parser），这些步骤能够在不进行耗时计算测试的情况下隔离常见错误，并在生成有效输入文件后利用LLMs加速验证测试。

Result: 研究结果揭示了LLMs在生成科学领域特定语言方面的局限性，同时为领域专家将其整合到领域特定计算生态系统中提供了一条实用路径。

Conclusion: 该方法使领域专家（可能不熟悉DSL）能够评估LLM生成的LAMMPS输入文件的有效性，并利用这些评估来分析最先进LLMs的性能表现和识别常见问题，为LLMs在科学计算领域的应用提供了评估框架。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are changing the way researchers interact with code and data in scientific computing. While their ability to generate general-purpose code is well established, their effectiveness in producing scientifically valid code/input scripting for domain-specific languages (DSLs) remains largely unexplored. We propose an evaluation procedure that enables domain experts (who may not be experts in the DSL) to assess the validity of LLM-generated input files for LAMMPS, a widely used molecular dynamics (MD) code, and to use those assessments to evaluate the performance of state-of-the-art LLMs and identify common issues. Key to the evaluation procedure are a normalization step to generate canonical files and an extensible parser for syntax analysis. The following steps isolate common errors without incurring costly tests (in time and computational resources). Once a working input file is generated, LLMs can accelerate verification tests. Our findings highlight limitations of LLMs in generating scientific DSLs and a practical path forward for their integration into domain-specific computational ecosystems by domain experts.

</details>
