### [44] [Temporal Entanglement in Quantum Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20765)
*Olalla A. Castro-Alvaredo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于分支点扭转场（branch point twist field）的方法来计算时间熵（temporal entropy），这是一种跨不同时间区域的纠缠度量，与通常的空间纠缠度量相对应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将纠缠度量从空间维度扩展到时间维度，探索时间依赖的纠缠特性。传统纠缠熵主要关注空间区域间的量子关联，而本文关注不同时间区域间的纠缠结构。

Method: 采用分支点扭转场方法，通过形式因子（form factor）计算来处理时间依赖性。该方法将空间纠缠度量的计算框架推广到时间维度，特别考虑了时间熵的复数和振荡特性。

Result: 时间熵展现出复数、振荡的特性，类似于全局淬火（global quench）后纠缠熵的演化行为。分析表明时空熵都包含理论的普适信息，特别是质量谱（mass spectrum）信息，且两者都可用准粒子图像（quasiparticle picture）解释结果。

Conclusion: 空间熵和时间熵是同一概念的两个方面，都封装了理论的普适信息。时间熵的某些定性特征，如其与全局淬火后纠缠熵的相似性，与已知的时间度量一致。

Abstract: In this paper I propose a branch point twist field approach to computing a temporal entropy, that is, an entanglement measure across different time regions, as opposed to the usual spacial measures. I discuss how the shift to time-dependence manifests in form factor calculations and how the generalization of the spacial measures to temporal ones reproduces expected features of the temporal entanglement: the entropy is complex, oscillatory and reminiscent of the evolution of entanglement following a global quench. Considering the temporal von Neumann entropy, I argue that spacial and temporal entropies are two sides of the same coin. They both encapsulate universal information about the theory, in particular its mass spectrum. Also in both cases, a quasiparticle picture can be employed to interpret results. Some qualitative features of this version of temporal entropy, such as its similarity to the entanglement entropy after a global quench, are shared with the known temporal measures.

</details>


### [45] [Thermodynamics and Geometrical Optics of Reissner Nordstrom de Sitter Black Holes in Noncommutative Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20824)
*Phongsakorn Sereewat,David Senjaya,Piyabut Burikham*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了非对易时空（noncommutative spacetime）中Reissner-Nordstrom-de Sitter黑洞的热力学、光学和动力学性质，重点分析了最小长度尺度Theta的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索非对易时空结构对黑洞物理性质的影响，特别是最小长度尺度Theta如何修正黑洞的热力学、光学和动力学行为。

Method: 采用双视界框架建立有效的热力学第一定律，引入捕获事件视界和宇宙学视界相关性的熵。应用温温条件确定熵修正，使用Gauss-Bonnet方法计算弱偏转角，并通过Lyapunov指数和准正则模连接几何与动力学。

Result: 分析揭示了非对易性诱导的二阶相变，表明短距离结构的重要作用。非对易性修正了有效势和临界碰撞参数，并系统性地影响了轨道不稳定性和阻尼。

Conclusion: 非对易时空结构显著影响黑洞的热力学、光学和动力学性质，最小长度尺度Theta在这些修正中起关键作用，为理解量子引力效应提供了新视角。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic, optical, and dynamical properties of Reissner-Nordstrom-de Sitter black holes in a noncommutative spacetime with a minimal length scale Theta. Within a two-horizon framework, we formulate an effective first law of thermodynamics and introduce an entropy capturing correlations between the event and cosmological horizons. Imposing the lukewarm condition, where both horizons share a common temperature, uniquely determines the entropy correction and yields closed-form expressions for thermodynamic quantities. The analysis reveals a noncommutativity-induced second-order phase transition, emphasizing the role of short-distance structure. On the optical side, we study photon motion and weak gravitational lensing, showing that noncommutativity modifies the effective potential and critical impact parameter. Using the Gauss-Bonnet method, we derive the weak deflection angle and analyze the effects of charge and cosmological constant. We further connect geometry and dynamics through the Lyapunov exponent and quasinormal modes, showing systematic impacts on orbital instability and damping.

</details>


### [46] [Extending the Euler-Heisenberg action to include effects of local Lorentz-symmetry violating backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20880)
*Wagno Cesar e Silva,João Paulo S. Melo,José A. Helayël-Neto*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本研究计算了由时空依赖背景各向异性引起的欧拉-海森堡有效作用量的修正，这些各向异性破坏了洛伦兹对称性。采用谱正则化方法评估修正狄拉克算子的泛函行列式，在标准模型扩展框架下获得二阶背景参数的有效作用量修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在计算由违反洛伦兹对称性的时空依赖背景各向异性引起的欧拉-海森堡（Euler-Heisenberg）有效作用量的修正。这些修正对于理解洛伦兹对称性破坏对量子电动力学效应的影响具有重要意义。

Method: 采用谱正则化方法（spectral regularization method）评估修正狄拉克算子的泛函行列式。在标准模型扩展（Standard Model Extension, SME）框架下，考虑洛伦兹破坏参数 $m_5(x)$、$a_μ(x)$ 和 $b_μ(x)$，计算有效作用量至背景参数的二阶。

Result: 结果显示，对于这些参数的特定CPT偶组合，二阶修正违反了Furry定理，这与先前基于显式费曼图计算的分析一致。有效作用量的动力学（双线性）部分出现了非动力学轴子类项，类似于凝聚态系统中常见的结构，如外尔半金属（Weyl semimetals）。

Conclusion: 该过程修改了麦克斯韦方程，导致相应的（非）能量-动量张量守恒和波动方程。真空表现为非均匀介质，通过eikonal近似计算局部色散关系发现，背景的时空依赖性导致色散关系中出现虚数贡献，波振幅可能被放大或衰减，这反映了波与背景之间的能量-动量交换。

Abstract: This work sets out to compute the corrections to the Euler-Heisenberg effective action that arise from spacetime-dependent background anisotropies that violate Lorentz symmetry. To accomplish our task, we evaluate the functional determinant of the modified Dirac operator using the spectral regularization method. Within the framework of the Standard Model Extension (SME), these Lorentz-violating parameters correspond to the coefficients $m_5(x)$, $a_μ(x)$, and $b_μ(x)$. The corrected effective action is attained up to the second-order in the background parameters. Our results indicate a violation of Furry's theorem at second-order for specific CPT-even combinations of these parameters, in agreement with previous analyses based on explicit Feynman diagram calculations in scenarios with Lorentz-symmetry violation. In the kinetic (bilinear) piece of the effective action, non-dynamical axion-like terms emerge, resembling structures commonly encountered in condensed-matter systems, such as Weyl semimetals. We show how this procedure modifies the Maxwell equations, from which we present both the corresponding (non-)conservation of the energy-momentum tensor and the wave equation. We also notice that the vacuum behaves as an inhomogeneous medium, and compute the local dispersion relation by working in the eikonal approximation. As a result of the spacetime-dependence of the background, there appear imaginary contributions in the dispersion relation and, consequently, the wave amplitudes may be amplified or attenuated, which expresses the energy-momentum exchange between the waves and the background.

</details>


### [47] [Horizon Edge Partition Functions in $Λ>0$ Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20913)
*Y. T. Albert Law,Varun Lochab*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究获得了de Sitter空间和静态Nariai时空中引力与高自旋规范场的余维-2视界"边缘"自由度的谱，推进了先前关于单圈热力学的研究，揭示了正宇宙常数下单圈配分函数中的新对称性破缺结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在推进先前对de Sitter空间和静态Nariai时空中引力与高自旋规范场的单圈热力学分析，特别关注余维-2视界"边缘"自由度的谱结构。

Method: 通过分析de Sitter空间和静态Nariai时空中引力与高自旋规范场的余维-2视界"边缘"自由度谱，研究这些模式的对称性结构及其在单圈配分函数中的表现。

Result: 边缘谱展现出普遍的平移对称性（shift symmetries），揭示了正宇宙常数（positive cosmological constant）下单圈配分函数中的新颖对称性破缺结构。对于引力子（graviton），这些模式具有宇宙视界（cosmic horizon）涨落的几何解释，且在Nariai情况下也持续存在。

Conclusion: 研究获得了de Sitter空间和Nariai时空中引力与高自旋规范场的边缘自由度谱，揭示了正宇宙常数下单圈配分函数中的新对称性破缺结构，为理解量子引力在宇宙学背景下的热力学性质提供了新视角。

Abstract: We obtain the spectra of codimension-2 horizon "edge" degrees of freedom for gravity and higher-spin gauge fields in de Sitter space and in the static Nariai spacetime, advancing previous Lorentzian and Euclidean analyses of one-loop thermodynamics. The edge spectra exhibit universal shift symmetries, revealing a novel symmetry-breaking structure in one-loop partition functions with positive cosmological constant. For the graviton, these modes admit a geometric interpretation as fluctuations of the cosmic horizon, which also persists in the Nariai case.

</details>


### [48] [Gaugings of Groupoids, Strings in Shadows, and Emergent Poisson $σ$-Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20914)
*Rafał R. Suszek*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种针对Polyakov-Alvarez-Gawędzki二维非线性σ模型的刚性李群胚对称性的规范原理，该模型具有度量目标空间和由阿贝尔gerbe产生的陈-西蒙斯微分特征给出的WZ项。该原理基于主胚丛及其连接的概念，并展示了模型降维到主胚丛阴影所需的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在为具有度量目标空间$(M,g_M)$和由阿贝尔gerbe $\mathcal{G}$产生的陈-西蒙斯（CS）微分特征给出的WZ项的Polyakov-Alvarez-Gawędzki二维非线性σ模型的刚性李群胚对称性$G=>M$建立规范原理。这扩展了先前针对作用群胚的研究方案。

Method: 方法基于Strobl和作者引入的主胚丛（principaloid bundle）及其连接$(P,Θ)$的概念。通过要求gerbe $\mathcal{G}$具有扭曲的$G$-等变结构，将模型降维到$P$的阴影，该结构预量化了gerbe曲率$H_M$到群胚神经的BSS上同调中3-上循环的乘法扩展$(H_M,ρ,0)$。降维过程伴随着$P$结构群的$g_M$-等距/$ρ$-完整约化。

Result: 研究展示了模型降维到主胚丛阴影需要gerbe的扭曲$G$-等变结构，并伴随结构群的组合约化。在辛（symplectic）设定下，增强过程导致标准泊松σ模型的出现。反之，通过平坦等变gerbe对（局部）泊松σ模型进行共增强，产生了一种以底层辛主胚丛阴影为配置丛的新场论。

Conclusion: 论文提出了完整的相关规范异常和不等价格规化的上同调分析。提出了简单的Cartan型关联机制来解释主胚丛结构群的约化，该机制允许任意数量的不同带电物质场物种与给定规范场耦合。这为具有刚性李群胚对称性的σ模型提供了系统的规范原理框架。

Abstract: The gauge principle is proposed for rigid Lie-groupoidal symmetries $G=>M$ of the Polyakov-Alvarez-Gawędzki 2$d$ non-linear $σ$-model with metric target $(M,g_M)$ and the WZ term given by a CS differential character coming from an abelian gerbe $\mathcal{G}$. The principle bases on the notion of principaloid bundle with connection $(P,Θ)$, introduced by Strobl and the Author. The descent of the model to the shadow of $P$ is demonstrated to require a twisted $G$-equivariant structure on $\mathcal{G}$, prequantising a multiplicative extension $(H_M,ρ,0)$ of the gerbe's curvature $H_M$ to a 3-cocycle in the BSS cohomology of the groupoid's nerve. The descent is accompanied by a combined $g_M$-isometric/$ρ$-holonomic reduction of the structure group of $P$, and uses an augmentation of the original gerbe by a trivial one depending quadratically on $Θ$. The latter couples to the field of the $σ$-model -- in an extension of the scheme worked out for the action groupoid by Gawędzki, Waldorf and the Author -- through the comomentum component of the Spencer pair of $ρ$, as described by Crainic et al. A fully fledged cohomological analysis of the relevant gauge anomaly and of inequivalent gaugings is presented. In the symplectic setting, the augmentation procedure is shown to lead to the emergence of the standard Poisson $σ$-model. Conversely, a coaugmentation of a (local) Poisson $σ$-model by a flat equivariant gerbe yields a novel field theory with the shadow of the underlying symplectic principaloid bundle as the configuration bundle, and with manifest lagrangean gauge symmetry. A simple Cartan-type associating mechanism is proposed to account for the reduction of the structure group of the principaloid bundle. The mechanism allows for the coupling of an arbitrary number of distinct charged matter-field species to a given gauge field.

</details>


### [49] [Sine-Liouville gravity as a Vertex Model on Planar Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.18916)
*Ivan Kostov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了平面图上六顶点模型单参数推广的普适行为，称为七顶点（7v）模型。该模型通过矩阵模型方法计算配分函数，揭示了其与正弦-刘维尔引力的联系，并分析了稀相和密相之间的流动关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索七顶点模型的普适行为，该模型作为六顶点模型的单参数推广，其环权重不再是拓扑的，且环动力学与晶格局部几何结构相互纠缠。这为研究具有几何依赖相互作用的统计模型提供了新视角。

Method: 采用矩阵模型方法，通过对偶矩阵模型的谱曲线计算七顶点模型的球面和圆盘配分函数。固定长度的圆盘配分函数是贝塞尔积分的变形，即Krätzel函数。通过比较七顶点矩阵模型和矩阵量子力学，分析它们在正弦-刘维尔引力中的互补实现。

Result: 研究发现七顶点矩阵模型和矩阵量子力学提供了正弦-刘维尔引力的两种互补非微扰实现，它们共享相同的经典谱曲线但描述不同类型的膜。七顶点矩阵模型覆盖了参数范围，其中闵可夫斯基矩阵量子力学缺乏多重快子散射的简单解释。稀相和密相之间的流动被识别为具有虚质量耦合的正弦-戈登模型中无质量流动的引力类比。

Conclusion: 七顶点模型在连续极限下表现出与O(n)环模型类似的大质量、稀相和密相，但其环权重具有几何依赖性。该模型与正弦-刘维尔引力存在深刻联系，流动的两个端点由耦合到刘维尔引力并在两个不同半径圆上紧致化的自由玻色子描述。

Abstract: We investigate the universal behaviour of a one-parameter generalisation of the six-vertex model on planar graphs, which we refer to as the seven-vertex (7v) model. The 7v model is characterised by a temperature coupling and its continuum limit exhibits massive, dilute and dense phases similarly to the $O(n)$ loop model. However, there is an important distinction: the loop weights are no longer topological and the dynamics of the loops is now entangled with the local geometry of the lattice. We compute the sphere and disk partition functions of the 7v model from the spectral curve of the dual matrix model. The disk partition function for fixed length is a deformation of the Bessel integral known as the Krätzel function. We argue that the 7v matrix model and Matrix Quantum Mechanics provide two complementary non-perturbative realisations of sine-Liouville gravity. Specifically, we find that the continuum limits of 7vMM and MQM share the same classical spectral curve but describe two different types of branes in sine-Liouville gravity. The 7vMM precisely covers the range of parameters where the Minkowskian MQM lacks a simple interpretation in terms of multiple tachyon scattering. We investigate the flow relating the dilute and dense phases and argue that this flow is the gravitational analogue of the massless flow in the sine-Gordon model with imaginary mass coupling. The two endpoints of the flow are described by a free boson coupled to Liouville gravity and compactified on circles with two different radii.

</details>


### [50] [Dynamical symmetries of the Calogero-Coulomb model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21325)
*Tigran Hakobyan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文构建了量子Calogero-Coulomb模型中包含粒子交换的动力学对称性，该对称性由受交换（Dunkl）算符形变的so(N+1,2)代数描述，其波函数可分类为so(1,2)代数的无限维最低权多重态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子Calogero模型在约束库仑场中的动力学对称性，特别关注包含粒子交换效应的对称代数结构。该工作旨在揭示这类可积系统的代数性质及其与共形对称性的联系。

Method: 通过引入受交换（Dunkl）算符形变的so(N+1,2)代数来构建动力学对称性，其不变子空间由Dunkl角动量张量和修正的Laplace-Runge-Lenz矢量生成。利用共形子代数so(1,2)表达具有线性谱的哈密顿量等距类比。

Result: 成功构造了量子Calogero-Coulomb模型的动力学对称性，该对称性由形变的so(N+1,2)代数描述。Calogero-Coulomb哈密顿量的波函数可分类为无限维最低权so(1,2)多重态，揭示了系统的代数结构特征。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了量子Calogero-Coulomb模型与形变李代数的深刻联系，证明了其波函数的代数分类性质，为理解这类可积系统的对称性结构提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We construct the dynamical symmetry of the quantum Calogero model with particle exchange in a confining Coulomb field. This symmetry is governed by the algebra $so(N+1,2)$, deformed by exchange (Dunkl) operators, with its invariant sector generated by the Dunkl angular momentum tensor and the modified Laplace-Runge-Lenz vector. The equidistant analogue of the Hamiltonian, with a linear spectrum, is expressed in terms of the conformal subalgebra $so(1,2)$. In addition, the wave functions of the Calogero-Coulomb Hamiltonian are classified into infinite-dimensional lowest-weight $so(1,2)$ multiplets.

</details>


### [51] [Shape modes of \(\mathbb{C}P^1\) vortices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21343)
*Nora Gavrea,Derek Harland,Martin Speight*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究规范\(\mathbb{C}P^1\) sigma模型中涡旋（vortex）内模（internal modes）的存在性，证明了一般\(\mathbb{C}P^1\)涡旋解至少存在一个形状模（shape mode），并发现其本征值接近散射阈值（scattering threshold）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究规范\(\mathbb{C}P^1\) sigma模型中涡旋内模的存在性问题，这类内模对于理解涡旋动力学和稳定性具有重要意义。

Method: 开发了清晰的几何形式体系（geometric formalism），突出Jacobi算子的对称性；基于能量泛函（energy functional）的Bogomol'nyi分解；对径向对称涡旋进行数值计算。

Result: 证明了一般\(\mathbb{C}P^1\)涡旋解在\(\mathbb{R}^2\)上至少存在一个形状模；数值计算了径向对称涡旋的形状模和相应频率；发现形状模本征值非常接近散射阈值。

Conclusion: 弱束缚形状模可能是\(\mathbb{C}P^1\)模型的特性；所发展的几何形式体系可推广到其他具有Bogomol'nyi分解的模型。

Abstract: In this paper we investigate the existence of internal modes of vortices in the gauged \(\mathbb{C}P^1\) sigma model. We develop a clean geometric formalism that highlights the symmetries of the Jacobi operator, obtained from the second variation of the energy functional. The formalism and subsequent results fundamentally rely on the Bogomol'nyi decomposition of the energy functional, and can therefore be extended to other models with such a decomposition. We prove the existence of at least one shape mode for a general \(\mathbb{C}P^1\) vortex solution on \(\mathbb{R}^2\), and find numerically the shape modes and corresponding frequencies of a radially symmetric vortex. A surprising result is that the shape mode eigenvalues are very close to the scattering threshold, suggesting weakly bound shape modes could be characteristic of the \(\mathbb{C}P^1\) model.

</details>

*Ctirad Klimcik*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study a class of E-models, referred to as Euclidean E-models, in which the operator E acting on the Drinfeld double squares to minus the identity rather than to the identity. This modification leads to significant structural differences from the standard E-model framework. Most notably, the sigma-models naturally associated with these E-models possess a Euclidean world-sheet.
  Although, for some Drinfeld doubles, every Lorentzian E-model admits a natural Euclidean counterpart, the duality, integrability, and renormalization properties of Euclidean E-models are independent of the Lorentzian case and must be studied separately.
  We illustrate the general constructions using the example of a Euclidean bi-Yang-Baxter deformation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Higher-spin symmetry is known to mix lower-spin fields with higher-spin fields, creating a complex interaction picture where no closed finite field sector is expected to exist for dimensions greater than three. In particular, we show that self-dual gravity with a cosmological constant emerges as a unique rigid part of higher-spin interactions.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用三种几何方法：首先使用Souriau最小耦合（minimal coupling）方法引入协变但非正则的坐标；其次通过相空间中的Ehresmann联络（Ehresmann connections）产生协变但非坐标的标架；最后引入协变泊松括号（covariant Poisson bracket）概念，直接推导协变运动方程。

Result: 建立了与背景规范场和引力场耦合的粒子的显式协变哈密顿表述（manifestly covariant Hamiltonian formulations），无论粒子是否具有自旋（spin）。同时阐明了该框架的变分原理（variational principle）和路径积分（path integral）起源。

Abstract: We investigate the tension between symplecticity and gauge covariance in classical Hamiltonian mechanics. The pursuit of manifest covariance over manifest symplecticity results in a unique geometric formulation. Firstly, covariant yet non-canonical coordinates are employed by adopting Souriau's approach to minimal coupling. Secondly, covariant yet non-coordinate frames arise from Ehresmann connections in phase space. Thirdly, the concept of covariant Poisson bracket is introduced, facilitating direct derivations of covariant equations of motion. In this way, we establish manifestly covariant Hamiltonian formulations of particles coupled to background gauge and gravitational fields, with or without spin. The variational principle and path integral origins of our framework are also explicated.

### [61] [At the Corner of Quantum and Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21941)
*Ludovic Varrin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在二维背景下发展了量子角点（quantum corner）框架，完整描述了二维扩展角点对称群的表示理论，并将其解释为量子引力的候选希尔伯特空间。通过胶合程序计算纠缠熵，并利用相干态在半经典极限下重现了贝肯斯坦-霍金熵公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 角点提议（corner proposal）将物理角点对称性代数作为量子引力的基本要素，类似于庞加莱群在量子场论中的作用。论文旨在二维背景下发展量子角点框架，建立量子引力候选希尔伯特空间的表示理论。

Method: 采用扩展相空间形式体系（extended phase-space formalism），发展二维扩展角点对称群（two-dimensional extended corner symmetry group）的完整表示理论。通过胶合程序（gluing procedure）构造量子态并计算纠缠熵，利用扭曲动量映射（twisted moment maps）和广义佩雷洛莫夫相干态（generalized Perelomov coherent states）连接经典与量子结构。

Result: 获得了二维扩展角点对称群的完整表示理论，其表示空间可解释为量子引力的候选希尔伯特空间。在静态球对称时空背景下，特定相干态族在半经典极限下重现了视界面积熵律，为贝肯斯坦-霍金公式提供了基于对称性的量子解释。

Conclusion: 论文成功在二维背景下发展了量子角点框架，建立了角点对称性的量子表示理论，并展示了其在描述局部子系统、计算纠缠熵以及解释贝肯斯坦-霍金熵方面的应用潜力。该框架为量子引力研究提供了基于对称性的新途径。

Abstract: In the presence of spacetime boundaries, diffeomorphisms in gravitational theories can become physical and acquire non-vanishing Noether charges. These charges obey an algebra which, within the extended phase-space formalism, faithfully realizes diffeomorphism algebra. The corner proposal takes this algebra of physical corner symmetries as a fundamental ingredient of quantum gravity, in close analogy with the role of the Poincaré group in quantum field theory. In this thesis we develop the quantum corner framework in the two-dimensional setting. We give the full representation theory of the two-dimensional extended corner symmetry group, which may be interpreted either as the symmetry group of two-dimensional gravity or as the corner symmetry group relevant for four-dimensional spherically symmetric gravity. Within the corner proposal, the resulting representation spaces are then interpreted as candidate Hilbert spaces for quantum gravity. This representation-theoretic structure naturally enables a description of local subsystems. In particular, we present a gluing procedure that constructs quantum states associated with an entangling corner between two spacetime subregions, and use it to compute the entanglement entropy between the two regions. To connect the quantum observables to the classical corner charges, we construct the coadjoint orbits of the quantum corner symmetry group and relate them to the classical structure through twisted moment maps and to the quantum structure through generalized Perelomov coherent states. This provides a notion of semiclassical limit within the corner framework. Finally, in the context of static, spherically symmetric spacetimes, we show that a distinguished family of coherent states reproduces the horizon area law for entropy in the semiclassical limit, yielding a quantum, symmetry-based explanation of the Bekenstein--Hawking formula.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We calculate the correction exponents in the chiral Heisenberg model in the $1/N$ expansion. These exponents are related to the slopes of $β$ functions at the phase transition point. ### [63] [On gauging Abelian extensions of finite and U(1) groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22110)
*Riccardo Villa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究阿贝尔扩展（Abelian extensions）形式的全局对称性 $A \to G \to K$，比较了直接对 $G$ 进行规范（gauging）与先对 $A$ 再对 $K$ 进行规范两种程序，证明了在有限阿贝尔群和 $K \simeq U(1)$ 情况下两者的等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有 $G$ 对称性的量子场论（quantum field theory）中，比较直接对 $G$ 进行规范与先对 $A$ 再对 $K$ 进行规范两种程序的等价性，并探讨连续 $K=U(1)$ 情况下的对偶对称性（dual symmetry）结构。

Method: 采用阿贝尔扩展 $A \to G \to K$ 的框架，其中 $A$ 为有限群，比较 $\mathcal{T}/G$ 与 $\mathcal{T}/A/K$ 两种规范程序。对于连续 $K=U(1)$ 情况，使用微分上同调（differential cohomology）更好地描述对偶对称性 $\widehat{\mathbb{Z}}_q^{(d-2)}$ 与磁 $U(1)_m^{(d-3)}$ 对称性的拓扑数据关系。

Result: 对于有限阿贝尔群和 $K \simeq U(1)$ 情况，证明了两种规范程序的等价性：$\mathcal{T}/G \simeq \mathcal{T}/A/K$。在连续 $K=U(1)$ 情况下，对偶对称性 $\widehat{\mathbb{Z}}_q^{(d-2)}$ 构成一个扩展，表征了磁 $U(1)_m^{(d-3)}$ 对称性的拓扑数据。

Conclusion: 阿贝尔扩展对称性的规范程序在有限阿贝尔群和 $K \simeq U(1)$ 情况下具有等价性，而连续情况的拓扑结构可通过微分上同调更好地描述，并与对称性分数化（symmetry fractionalization）存在关联。

Abstract: We consider Abelian extensions of global symmetries of the form $A \to G \to K$, with $A$ finite (and similar higher-group structures). For a quantum field theory $\mathcal{T}$ with symmetry $G$, we compare gauging $G$ directly with gauging first $A$ and then $K$, and show that for finite Abelian groups and for $K \simeq U(1)$ the two procedures are equivalent as expected, $\mathcal{T}/G \simeq \mathcal{T}/A/K$. In the continuous case $K=U(1)$, after gauging the full extension, the dual symmetry $\widehat{\mathbb{Z}}_q^{(d-2)}$ fits into an extension characterizing the topological data of the magnetic $U(1)_m^{(d-3)}$ symmetry. This is better described using differential cohomology. We also briefly comment on the relation to symmetry fractionalization.

The broken charge is the Kugo-Ojima charge. The corresponding unphysical Goldstone boson is a bound-state superposition of two gluons, three gluons and a ghost-antighost pair. Mass generation occurs via the Schwinger mechanism, triggered by the formation of the Goldstone boson. Once corrected for symmetry breaking, the color charge operator is unbroken and confining.

### [65] [CayleyPy-4: AI-Holography. Towards analogs of holographic string dualities for AI tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22195)

Zaitsev,F. Petrov,L. Petrov,T. Gaintseva,A. Gavrilova,M. N. Smirnov,N. Kalinin,A. Khan,K. Jung,H. Mousset,H. Isambert,O. Debeaupuis*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探索大型图上的AI方法，提出离散全息弦对偶性（discrete holographic string dualities）的新概念。研究动机源于许多现代AI任务（如GPT风格语言模型或强化学习系统）可视为预测图上粒子轨迹的直接类比。

Method: 研究针对一大类Cayley图，证明其存在离散弦（discrete strings）的对偶描述。特别关注对称群S_n的Cayley图，通过机器学习与传统工具结合获得新数据集，并在大量初始示例中验证对偶性。

Result: 发现对称群S_n的Cayley图对应平坦平面多边形（flat, planar polygons），图直径等于多边形内整数点数乘以n。图的顶点可全息映射到多边形内路径，图距离对应路径下面积，直接实现"复杂度=体积"（"complexity = volume"）范式。在大n极限下发现连续共形场论（continuous CFTs）和对偶弦的证据。

Conclusion: 此类对偶性可能扩展到一系列AI系统，带来更高效的计算方法。弦全息图像（string holographic images）作为数据嵌入的自然候选，受AdS/CFT中"复杂度=体积"原理启发。新数据集将为更一般情况下的对偶性建立提供工具。

Abstract: This is the fourth paper in the CayleyPy project, which applies AI methods to the exploration of large graphs. In this work, we suggest the existence of a new discrete version of holographic string dualities for this setup, and discuss their relevance to AI systems and mathematics. Many modern AI tasks -- such as those addressed by GPT-style language models or RL systems -- can be viewed as direct analogues of predicting particle trajectories on graphs. We investigate this problem for a large family of Cayley graphs, for which we show that surprisingly it admits a dual description in terms of discrete strings. We hypothesize that such dualities may extend to a range of AI systems where they can lead to more efficient computational approaches. In particular, string holographic images of states are proposed as natural candidates for data embeddings, motivated by the "complexity = volume" principle in AdS/CFT.
  For Cayley graphs of the symmetric group S_n, our results indicate that the corresponding dual objects are flat, planar polygons. The diameter of the graph is equal to the number of integer points inside the polygon scaled by n. Vertices of the graph can be mapped holographically to paths inside the polygon, and the usual graph distances correspond to the area under the paths, thus directly realising the "complexity = volume" paradigm. We also find evidence for continuous CFTs and dual strings in the large n limit. We confirm this picture and other aspects of the duality in a large initial set of examples. We also present new datasets (obtained by a combination of ML and conventional tools) which should be instrumental in establishing the duality for more general cases.

### [66] [Sparse Weak-Form Discovery of Stochastic Generators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20904)
*Eshwar R A,Gajanan V. Honnavar*

Main category: stat.ME

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种数据驱动的随机微分方程（SDEs）发现框架，首次将弱形式分部积分方法与随机系统识别目标相结合，通过空间高斯核函数消除结构回归偏差，实现漂移和扩散项的准确识别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在统一随机微分方程发现中的两种主要方法：弱形式SINDy（Weak SINDy）的分部积分方法和随机SINDy（stochastic SINDy）的随机系统识别目标。现有方法在随机设置中使用时间测试函数时存在结构回归偏差问题，需要新的框架来解决这一局限性。

Method: 核心创新是采用空间高斯测试函数$K_j(x)=\exp(-|x-x_j|^2/2h^2)$替代时间测试函数。由于核权重$K_j(X_{t_n})$是$\mathcal{F}_{t_n}$-可测的，而布朗创新$\xi_n$独立于$\mathcal{F}_{t_n}$，该方法保证了所有噪声项在给定当前状态下的条件期望为零。该设计将SDE识别问题转化为两个稀疏线性系统——一个用于漂移项$b(x)$，一个用于扩散张量$a(x)$——它们共享单一设计矩阵，并通过$\ell_1$正则化回归与分组交叉验证联合求解。对于状态依赖扩散，采用两步偏差校正程序处理。

Result: 在Ornstein-Uhlenbeck过程、双阱朗之万系统和乘性扩散过程三个基准测试中验证，该方法成功恢复了所有活跃多项式生成器，系数误差低于4%，平稳密度总变差距离低于0.01，自相关函数准确再现了所有三个基准的真实弛豫时间尺度。

Conclusion: 该框架首次统一了弱形式SINDy和随机SINDy方法，通过空间高斯核函数有效消除了随机设置中的结构回归偏差，实现了随机微分方程漂移和扩散项的准确数据驱动发现，在多个基准测试中表现出优异的性能。

Abstract: We introduce a framework for the data-driven discovery of stochastic differential equations (SDEs) that unifies, for the first time, the weak-form integration-by-parts approach of Weak SINDy with the stochastic system identification goal of stochastic SINDy. The central novelty is the adoption of spatial Gaussian test functions $K_j(x)=\exp(-|x-x_j|^2/2h^2)$ in place of temporal test functions. Because the kernel weight $K_j(X_{t_n})$ is $\mathcal{F}_{t_n}$-measurable and the Brownian innovation $ξ_n$ is independent of $\mathcal{F}_{t_n}$, every noise term in the projected response has zero conditional mean given the current state -- a property that guarantees unbiasedness in expectation and prevents the structural regression bias that afflicts temporal test functions in the stochastic setting. This design choice converts the SDE identification problem into two sparse linear systems -- one for the drift $b(x)$ and one for the diffusion tensor $a(x)$ -- that share a single design matrix and are solved jointly via $\ell_1$-regularised regression with grouped cross-validation. A two-step bias-correction procedure handles state-dependent diffusion. Validated on the Ornstein--Uhlenbeck process, the double-well Langevin system, and a multiplicative diffusion process, the method recovers all active polynomial generators with coefficient errors below 4\%, stationary-density total-variation distances below 0.01, and autocorrelation functions that faithfully reproduce true relaxation timescales across all three benchmarks.

Our work paves the way towards complex antenna geometries optimized for local addressing of PCMs to achieve sophisticated crystallization patterns, enabling on-demand programming of individual nanoantennas within metasurfaces.

More recently, topological point singularities encoded into photonic structures have been shown to enable confinement of optical modes with the topologically nontrivial nature of the cavity imprinted into the vorticity of optical far fields. Here we demonstrate that the two latter concepts - domain wall and point singularities - can be unified into an even more powerful tool to enable arbitrarily shaped resonant cavities of any dimension supporting spectrally stable zero-energy modes. *Jakob Wetzel,Javier Taboada-Gutiérrez,Matthias Roeper,Felix G. Kaps,Giuliano Esposito,Drini Marchese,Robin Buschbeck,Pauline Lenz,John M. Klopf,Hans A. Bechtel,Stephanie N. Gilbert Corder,Jeremie Teyssier,Susanne C. Kehr,Lukas M. Eng,Alexey B. Kuzmenko,Samuel D. Seddon*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究展示了扭曲钙钛矿LaAlO₃中的铁弹性孪晶壁（ferroelastic twin walls）可作为天然平台，实现纳米尺度光的宽带横向限制和优异通道化，无需制造工艺即可获得比自由空间波长小260倍的横向光学尺寸。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度光的控制和操控对于基础科学和纳米光子技术的发展至关重要。虽然二维材料的堆叠和扭曲研究已取得进展，但各向异性块体晶体（anisotropic bulk crystals）的相应能力尚未充分探索。

Method: 利用扭曲钙钛矿LaAlO₃中的铁弹性孪晶壁，这些是分离不同取向畴区的晶体学完美二维片层（crystallographically perfect 2D-sheets），作为天然平台研究光的纳米尺度限制和通道化。

Result: 局域于孪晶壁的电磁场表现出比自由空间波长小260倍的横向光学尺寸。根据相邻畴取向和频率，孪晶壁模式优先集中或排斥电磁能量，构成宽带中红外（MIR）和太赫兹（THz）纳米光子学的天然构建模块。

Conclusion: 铁弹性孪晶壁为纳米尺度光的宽带横向限制和优异通道化提供了天然平台，无需制造工艺即可实现极小的光学尺寸，为极化激元电路（polaritonic circuitry）的宽带中红外和太赫兹纳米光子学提供了天然构建模块。

Abstract: The control and steering of light at nanometre length scales is crucial for the development of both fundamental science and nanophotonic technologies. Recent advancements have been achieved by exploiting various crystalline anisotropies, allowing for subdiffractional and diffraction-less canalisation of energy. These studies in particular benefit from stacking and twisting of 2D materials, whereas corresponding capabilities of anisotropic bulk crystals are rather unexplored. In this work, we show that ferroelastic twin walls - crystallographically perfect 2D-sheets that separate regions of differently oriented domains - in the distorted perovskite LaAlO3 provide a natural platform for broadband lateral confinement and superb canalisation of light at the nanoscale. Without fabrication processes, the electromagnetic fields localised at such walls exhibit lateral optical sizes up to 260 times smaller than the free-space wavelength. Depending on the adjacent domain orientation and frequency, the twin wall pattern preferentially concentrates or repels the electromagnetic energy, constituting a natural building block towards broadband MIR and THz nanophotonics for polaritonic circuitry.

</details>

### [71] [A unified machine learning framework for ab initio multiscale modeling of liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20493)
*Anna T. Bui,Stephen J. Cox*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种结合机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）与神经经典密度泛函理论（neural cDFT）的多尺度建模框架，用于从第一性原理预测流体的热力学行为，显著提高了计算效率并保持了概念透明度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解和预测液体物质在不同长度尺度上的行为，仅基于薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）编码的微观相互作用，是物理科学中的一个核心挑战。实现这一目标不仅需要准确高效的分子间作用力描述，还需要一个连接微观、介观和宏观尺度的一致框架。

Method: 通过结合机器学习原子间势（machine-learned interatomic potentials, MLIPs）与神经经典密度泛函理论（neural classical density functional theory, neural cDFT）构建框架。MLIPs基于量子力学能量和力训练，用于生成非均匀微观密度分布，这些数据再用于训练神经cDFT。

Result: 第一性原理神经cDFT不仅计算效率显著高于分子模拟，还能准确再现水和二氧化碳的体相状态方程（bulk equations of state）和液-气相图（liquid-vapor phase diagrams）。该框架预测了限制条件如何改变水的液-气共存，并捕捉了超临界二氧化碳中的Fisher-Widom线和Widom线等复杂行为。

Conclusion: 第一性原理神经cDFT在单一统一概念框架内，为流体的多尺度建模建立了一条通用的第一性原理路径，提供了从微观相互作用到宏观热力学行为的透明桥梁。

Abstract: Understanding and predicting the behavior of liquid matter across length scales, using only the microscopic interactions encoded in the Schrödinger equation, remains a central challenge in the physical sciences. Achieving this goal requires not only an accurate and efficient description of intermolecular forces but also a consistent framework that bridges the micro-, meso-, and macroscales. Here, by combining machine-learned interatomic potentials (MLIPs) with neural classical density functional theory (neural cDFT), we present such a framework. The underlying idea is simple: MLIPs trained on quantum-mechanical energies and forces are used to generate inhomogeneous microscopic density profiles, which in turn serve as the training data for neural cDFT. The resulting ab initio neural cDFT is not only significantly more computationally efficient than molecular simulations, but also provides a conceptually transparent route to the thermodynamics of both homogeneous and inhomogeneous systems. We demonstrate the approach for both water and carbon dioxide using several exchange-correlation functionals. Beyond accurately reproducing bulk equations of state and liquid-vapor phase diagrams, ab initio neural cDFT predicts, from first principles, how confinement modifies liquid-vapor coexistence in water. It also captures complex behavior in supercritical carbon dioxide such as the Fisher-Widom and Widom lines. Ab initio neural cDFT establishes a general first-principles route to multiscale modeling of fluids within a single unified conceptual framework.

</details>


### [72] [olLOSC: Unified and efficient density functional approximation to correct delocalization error in molecules and periodic materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21906)
*Yichen Fan,Jacob Z. Williams,Weitao Yang*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了olLOSC方法，一种基于轨道自由电子线性响应计算曲率的局域轨道标度校正方法，用于校正密度泛函理论中的离域误差，在分子和材料中实现了高效、统一的校正方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密度泛函理论（DFT）在计算分子和材料量子性质方面具有潜力，但常用的密度泛函近似（DFAs）存在系统性离域误差（delocalization error），表现为低估带隙、过度离域的电荷以及界面能级错位等问题，限制了其定量预测能力。虽然已有多种方法尝试解决此问题，但仍缺乏一个准确、高效且统一的解决方案来描述有限系统和材料的总能量、电荷密度和能带结构。

Method: 基于线性响应局域轨道标度校正（lrLOSC），本文提出了olLOSC方法：一种通过轨道自由电子线性响应（orbital-free electronic linear response）计算曲率的局域轨道标度校正方法。该方法保持了与lrLOSC相当的精度，但计算效率显著提高。

Result: olLOSC能够校正离域误差，特别是在分子和具有小到中等带隙的材料中，有效改善了低估的带隙和总能量。该方法在相同的轨道自由近似下，实现了对分子和材料的统一校正。

Conclusion: olLOSC通过统一的近似方法，为在分子、材料和界面之间实现稳健且高效的密度泛函理论应用开辟了道路，为解决离域误差问题提供了有前景的解决方案。

Abstract: Density functional theory (DFT) is the most promising method for calculating quantum properties of molecules and materials at moderate and large scales. However, commonly used density functional approximations (DFAs) have systematic delocalization error, as demonstrated by underestimated band gaps, over-delocalized charges, and energy level misalignment at interfaces, which limits its quantitative prediction. Extensive efforts, such as the $GW$ approximation to many-body perturbation theory, system-specific tuning of DFA parameters, and correction functionals have been developed to address delocalization error. However, an accurate, efficient, and unified solution to describe total energy, charge density and band structure for both finite systems and materials is still not available. Building on the linear-response localized orbital scaling correction (lrLOSC), we introduce olLOSC: a localized orbital scaling correction with curvature calculated by orbital-free electronic linear response. olLOSC has comparable accuracy to lrLOSC, but is much more computationally efficient. olLOSC corrects delocalization error - especially underestimated gaps, but also the total energy - both in molecules and in materials with small and moderate band gaps, within the same orbital-free approximation. Critically, with a a unified approximation, olLOSC opens the path for robust and efficient DFT applications across molecules, materials, and interfaces.

</details>

Method: 采用瞬态时间相关函数方法（transient time correlation function method, TTCF）评估石墨烯壁间受限水系统的滑移长度随剪切速率的变化。计算了跨越六个数量级剪切速率下的相应Navier摩擦系数，并与平衡极限进行比较。

Conclusion: TTCF方法在高滑移（低应变率）系统中展现出卓越能力，能够准确计算实验相关条件下的滑移特性。该研究证实了平衡方法在实验可及应变率下与NEMD测量结果的一致性，为低剪切速率系统的精确表征提供了有效工具。

Abstract: The transient time correlation function method (TTCF) has emerged as a powerful methodology for accurately probing systems at low shear rates. In the present study, TTCF was used to evaluate the shear rate dependence of the slip length in a high-slip system consisting of water confined between graphene walls at experimentally accessible shear rates, for which classical nonequilibrium molecular dynamics (NEMD) is unfeasible. The corresponding Navier friction coefficient was computed for all shear rates spanning six orders of magnitude and compared with the equilibrium limit. We report for the first time NEMD results obtained at experimentally accessible shear rates using the TTCF approach for a system that has attracted significant interest over the past decades. The slip length calculated with TTCF is in good agreement with previous equilibrium molecular dynamics simulations and experiments. Our aim here is to highlight the extraordinary power of TTCF, particularly for high-slip (low strain-rate) systems, and to verify that equilibrium methods directly match NEMD measurements at experimentally accessible strain rates.

### [75] [Nonexistence of multi-bubble radial solutions to the 3D energy critical wave equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21602)
*Ruipeng Shen*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了3D径向聚焦能量临界波方程不存在包含两个或更多孤立子的全局解或II型爆破解，从而完成了径向解渐近行为的完全分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然已知3D径向情况下任何全局解或II型爆破解（type II blow-up solution）在时间趋于无穷或爆破时刻会分解为多个解耦的基态（ground states）、自由波和小误差（即孤立子分解soliton resolution），但所有已知例子都只包含不超过一个孤立子。本文旨在探究是否存在包含多个孤立子的解。

Method: 通过数学分析证明方法，研究3D径向聚焦能量临界波方程（focusing, energy-critical wave equation）的解的渐近行为，特别关注包含多个孤立子的可能性。

Result: 证明了在3D径向情况下，不存在任何包含两个或更多孤立子的全局解或II型爆破解，这意味着所有已知的孤立子分解实例都只包含至多一个孤立子。

Conclusion: 这一结果完成了对径向解渐近行为的完全分类，表明在3D径向能量临界波方程中，多孤立子结构在全局解和II型爆破解中不可能出现。

Abstract: In this work we consider the focusing, energy-critical wave equation in 3D radial case. It has been verified that any global or type II blow-up solution decomposes into a superposition of several decoupled grounds states, a free wave and a small error, as time tends to infinity or the blow-up time. This is usually called soliton resolution. However, all known examples of soliton resolution in the 3D radial case come with no more than one soliton. In this work we prove the nonexistence of any global or type II blow up solution with two or more solitons, thus give a complete classification of asymptotic behaviours of radial solutions.

### [77] [Inverse Spectral Analysis of Singular Radial AKNS Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21961)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于两个不同有效角动量参数κ的谱数据方法，研究奇异AKNS算子的局部逆谱问题。对特定参数对(κ₁,κ₂)进行分析，包括(0,1)、(1,2)、(0,3)和(0,2)。

Result: 对于参数对(0,1)、(1,2)和(0,3)，证明了局部唯一性（local uniqueness）。对于(0,2)情况，证明了谱映射在原点处的Fréchet微分（Fréchet differential）是单射（injective），但其值域是否闭（closed）的问题仍然开放。

Conclusion: 该研究在奇异AKNS算子的逆谱问题中取得了部分进展，对特定参数对建立了局部唯一性结果，但对(0,2)情况的Fréchet微分值域闭性问题仍需进一步研究。

Abstract: We study an inverse spectral problem for singular AKNS operators based on
  spectral data associated with two distinct values of the effective angular momentum
  parameter $κ\,$.
  Our main focus is the local inverse problem near the zero potential.
  For the pairs $(κ_1,κ_2)=(0,1)$, $(1,2)$ and $(0,3)\,$, we establish local
  uniqueness.
  For $(0,2)\,$, we prove that the Fréchet differential of the spectral map
  at the origin is injective, while the question whether its range is closed
  remains open.

### [78] [Single-Trajectory Gibbs Sampling for Non-Commuting Observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21595)
*Hongrui Chen,Jiaqing Jiang,Bowen Li,Lexing Ying*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出两种非破坏性测量方案，将单轨迹吉布斯采样框架扩展至任意非对易可观测量，显著降低了量子多体系统热期望值的计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体系统热期望值估计是物理、化学和材料科学的核心挑战。现有单轨迹吉布斯采样方法主要局限于与哈密顿量对易的可观测量，限制了其应用范围。

Method: 提出两种测量构造方案：首先构建满足精确细致平衡条件的测量，确保系统在整个轨迹中保持平衡；其次在量子吉布斯采样器具有正谱隙的假设下，设计简化测量方案，使后选择态可作为快速重新混合的暖启动。

Result: 两种方案均能实现非破坏性测量，将重新采样成本与全局混合时间解耦，且自相关时间可能显著短于全局混合时间。两种测量方案均支持高效量子电路实现，仅需多对数哈密顿模拟时间。

Conclusion: 该工作从根本上将单轨迹框架扩展至任意非对易可观测量，通过消除样本间完全重新混合的需求，显著降低了量子多体系统热期望值估计的计算开销。

Abstract: Estimating thermal expectation values of quantum many-body systems is a central challenge in physics, chemistry, and materials science. Standard quantum Gibbs sampling protocols address this task by preparing the Gibbs state from scratch after every measurement, incurring a full mixing-time cost at each step. Recent advances in single-trajectory Gibbs sampling \cite{jiang2026} substantially reduce this overhead: once stationarity is reached, measurements can be collected along a single trajectory without re-thermalizing, provided the measurement channel preserves the Gibbs ensemble. However, explicit constructions of such non-destructive measurements have been limited primarily to observables that commute with the Hamiltonian. In this work, we fundamentally extend the single-trajectory framework to arbitrary, non-commuting observables. We provide two measurement constructions that extract measurement information without fully destroying the Gibbs state, thereby eliminating the need for full re-mixing between samples.
  First, we construct a measurement that satisfies exact detailed balance. This ensures the system remains in equilibrium throughout the trajectory, allowing measurement outcomes to decorrelate in an autocorrelation time that could be significantly shorter than the global mixing time. Second, assuming the underlying quantum Gibbs sampler has a positive spectral gap, we design a simplified measurement scheme that ensures the post-selected state serves as a warm start for rapid re-mixing. This approach successfully decouples the resampling cost from the global mixing time. Both measurement schemes admit efficient quantum circuit implementations, requiring only polylogarithmic Hamiltonian simulation time.

</details>


### [79] [A generalized Coulomb problem for a spin-1/2 fermion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21839)
*V. B. Mendrot,A. S. de Castro,P. Alberto*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了3+1维狄拉克方程在标量、矢量和张量相互作用组合下的精确束缚态解，所有相互作用均通过中心库仑势描述。通过选择合适的径向函数Ansätze系数，得到了以广义拉盖尔多项式表示的波函数，并确定了精确能谱及其对势参数的依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索狄拉克方程在标量、矢量和张量相互作用组合下的精确解问题，特别是当这些相互作用均通过中心库仑势描述时。该研究旨在为这一广义库仑问题提供精确的束缚态解，并建立平面问题与球对称问题之间的映射关系。

Method: 方法包括利用径向函数Ansätze系数的选择自由度，推导出以广义拉盖尔多项式（generalized Laguerre polynomials）表示的波函数。通过量子化条件确定精确能谱，并分析能谱对势参数的依赖性。同时建立了平面问题与球对称库仑问题之间的直接映射关系。

Result: 获得了广义库仑问题的精确束缚态解，包括波函数和能谱的解析表达式。证明了该解能够涵盖文献中已有的多个特例解，并推导了两个新的特例：通过库仑加常数张量势实现的旋量和赝旋量对称性破缺，以及标量加张量库仑势问题。

Conclusion: 本文成功解决了3+1维狄拉克方程在标量、矢量和张量相互作用组合下的广义库仑问题，获得了精确的束缚态解。通过建立平面问题与球对称问题的映射关系，为球对称库仑问题提供了解决方案，并扩展了现有文献中的特例分析。

Abstract: We study the Dirac equation in 3+1 dimensions with a general combination of scalar, vector and tensor interactions with arbitrary strengths, all of them described by central Coulomb potentials acting on a particular plane of motion. For the tensor coupling a constant term is also included, since this gives rise to an effective Coulomb potential, which is necessary for the formation of bound states in a pure tensor coupling configuration. The exact bound-state solutions for this generalized Coulomb problem are computed by exploiting the freedom in choosing the coefficients of the \textit{Ansätze} for the radial functions, which leads to wave functions in terms of generalized Laguerre polynomials. From the quantization condition, the exact energy spectrum is also determined and its dependence on the parameters of the potentials is discussed. We show that similar features of the equations for the problem in the plane and the spherically symmetric problem allow a simple and direct mapping between them, thereby providing the solution to the spherical Coulomb problem. Our results are validated by showing that the solutions correctly encompass several previous solutions available in the literature for particular cases of this problem, for which we further develop the analysis of the parameters. We also derive two new particular cases not yet reported in the literature: the case of breaking of spin and pseudospin symmetries by the addition of a Coulomb plus constant tensor potential and the problem of a scalar plus tensor Coulomb potentials.

</details>


### [80] [Non-Hermiticity induced thermal entanglement phase transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21968)
*Bikashkali Midya*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明，在无外磁场条件下，具有非对称海森堡XY相互作用的典型双量子比特有效非厄米系统，能够仅通过非厄米性诱导最大二分纠缠和量子相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非厄米系统中量子纠缠和相变的独特性质，特别是研究非厄米性如何作为独立参数诱导最大纠缠和量子相变，区别于传统厄米系统。

Method: 理论分析一个原型双量子比特有效非厄米系统，该系统在无外磁场条件下具有非对称海森堡XY相互作用。采用奇异值分解广义密度矩阵（singular-value-decomposition generalized density matrix）计算双正交系统中的纠缠。

Result: 在热平衡T→0条件下，当非厄米参数γ大于临界值γ_c=J√(1-δ²)时，系统达到最大纠缠C=1；当γ<γ_c时，纠缠非最大且由C=√(1-(γ/J)²)给出。纠缠在γ=γ_c处发生不连续跃迁至零。

Conclusion: 该相变源于非厄米性驱动的基态简并处的能隙闭合，这从根本上区别于例外点（exceptional point）。研究建议使用奇异值分解广义密度矩阵计算双正交系统中的纠缠。

Abstract: Theoretical analysis of a prototypical two-qubit effective non-Hermitian system characterized by asymmetric Heisenberg $XY$ interactions in the absence of external magnetic fields demonstrates that maximal bipartite entanglement and quantum phase transitions can be induced exclusively through non-Hermiticity. At thermal equilibrium as $T\rightarrow 0$, the system attains maximal entanglement ${C}=1$ for values of the non-Hermiticity parameter greater than a critical value $γ>γ_c=J\sqrt{(1-δ^2)}$, where $J$ denotes the exchange interaction and $δ$ represents the anisotropy of the system; conversely, for $γ< γ_c$, entanglement is nonmaximal and given by ${C} = \sqrt{(1 - (γ/J)^2)}$. The entanglement undergoes a discontinuous transition to zero precisely at $γ= γ_c$. This phase transition originates from the closing of the energy gap at a non-Hermiticity-driven ground state degeneracy, which is fundamentally different from an exceptional point. This work suggests the use of singular-value-decomposition generalized density matrix for the computation of entanglement in bi-orthogonal systems.

Abstract: Low-dimensional materials exhibit exotic properties due to enhanced quantum fluctuations, making the understanding of their microscopic origin central in condensed matter physics. Analogue quantum simulators offer a powerful approach for investigating these systems at the microscopic level, particularly in large-scale regimes where quantum entanglement limits classical numerical methods. To date, analogue simulators have largely focused on universal Hamiltonians rather than material-specific quantitative comparisons. Here we use a Rydberg-based quantum simulator to study the bulk-layered frustrated quantum magnet TmMgGaO$_4$. ### [82] [Noise-induced contraction of MPO truncation errors in noisy random circuits and Lindbladian dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20400)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法包括模拟两种设置：(1) 一维Haar随机电路在退极化噪声（depolarizing noise）或振幅阻尼噪声（amplitude-damping noise）下的演化；(2) 一维Lindblad动力学中非可积量子伊辛模型（non-integrable quantum Ising model）在相同噪声类型下的演化。通过分析系统密度矩阵的平均纯度（average purity）弛豫和截断误差收缩行为来研究MPO模拟效率。

Result: 研究结果显示，系统密度矩阵的平均纯度在时间尺度上与噪声率成反比地弛豫到稳态值。截断误差在系统尺寸N和演化时间t上均呈指数收缩，因为含噪声动力学将不同密度矩阵映射向同一稳态。这为L1截断误差提供了比现有界限在N上指数级更紧的经验界限。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，MPO模拟算法可能高效地从任意深度的1D含噪声随机电路输出中采样，并能有效模拟1D Lindblad动力学的稳态。这些结果为含噪声量子系统的MPO模拟效率提供了经验证据。

Abstract: We study how matrix-product-operator (MPO) truncation errors evolve when simulating two setups: (1) 1D Haar-random circuits under either depolarizing noise or amplitude-damping noise, and (2) 1D Lindbladian dynamics of a non-integrable quantum Ising model under either depolarizing or amplitude-damping noise. We first show that the average purity of the system density matrix relaxes to a steady value on a timescale that scales inversely with the noise rate. We then show that truncation errors contract exponentially in both system size $N$ and the evolution time $t$, as the noisy dynamics maps different density matrices toward the same steady state. This yields an empirical bound on the $L_1$ truncation error that is exponentially tighter in $N$ than the existing bound. Together, these results provide empirical evidence that MPO simulation algorithms may efficiently sample from the output of 1D noisy random circuits [setup (1)] at arbitrary circuit depth, and from the steady state of 1D Lindbladian dynamics [setup (2)].

### [83] [The typicality of symmetry-induced entanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20786)
*Christian Boudreault,Nicolas Levasseur*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在全局守恒电荷约束下的对称可分性问题（SSP），发现大多数对称可分态实际上远离对称可分性，并探讨了其在超选择规则或无共同参考系量子任务中的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在存在全局守恒电荷 $N$ 的情况下，需要探究给定可分态是否能分解为电荷守恒的分量，这一问题被定义为对称可分性问题（Symmetric Separability Problem, SSP）。研究旨在理解对称可分性在随机态中的普遍性及其在量子信息处理中的意义。

Method: 使用数纠缠（number entanglement, NE）作为对称可分性失败的见证量，该概念源自arXiv:2110.09388。通过分析随机态中NE的高斯集中现象，研究对称可分性的统计特性。

Result: 对于几乎所有的 $N$，随机态上的SSP以概率一被否定回答。大多数对称可分态实际上远离对称可分性，NE呈现围绕严格正平均值的Gaussian concentration现象。

Conclusion: 研究结果对存在超选择规则（superselection rule）或缺乏共同参考系的量子任务具有重要影响。论文在$N$约束下的可分空间大小问题上取得进展，并触及了SSP复杂性和多体纠缠（multiparty entanglement）问题。

Abstract: In the presence of a globally conserved charge $N$, a natural question is whether a given separable state can be separated into charge-conserving components. We dub this problem the Symmetric Separability Problem (SSP). On random states, the SSP is answered negatively with probability one for almost all $N$. Using a witness to the failure of symmetric separability, namely the number entanglement (NE) introduced in arXiv:2110.09388, we show that most symmetric and separable states are actually far from being symmetrically separable, with the NE featuring Gaussian concentration around a strictly positive mean value. We discuss some consequences of our results for quantum tasks in the presence of a superselection rule or in the absence of a common reference frame. Progress is made on the question of the size of the separable space constrained by $N$. We also touch upon the question of the complexity of SSP, and multiparty entanglement.

### [84] [Robust Quantum Sensing via Prethermal Spin Orbits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21057)
*Enrico Daniel Richter,Ryan J. Smith,Brayden Glockzin,Emanuel Druga,Thomas Schenkel,Ashok Ajoy*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于相互作用保护的磁力测量方案，通过周期性驱动将集体磁化导向两个长寿命的Floquet预热"轨道"轴，实现对目标磁场的高灵敏度测量，同时强烈抑制背景场和环境扰动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子传感器的实际性能常受环境漂移（偏置场不稳定、温度波动、机械振动）、背景场和不完美控制脉冲的限制。这促使开发能够内在补偿此类扰动、同时保持对目标场高灵敏度的物理机制。

Method: 引入相互作用保护的磁力测量方案，其中周期性驱动将集体磁化导向两个长寿命的预热Floquet"轨道"轴，这些轴在Bloch球上充分分离。通过在轴间快速切换，将目标场编码为差分信号，而背景场表现为被强烈抑制的共模运动。

Result: 该方案实现了>1000倍的背景场抑制，同时消除了预热瞬态，能够在无需预测滤波或频谱调谐的情况下准确重建快速变化的音频带磁信号。实验使用耦合核自旋的密集系综作为宽带（0-1 kHz）磁力计验证了原理。

Conclusion: Floquet预热化可作为鲁棒量子传感器的资源，结合了宽带磁场灵敏度与对多样环境和控制扰动的内在免疫性，为超越受控实验室条件的稳定量子计量学开辟了道路。

Abstract: Practical performance of quantum sensors is often curtailed by uncontrolled environmental drift (bias-field instability, temperature fluctuations, mechanical vibration), background fields, and imperfect control pulses. This motivates developing physical mechanisms that intrinsically compensate for such perturbations while retaining high sensitivity to target fields. We introduce an interaction-protected magnetometry scheme where periodic driving steers the collective magnetization onto two long-lived, prethermal Floquet "orbit" axes well-separated on the Bloch sphere. Rapid toggling between these axes encodes target fields as a differential signal, whereas background fields appear as common-mode motion that is strongly rejected, achieving >1000-fold suppression while canceling prethermal transients. This enables accurate reconstruction of rapidly varying audio-band magnetic signals without predictive filtering or spectral tuning. We provide an experimental proof-of-principle using a dense ensemble of coupled nuclear spins, operated here as a broadband (0-1 kHz) magnetometer. The protocol is remarkably tolerant to imperfections, operating robustly across millions of pulses under pulse-angle (~10°) and pulse frequency (>1 kHz) errors, large bias-field drifts (>50 $\mathrmμ$T), temperature variations over 150 K, and harsh mechanical vibrations. These results establish Floquet prethermalization as a resource for robust quantum sensors that combines broadband magnetic-field sensitivity with intrinsic immunity to diverse environmental and control perturbations, opening a path toward stable quantum metrology beyond controlled laboratory conditions.

</details>


### [85] [A Refined Biorthogonal Framework for Non-Hermitian Quantum Theory and Its Application in Dynamical Phase Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21281)
*Fei Wang,Guoying Liang,Zecheng Zhao,Bao-Ming Xu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种非厄米（non-Hermitian）量子理论的统一框架，通过修正双正交（biorthogonal）表述，解决了该领域长期存在的理论争议。该框架在厄米极限下可自然回归标准量子力学，并应用于分析一维SSH模型中的动力学相变（dynamical phase transition），发现了无法用绕数（winding number）表征的新相变类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米系统中状态和动力学的描述与理论框架的选择密切相关，这是该领域持续争议的焦点。本研究旨在解决这一争议，建立一个统一的理论理解。

Method: 基于一个物理假设：非厄米系统的左矢和右矢动力学都必须满足薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）。在此假设基础上，作者修正了双正交框架（biorthogonal framework），提出了非厄米量子理论的一致重述。

Result: 修正后的框架在厄米极限下可自然回归标准量子力学。应用于一维Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型时，该框架将厄米两带系统中的相变条件$\mathbf{d}_{k}^i\cdot\mathbf{d}_{k}^f=0$推广到非厄米情况：$\mathrm{Re}\Bigl[\frac{\mathbf{d}_{k}^i}{d_{k}^i}\cdot\frac{\mathbf{d}_{k}^f}{d_{k}^f}\Bigr]=0$。更重要的是，发现了无法用绕数（winding number）表征的全新动力学相变类型。

Conclusion: 提出的修正框架为研究非厄米系统提供了统一的理论基础，有望在该领域获得广泛应用。该框架不仅解决了现有争议，还揭示了传统绕数表征无法捕捉的新相变现象。

Abstract: The description of states and dynamics in non-Hermitian systems is fundamentally linked to the choice of an appropriate theoretical framework--a point of ongoing debate in the field. This work addresses this issue by proposing a consistent formulation that reconciles existing controversies and establishes a unified theoretical understanding. Our approach rests on a foundational premise: The dynamics of both left- and right-vectors of a non-Hermitian system must satisfy the Schrödinger equation. Building on this physically motivated assumption, we refine the biorthogonal framework, leading to a consistent reformulation of non-Hermitian quantum theory. This refined framework can naturally reduce to standard quantum mechanics in the Hermitian limit. As a concrete application, we analyze the dynamical phase transition in a one-dimensional Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model within this refined framework. Notably, our formulation naturally generalizes the known condition for such transitions in Hermitian two-band systems, namely, $\mathbf{d}_{k}^i\cdot\mathbf{d}_{k}^f=0$, to the non-Hermitian case, where it takes the form $\mathrm{Re}\Bigl[\frac{\mathbf{d}_{k}^i}{d_{k}^i}\cdot\frac{\mathbf{d}_{k}^f}{d_{k}^f}\Bigr]=0$. Furthermore, we identify entirely new dynamical phase transitions that cannot be characterized by the winding number. We hope that this refined framework will find broad applications in the study of non-Hermitian systems.

### [86] [Enhanced Emission from Boron-Vacancy Center in Rhombohedral Boron Nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21422)
*Nasrin Estaji,Ismaeil Abdolhosseini Sarsari,Gergő Thiering,Adam Gali*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理计算发现，菱形堆叠氮化硼（rBN）中带负电硼空位中心（V_B^-）的亮度比六方氮化硼（hBN）提高至少一个数量级，同时保持或改善自旋特性，为室温单自旋量子传感应用提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维氮化硼（2D BN）蜂窝晶格的不同堆叠组合能显著改变其性质，但如何通过堆叠工程优化量子缺陷特性尚需探索。研究旨在探索不同堆叠结构对硼空位中心（V_B^-）发光和自旋性能的影响。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）比较菱形氮化硼（rhombohedral BN, rBN）和六方氮化硼（hexagonal BN, hBN）中带负电硼空位中心（V_B^-）的性质。分析重点包括晶体场对称性降低对缺陷性能的影响。

Result: rBN中V_B^-中心的亮度比hBN中提高至少一个数量级，而自旋特性保持相当甚至有所改善。这种增强源于rBN中晶体场对称性的降低，使得室温下单自旋相干控制（single-spin coherent control）在rBN中成为可能。

Conclusion: BN层的工程化堆叠（engineered stacking）为定制嵌入量子缺陷（embedded quantum defects）性质提供了有效手段。rBN中的V_B^-中心可作为单自旋量子传感器（single-spin quantum sensor）在二维宿主材料中应用。

Abstract: Various stacking combinations of the two-dimensional (2D) boron nitride (BN) honeycomb lattice can significantly modify the properties of the resulting 2D BN crystal. Here, we demonstrate through first-principles calculations that the brightness of the negatively charged boron-vacancy center (V$_\text{B}^{-}$) is enhanced by at least one order of magnitude in rhombohedral BN (rBN) compared to hexagonal BN (hBN), while the spin properties remain either comparable or even improved. This enhancement arises from the reduced symmetry of the crystal field in rBN. Our results suggest that room-temperature single-spin coherent control of V$_\text{B}^{-}$ is feasible in rBN, enabling its application as a single-spin quantum sensor in this 2D host. These findings demonstrate that engineered stacking of BN layers provides a powerful means to tailor the properties of embedded quantum defects.

</details>


### [87] [Resonance-Suppression Principle for Prethermalization beyond Periodic Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21540)
*Jian Xian Sim*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个共振抑制原理，用于解释非周期驱动量子多体系统中的慢加热现象，揭示了驱动频谱的算术结构如何通过抑制多光子共振来延长预热寿命。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡态量子多体系统在强快速驱动下的动力学行为，在非周期驱动情况下缺乏统一理解。与周期驱动（Floquet预热化）中加热速率随驱动频率指数级减慢不同，非周期驱动表现出不同的加热标度规律，需要建立统一原理来解释这些现象。

Method: 研究通过识别共振抑制原理来分析预热寿命τ*的控制机制。该方法区分了单光子抑制（由驱动傅里叶变换在低频的抑制律f(Ω)量化）和多光子抑制（要求嵌套对易子在特定算术结构下保持可控）。采用迭代旋转框架方案中的小除数机制来推导τ*的标度规律。

Result: 研究发现，当多光子抑制成立时，预热寿命τ*随驱动速度λ的标度由低频抑制律f(Ω)控制。通过准Floquet驱动的案例研究，展示了多光子抑制失效时线性响应和非微扰理论中τ*标度的分离。该原理能够解释文献中关于非周期驱动的不一致性。

Conclusion: 共振抑制原理为理解非周期驱动中的慢加热现象提供了统一框架，并可用于设计可编程量子模拟器中的预热物质相。研究提出了具有可调τ*的新型非周期"阶乘"驱动作为应用示例，为工程化预热相提供了设计原则。

Abstract: Non-equilibrium dynamics of strongly and rapidly driven quantum many-body systems is poorly understood beyond periodic driving, where heating is exponentially slow in the drive frequency (Floquet Prethermalization). In contrast, non-periodic drives were found to exhibit widely different heating scalings with no unifying principle. This work identifies a resonance-suppression principle governing slow heating up to a prethermal lifetime $τ_*$: When the drive's spectral arithmetic structure restricts multiphoton resonances, $τ_*$ is controlled by low-frequency spectral suppression. The principle distinguishes (i) Single-photon suppression, quantified by a low-frequency suppression law $f(Ω)$ for the drive's Fourier Transform weight near $Ω=0$, from (ii) Multi-photon suppression, where nested commutators remain controlled if exceptional arithmetic structure satisfies a subadditive property. Remarkably, if multi-photon suppression holds, $τ_*$ scaling with drive speed $λ$ is governed by $f(Ω)$. This law of $τ_*$ is found through a small-divisor mechanism in this work's iterative rotating frame scheme. Multi-photon suppression breakdown separates $λ$-scaling of $τ_*$ in linear response and non-perturbative theory, shown by a case study of Quasi-Floquet driving. The principle is applied to (i) Resolve inconsistencies in literature on non-periodic driving, and (ii) Provide design principles for engineering prethermal phases of matter in programmable quantum simulators, exemplified by new non-periodic `Factorial' drives with tunable $τ_*$.

</details>


### [88] [Non-Markovian renormalization of optomechanical exceptional points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22130)
*Aritra Ghosh,M. Bhattacharya*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了非马尔可夫机械耗散对红边带驱动线性化光机械系统中异常点的影响，揭示了结构化环境会改变模式合并位置，且忽略这种记忆效应会显著抑制Petermann因子发散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解非马尔可夫机械耗散如何影响光机械系统中的异常点，特别是在结构化机械环境中，传统马尔可夫预测可能不准确，这对于基于异常点的器件设计至关重要。

Method: 采用伪模映射方法，针对选定的非欧姆机械浴，推导了记忆重整化异常点的解析条件，从而分析结构化环境对模式合并位置的影响。

Result: 研究发现结构化环境会将模式合并位置从马尔可夫预测处位移，忽略这种记忆诱导的位移会使Petermann因子的发散程度被抑制数个数量级。此外，非马尔可夫性会改变腔反射谱，表现为更浅的光机械诱导透明凹陷。

Conclusion: 当储层诱导的记忆效应不可忽略时，准确的浴模型对于基于异常点的器件成功运行至关重要。光机械诱导透明凹陷的变浅提供了结构化机械环境的实验可观测特征。

Abstract: We investigate how non-Markovian mechanical dissipation affects exceptional points in linearized optomechanical systems with red-sideband drive. For a chosen non-Ohmic mechanical bath, we derive analytical conditions for the memory-renormalized exceptional point by employing a pseudomode mapping, thereby demonstrating that structured environments displace the mode coalescence away from the Markovian prediction. Crucially, we reveal that failing to account for this memory-induced shift suppresses the divergent Petermann factor by orders of magnitude, showing that accurate bath modeling is essential for the successful operation of exceptional-point-based devices whenever reservoir-induced memory is non-negligible. We finally show that non-Markovianity modifies the cavity reflection spectrum, manifesting as a shallower optomechanically-induced-transparency dip, providing therefore an experimentally-accessible signature of structured mechanical environments.

</details>


### [89] [Precision's arrow of time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22284)
*Luis E. F. Foa Torres,G. Pappas,V. Achilleos,D. Bautista Avilés*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新的时间箭头机制——精度诱导不可逆性（Precision-Induced Irreversibility），该机制不需要环境纠缠或非线性动力学，仅通过放大、非正规性和有限动态范围三个要素的相互作用即可产生操作性的时间箭头。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上时间箭头通常归因于环境纠缠导致的退相干和非线性动力学导致的混沌两种机制。本文旨在探索第三种不需要这些条件的途径，揭示形式可逆性与物理可逆性之间的差异。

Method: 通过分析非厄米演化（non-Hermitian evolution）中放大、非正规性（non-normality）和有限动态范围（finite dynamic range）三个要素的相互作用。采用回声保真度测试（echo-fidelity tests）在任意精度计算和硬件上验证这种转变。

Result: 研究发现存在一个尖锐的时间可预测性界限（temporal predictability horizon），该界限与可用精度呈线性比例关系。超过此界限后，不同的状态会坍缩到相同的表示上，导致形式可逆性与物理可逆性发生分离。

Conclusion: 精度诱导不可逆性为时间箭头提供了第三条路径，仅需三个基本要素的相互作用即可产生操作性的时间方向性。移除其中任何一个要素都可能恢复可逆性，揭示了量子演化中形式性质与物理可实现性之间的根本差异。

Abstract: The arrow of time is usually attributed to two mechanisms: decoherence through environmental entanglement, and chaos through nonlinear dynamics. Here we demonstrate a third route, Precision-Induced Irreversibility (PIR), requiring neither. No entanglement. No nonlinearity. Just three ingredients: amplification, non-normality, and finite dynamic range, whose interplay yields an operational arrow of time; remove any one and reversibility can be restored. Non-Hermitian evolution remains mathematically invertible, yet beyond a sharp temporal predictability horizon scaling linearly with available precision, distinct states collapse onto identical representations. Echo-fidelity tests confirm this transition across arbitrary-precision calculations and hardware, revealing where formal invertibility and physical reversibility diverge.

</details>

Abstract: This document presents an overview of the design, implementation, and expected performance of the Advanced Virgo Plus (AdV+) upgrades in view of the O5 observing run. Following the experience gained during the O4 commissioning and operations, the Virgo Collaboration has revised the upgrade strategy to address limitations associated with marginally stable recycling cavities. The O5 upgrade program combines elements from the original AdV+ Phase II project with new design solutions, including the implementation of stable recycling cavities, a major modification to the central interferometer layout, and a comprehensive renewal of critical subsystems. The planned upgrades are organized in two steps, targeting progressive improvements in operational stability, noise reduction, and detector sensitivity. Key developments include new vacuum infrastructures, suspensions, mirrors, optical configurations, quantum noise reduction systems, and high-power laser technologies. The resulting configuration is expected to significantly enhance the interferometer performance, enabling a substantial increase in astrophysical reach and scientific return during O5.

# math.PR [[Back]](#toc)

### [91] [A positive formula for volumes of moduli spaces of flat unitary connections on compact surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20517)
*Quentin François,David García-Zelada,Thierry Lévy,Pierre Tarrago*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文为穿孔紧致定向曲面上的U(n)值平坦联络模空间体积提供了显式的正表达式，通过求和描述多边形上彩色蜂巢结构的多面体体积获得，并推导出U(n)值Yang-Mills测度边际的正公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究穿孔紧致定向曲面上U(n)值平坦联络模空间的体积计算问题，旨在获得显式的正表达式，这与Knutson和 Tao描述两个厄米矩阵和谱的工作精神一致。

Method: 通过求和描述多边形上彩色蜂巢（colored honeycombs）的显式多面体（explicit polytopes）体积来计算模空间体积，借鉴了Knutson和Tao处理厄米矩阵谱问题的方法论。

Result: 获得了模空间体积的显式正表达式，并作为推论，为紧致定向曲面上U(n)值Yang-Mills测度的边际（marginals）提供了基于显式路径过程概率分布的正公式。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了穿孔曲面上U(n)平坦联络模空间体积与多边形上彩色蜂巢多面体体积之间的显式对应关系，为Yang-Mills测度的边际分布提供了新的计算方法。

Abstract: We provide a manifestly positive expression for the volume of the moduli spaces of flat $\mathrm{U}(n)$-valued connections on punctured compact oriented surfaces. This volume is obtained by summing volumes of explicit polytopes describing coloured honeycombs on a polygon, in the spirit of the work of Knutson and Tao describing the spectrum of the sum of two hermitian matrices. As a corollary, we also provide a positive formula for marginals of the $\mathrm{U}(n)$-valued Yang-Mills measure on a compact oriented surface in terms of the probability distribution of an explicit path process.

</details>


### [92] [Restriction and mixing properties of interacting particle systems with unbounded range](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21817)
*Benedikt Jahnel,Jonas Köppl*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文研究了无限图上具有无界相互作用范围的相互作用粒子系统，证明了有限粒子系统近似无限体积动力学的显式非渐近误差界，并提供了空间关联衰减的定量界限，应用于证明一维格点上指数衰减的相互作用系统不会自发破坏时间平移对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究无限图上具有无界相互作用范围（unbounded interaction range）的相互作用粒子系统（interacting particle systems），旨在建立有限系统近似无限体积动力学的严格误差分析，并探讨此类系统的对称性保持特性。

Method: 在一般可数无限图（countably infinite graphs）上，通过证明显式非渐近误差界（explicit non-asymptotic error bounds）来近似无限体积动力学，同时提供空间关联衰减（spatial decay of correlations）在时间t>0时的非渐近定量界限。

Result: 获得了有限粒子系统近似无限体积动力学的显式误差界，并证明了在$\mathbb{Z}$上相互作用强度指数衰减（decays exponentially fast）的系统不会自发破坏时间平移对称性（time-translation symmetry），无论是强意义还是弱意义上。

Conclusion: 相互作用粒子系统在指数衰减相互作用下具有对称性保持特性，有限系统近似无限体积动力学的误差可被严格量化，这为研究无限系统的动力学行为提供了数学基础。

Abstract: We consider interacting particle systems with unbounded interaction range on general countably infinite graphs $S$ and prove explicit non-asymptotic error bounds for approximations of the infinite-volume dynamics by systems of finitely many interacting particles. Moreover, we also provide non-asymptotic quantitative bounds on the spatial decay of correlations at times $t>0$ and then apply these results to show that interacting particle systems on $\mathbb{Z}$ whose interaction strengths decays exponentially fast cannot spontaneously break the time-translation symmetry, neither in the strong, nor in the weak sense.

### [93] [Exact center symmetry and first-order phase transition in QCD with three degenerate dynamical quarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22046)
*Gergely Endrodi,Guy D. Moore,Adam Pieczynski,Alessandro Sciarra*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索强相互作用基本相图的一个特定区域，特别是虚同位旋化学势条件下的QCD行为，以阐明手征对称性破缺与解禁闭之间的关系。

Method: 采用第一性原理晶格模拟方法，使用stout-smeared rooted staggered夸克在单一晶格间距下进行模拟。通过专用的多直方图方法分析Polyakov loop分布的有限尺寸标度行为。

Result: 在特定虚同位旋化学势条件下，三味夸克QCD表现出精确的中心对称性，该对称性在低温下保持完整，在高温下自发破缺。通过分析Polyakov loop分布的有限尺寸标度，证实了存在一级解禁闭相变。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了强相互作用基本相图中质量-同位旋化学势平面上的QCD行为，为理解手征对称性破缺与解禁闭之间的关系提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We study QCD with three degenerate flavors of dynamical quarks using first-principles lattice simulations. For a specific choice of imaginary isospin chemical potential, this theory possesses an exact center symmetry, just like pure gauge theory. This exact symmetry is expected to be intact at low temperatures and spontaneously broken in the high-temperature regime. By analyzing the finite-size scaling of the Polyakov loop distribution, obtained with a dedicated multi-histogram approach, we demonstrate that there is a first-order deconfinement phase transition in between. Our results are obtained employing stout-smeared rooted staggered quarks at one lattice spacing. Using simulations at different quark masses we sketch the behavior of QCD in the mass-isospin chemical potential plane, shedding new light on this corner of the fundamental phase diagram of the strong interactions and the relationship between chiral symmetry breaking and deconfinement.

### [94] [Broad presence of ferromagnetism in bees and relationship to phylogeny, natural history, and sociality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20312)
*Laura Russo,Caleb Allen,Cameron S. Jorgensen,Lizabeth Quigley,C. Charlotte Buchanan,Michael Winklhofer,Seán G. Brady,Laurence Packer,Anne Murray,Dustin A. Gilbert*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 该研究首次系统性地揭示了基于铁磁性颗粒（ferromagnetic particles）的磁感受能力在多种蜜蜂物种中广泛存在，且与物种特征和自然历史相关，但缺乏系统发育信号（phylogenetic signal）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已知磁感受（magnetoreception）在真社会性昆虫如蜜蜂中与通讯和觅食相关，但其系统发育模式、与物种特征及自然历史的关系仍不清楚。研究旨在探索磁感受在蜜蜂多样性中的分布规律。

Method: 研究测试了96种蜜蜂物种，检测基于铁磁性颗粒的推定磁感受能力，并分析其与系统发育、物种特征（如体型大小、社会行为）的关系。

Result: 在测试的96种蜜蜂中，72种检测到推定磁感受能力，表明该能力在蜜蜂中广泛存在但缺乏系统发育信号。磁信号强度在种内和种间存在变异，且随体型增大和社会行为增强而增加。

Conclusion: 基于铁磁性颗粒的磁感受能力在蜜蜂进化前就已存在，其分布广泛但缺乏系统发育保守性，磁信号强度与体型大小和社会行为等生态特征相关。

Abstract: Scientists have long been fascinated by magnetoreception, the innate capacity of many animals to sense and use the Earth's magnetic field for navigation. In eusocial insects like honey bees, magnetoreception has been linked to communication and foraging. However, little is known about magnetoreception's phylogenetic patterns and relationship to species traits and natural history. Here, we demonstrate that putative magnetoreception based on ferromagnetic particles is widespread across a diversity of bee species (72 out of 96 species tested), with no phylogenetic signal. We also detected such putative magnetoreception in non-bee outgroups, suggesting this magnetic capacity predates the evolution of the Anthophila. While magnetic signals were found across a diversity of life history traits, the strength of the magnetic signal varied within and between species, and increased with body size and social behavior.

### [95] [Missing-mass search in forward-proton-tagged dilepton events with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20837)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上利用质子-质子碰撞，通过光子诱导过程寻找衰变为同味带电轻子对（电子或μ子）的可观测粒子V及其不可观测组分X。通过ATLAS前向质子谱仪和中心探测器重建完整四动量，在100-900 GeV缺失质量谱中搜索窄共振，未发现显著超出标准模型预期的信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过光子诱导过程（photon-induced process）在质子-质子碰撞中寻找超出标准模型（Beyond Standard Model, BSM）的新物理。特别关注可观测粒子V衰变为同味带电轻子对（same-flavour charged leptons）并伴随不可观测组分X的信号，该方法具有模型无关性（model-independent）。

Method: 利用ATLAS前向质子谱仪（forward proton spectrometer）测量出射质子能量，重建完整光子-光子四动量（four-momentum）。通过减去ATLAS探测器测量的中心系统可见四动量，重建"缺失质量"（missing mass），从而无需了解X的性质即可重建不可观测组分。在100-900 GeV缺失质量谱中搜索窄共振（narrow resonance）。

Result: 在13 TeV质心能量、14.7 fb⁻¹积分亮度的质子-质子碰撞数据中，未观察到显著超出标准模型预期的信号。对三种不同信号模型设置了95%置信水平（confidence level）的基准截面（fiducial cross sections）上限，范围为128-2.5 fb。同时为BSM过程设置了模型无关的可见截面（visible cross section）上限。

Conclusion: 研究未发现超出标准模型预期的显著信号，为光子诱导过程中产生可观测粒子V及其不可观测组分X的BSM过程设置了严格的截面上限。该方法展示了利用缺失质量重建实现模型无关搜索的有效性，为未来类似搜索提供了基准。

Abstract: A search is conducted in proton-proton collisions at the Large Hadron Collider for photon-induced production $pp\rightarrow pp+ γγ, (γγ\rightarrow VX)$ of a visible particle $V$ decaying into a pair of same-flavour charged leptons ($e^+e^-$ or $μ^+μ^-$) and an undetected invisible component $X$. Measurements of the outgoing proton energies by the ATLAS forward proton spectrometer allow the full photon-photon four-momentum to be reconstructed. By subtracting the visible four-momentum of the central system measured with the ATLAS detector, the 'missing mass' of any event components not detected in the central region can be reconstructed, enabling the reconstruction of $X$ without knowing its properties, thus allowing the search to be model-independent. A search for a narrow resonance is performed in the missing-mass spectrum between 100 GeV and 900 GeV. The analysis uses data collected in 2017 from proton-proton collisions at a centre-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s} =$ 13 TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 14.7 fb$^{-1}$. No significant excess over the Standard Model expectation is observed and upper limits at 95% confidence level are set on the fiducial cross sections for three different signal models in the range between 128 and 2.5 fb. Additionally, model-independent limits are set on the visible cross section of BSM processes, for two sets of selection criteria. Both individual lepton flavour decay channels of the visible boson and a combination of the two channels are considered.

The search is performed for $X$ mass in the range of 160$\unicode{x2013}$220 MeV/$c^2$. Three events were observed in the signal region, with two events near an $X$ mass of 177 MeV/$c^2$. Abstract: CERN's AD/ELENA ``antimatter factory'' - unique worldwide - serves several experiments, all of which use electromagnetic traps to accumulate antiprotons for fundamental science. GBAR has also pioneered an electrostatic scheme using a pulsed drift tube to decelerate the 100 keV antiproton beam, rather than slowing the antiprotons in a foil, as is commonly done in other experiments. Following first results producing a 6 keV antihydrogen beam directly after the decelerator, a trap has now been installed to increase the production rate. The emittance growth resulting from the deceleration is reduced in the trap by Coulomb interaction with a cold electron cloud. The antiproton cloud is further compressed using rotating wall cooling and can be re-accelerated up to energies of 10 keV, including a time focus. ### [99] [Study of the Run-3 muon flux at the SND@LHC experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21878)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Long-range muons produced in proton-proton collisions at the ATLAS interaction point constitute the primary background for neutrino interaction searches at the SND@LHC experiment. This work presents a comprehensive characterization of the muon flux throughout LHC Run-3, benchmarking Monte Carlo simulations against experimental measurements. Measured and simulated muon rates agree within 10-15% across all Run-3 configurations. Following the substantial background increase in 2024 as a result of a beam optics change, the reversion to nominal optics in 2025 did not restore the 2022-2023 levels due to the unprecedented adoption of horizontal crossing in ATLAS. As enlightened by simulation results, the latter enhanced the contribution of high-angle muons originating from diffractive proton losses in the LHC Dispersion Suppressor region. Their identification enabled the design of mitigation strategies that were experimentally validated. The simulation framework was also applied to the future High-Luminosity LHC configuration, resulting in a considerable muon rate rise, driven by both the planned luminosity increase and the enlarged magnet aperture. Nevertheless, the upgrade from emulsion films to silicon vertex detectors will preserve the efficiency of the experiment even in such a high-rate environment.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在验证DALI（Dark matter Axion Like-particle Interferometer）方法的可行性，通过缩比原型机进行暗物质搜索，为后续更大规模、更宽质量范围的探索提供技术验证。

Method: 采用低温（cryogenic）、磁化（magnetized）的缩比DALI原型机进行实验，分析了36小时的数据，在6.883-6.920 GHz频段搜索轴子类粒子信号。

Result: 数据分析未发现统计显著的轴子类粒子信号，在28.54 μeV处设定了轴子-光子耦合（axion-photon coupling）灵敏度上限g_{aγγ}≲1.27×10^{-11} GeV^{-1}的新排除极限。

Conclusion: 结果验证了DALI方法的可行性，为下一阶段使用升级仪器的晕轮探测器（haloscope）探索更宽质量范围提供了技术基础和研究动力。

Abstract: We report a pilot dark-matter search with a cryogenic, magnetized, scaled-down DALI prototype. An analysis of 36 hours of data reveals no statistically significant excess attributable to axionlike particles. We therefore set new exclusion limits in the 6.883--6.920 GHz band, reaching an axion-photon coupling sensitivity of $g_{aγγ}\lesssim 1.27\times10^{-11}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$ at 28.54 $μ$eV. These results consolidate the DALI approach and motivate a next-stage haloscope to explore a broader mass range with upgraded instrumentation.

### [101] [Search for low-mass vector and scalar resonances decaying into a quark-antiquark pair in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21965)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究在50-300 GeV质量范围内搜索衰变为夸克-反夸克对的新共振态，使用CMS实验在13 TeV质子-质子对撞中收集的数据，未发现显著信号，并设定了该质量范围内迄今最严格的耦合限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在搜索质量在50-300 GeV范围内、衰变为夸克-反夸克对的新共振态（resonances），以探索超出标准模型（Standard Model）的新物理现象。研究特别关注与硬初始态辐射（hard initial-state radiation）伴随产生的共振态，这有助于识别潜在的新粒子信号。

Method: 研究使用CMS实验在CERN大型强子对撞机（LHC）上收集的13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据，对应积分亮度为13 fb⁻¹。采用ParticleNet算法区分共振态衰变为底夸克对（bottom quark pairs）与轻夸克对的过程，并抑制背景。通过分析大半径喷注（large-radius jet）的双叉子结构（two-pronged substructure）和不变质量谱（invariant jet mass spectrum）来寻找峰值信号。

Result: 未观察到任何共振态存在的证据，在50-300 GeV质量范围内没有发现显著的峰值超出（peaking excesses）。研究设定了新标量（scalar）和矢量（vector）共振态与夸克耦合（couplings）的上限，这些限制在50-250 GeV质量范围内代表了迄今最严格的约束条件。

Conclusion: 该搜索未发现质量在50-300 GeV范围内衰变为夸克-反夸克对的新共振态证据。研究结果对超出标准模型的新物理参数空间提供了重要约束，特别是在50-250 GeV质量范围内设定了迄今最严格的耦合限制。

Abstract: A search for resonances with masses from 50 to 300 GeV decaying into a quark-antiquark pair is presented. The search uses proton-proton collision data at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV collected by the CMS experiment at the CERN LHC in 2016$-$2018, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 13 fb$^{-1}$. Two coupling scenarios are considered, with the resonances coupled either equally to all flavors of quarks or preferentially to bottom quarks. The search targets resonances produced in association with hard initial-state radiation, resulting in a large-radius jet with a two-pronged substructure. The ParticleNet algorithm is used to distinguish resonance decays to bottom quark pairs from lighter quark pairs and to suppress background processes. The invariant jet mass spectrum is scrutinized for peaking excesses over a falling background. No evidence for such resonances is observed. Limits are set on the couplings of new scalar and vector resonances to quarks, representing the most stringent limits to date in the mass range of 50$-$250 GeV.

Method: BESIII实验利用前所未有的数据集——超过10¹⁰个J/ψ事件和2.7×10⁹个ψ(2S)事件，显著提升了粲偶素弱衰变搜索的灵敏度。该方法聚焦于半轻子、非轻子和味改变中性流衰变通道的系统研究。

Result: BESIII实验在各种粲偶素弱衰变通道上建立了最新且最严格的上限，涵盖了半轻子、非轻子和味改变中性流衰变过程。这些结果为探测新物理效应提供了关键约束。

Conclusion: BESIII实验通过大规模数据集显著推进了粲偶素弱衰变的研究，为探索非微扰QCD动力学和超越标准模型的新物理提供了重要平台，特别是在味改变中性流衰变等高度压制的通道中。

Abstract: The weak decays of charmonium, involving $J/ψ$ and $ψ(2S)$ states, are instrumental in probing both non-perturbative QCD dynamics and flavor structure of the standard model~(SM). The extremely rare nature of charmonium weak decays makes them highly sensitive to new physics beyond the SM, particularly in channels heavily suppressed in the SM, such as flavor-changing neutral current~(FCNC) decays. This review highlights the critical role of the BESIII experiment, which leverages an unprecedented dataset of over $10^{10}$ $J/ψ$ events and $2.7\times10^{9}$ $ψ(2S)$ events to push the sensitivity of charmonium weak decay searches. We present the latest and most stringent upper limits established by BESIII on various semi-leptonic, non-leptonic, and FCNC charmonium weak decay channels.
