### [164] [Order in the interference of a long chain of Bose condensates with unrestricted phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20436)
*Vasiliy Makhalov,Andrey Turlapov*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究分析了周期性玻色凝聚体链在自由空间演化中的干涉效应，发现相位关系对干涉图案演化具有决定性影响：等相位时出现Talbot效应，随机相位时则产生不同的空间有序干涉图案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索周期性玻色凝聚体链在自由空间演化中的干涉行为，特别关注相邻及更远凝聚体之间相位差对后续演化和干涉图案的显著影响。

Method: 通过分析长周期性玻色凝聚体链在自由空间中的演化过程，研究比较了等相位条件和随机相关相位条件下的干涉行为差异。

Result: 研究发现：等相位时初始周期性密度分布会重现（Talbot效应）；随机相关相位时干涉中也会出现空间有序，但条纹演化与Talbot效应存在定性差异；即使小的相位无序也足以在长时间演化后定性改变干涉图案。

Conclusion: 该效应可用于测量相邻凝聚体之间的相干量以及沿链的相关长度，为研究玻色凝聚体系统的相位相干性提供了新的测量方法。

Abstract: For a long periodic chain of Bose condensates prepared in the free space, the subsequent evolution and interference dramatically depend on the difference between the phases of the adjacent and more distant condensates. If the phases are equal, the initial periodic density distribution reappears at later times, which is known as the Talbot effect. For randomly-related phases, we have found that a spatial order also appears in the interference, while the evolution of the fringes differs with the Talbot effect qualitatively. Even a small phase disorder is sufficient for qualitatively altering the interference, though maybe at long evolution times. This effect may be used for measuring the amount of coherence between adjacent condensates and the correlation length along the chain.

</details>


### [165] [Interference of a chain of Bose condensates in the Pitaevskii-Gross approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20439)
*I. N. Mosaki,A. V. Turlapov*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究分析了玻色凝聚体从光晶格释放后的自由膨胀和干涉现象，发现即使在相位涨落情况下，空间密度分布的频谱仍具有可重复性，并识别出两种不同类型的频谱峰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解玻色凝聚体从光学晶格（optical lattice）释放后的干涉行为，特别是相位涨落（phase fluctuations）对干涉条纹的影响以及空间密度分布频谱的特征。

Method: 在Pitaevskii-Gross方程的框架下计算凝聚体的干涉，并将计算结果与实验数据[Phys. Rev. Lett. 122, 090403 (2019)]进行比较。

Result: 计算成功再现了频谱峰的位置，包括其对粒子间相互作用（interparticle interaction）的依赖关系；然而在某些情况下，计算得到的峰高与实验观测值存在差异。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了相位涨落情况下干涉条纹的统计特性，识别出两种不同类型的频谱峰：一种源于相位涨落，另一种与凝聚体间的相干性（coherence）相关。

Abstract: A long chain of Bose condensates freely expands and interferes after being released from an optical lattice. The interference fringes are well resolved both in the case of equal phases of the condensates and in the case of fluctuating phases. In the second case the positions of the fringes also fluctuate. The spectrum of the spatial density distribution, however, is reproducible despite the fluctuations. Moreover two types of peaks are distinguishable in the spectrum. The first type arises due to the phase fluctuations, the second type is associated with the coherence between the condensates. In the framework of the Pitaevskii-Gross equation we calculate the interference of the condensates and compare the calculation with experiment [Phys. Rev. Lett. 122, 090403 (2019)]. The calculation reproduces the positions of the spectrum peaks, including the dependence on the interparticle interaction. The calculated heights of the peaks, however, in some cases differ with the experimental ones.

</details>


### [166] [Semi-classical evaporative cooling: classical and quantum distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20446)
*A. A. Arvizu-Velazquez,A. A. del Río-Lima,S. Dondé-Rodríguez,F. J. Poveda-Cuevas*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统一的半经典框架来描述囚禁原子气体的蒸发冷却过程，同时考虑了经典和量子统计。通过结合全局热力学与相空间分布，推导出了广泛囚禁势下粒子数和内能的通用解析表达式，并基于截断能量分布制定了递归蒸发协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立一个统一的理论框架来描述囚禁原子气体的蒸发冷却过程，该框架需要同时涵盖经典和量子统计效应。研究动机源于需要理解不同囚禁势下蒸发冷却的普适特性，并为超冷原子系统的实验优化提供理论指导。

Method: 研究方法基于统一的半经典框架，结合全局热力学（global thermodynamics）与相空间分布（phase-space distributions）。针对广泛的囚禁势家族，推导了粒子数和内能的通用解析表达式。在此基础上，基于截断能量分布（truncated energy distributions）制定了递归蒸发协议（recursive evaporation protocol）。

Result: 研究获得了适用于广泛囚禁势的通用解析表达式，揭示了系统自由度对冷却效率的调控作用。数值模拟显示了经典与量子系统在接近简并时的对比行为，特别是在四极阱（quadrupole traps）中观察到独特的特征，这源于其非标准的相空间标度（nonstandard phase-space scaling）。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个通用的理论工具，可用于模拟实验相关几何结构中的蒸发冷却过程。结果为优化超冷原子系统中的冷却轨迹提供了定量指导，揭示了不同囚禁势下冷却效率的普适特性。

Abstract: A unified semiclassical framework is presented to describe the evaporative cooling of trapped atomic gases, accounting for both classical and quantum statistics. By combining global thermodynamics with phase-space distributions, general analytic expressions for the particle number and internal energy are derived for a broad family of confining potentials. Building on these results, a recursive evaporation protocol is formulated based on truncated energy distributions, enabling stepwise mapping between successive thermodynamic states and revealing the system's degree of freedom governance over cooling efficiency. Numerical simulations of the systems highlight the contrasting behavior of classical and quantum systems as they approach degeneracy, with particularly distinctive signatures in quadrupole traps, due to their nonstandard phase-space scaling. The results provide a versatile theoretical tool for modeling evaporative cooling across experimentally relevant geometries and offer quantitative guidance for optimizing cooling trajectories in ultracold atomic systems.

### [167] [Emergence of Unique Steady Edge States in Trapped Ultracold Atom Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20763)
*Roland Cristopher F. Caballar*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究证明，在一维开放量子系统中，超冷原子阵列与玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）耦合时，系统边缘会出现独特的稳态，这源于激光激发和向BEC发射激发的联合效应，表明该系统是一种拓扑材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一维开放量子系统中超冷原子阵列与玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）耦合时的稳态行为，探索由激光激发和向BEC衰减共同作用产生的边缘态现象。

Method: 通过主方程（master equation）描述该开放量子系统的动力学，并采用数值和解析方法求解稳态解；同时数值演化系统随时间的变化以验证稳态的存在性和唯一性。

Result: 在谐波势阱阵列的两个边缘处出现了独特的稳态，这些稳态的存在与每个势阱中囚禁的原子数量无关，证明了其存在性和唯一性。

Conclusion: 该驱动囚禁超冷原子系统与BEC耦合构成了一种拓扑材料，其拓扑不变量由主方程表征，边缘稳态的出现是系统拓扑性质的体现。

Abstract: We show that, for a one - dimensional open quantum system of ultracold atoms trapped in an array of harmonic potentials that is weakly coupled to a background Bose - Einstein Condensate (BEC), a unique steady state emerges at either of the two edges of the array due to the combined effects of excitation via lasers of these ultracold atoms and decay back to their initial energy levels via emission of excitations into the BEC, acting as an excitation reservoir. We then solve, both numerically and analytically, for the steady states of the master equation that describes the dynamics of this open quantum system, and show that these steady states occur at the edges of the array of harmonic potentials trapping these atoms. Using the open quantum system's master equation to evolve it numerically over time, we demonstrate that these steady states at the edge of the system will emerge regardless of the number of atoms trapped in each of the harmonic potentials in the array, establishing both their existence and uniqueness, and demonstrating that this driven trapped ultracold atom system coupled to a BEC is a topological material whose topological invariant is characterized by its master equation.

### [168] [Heterosymmetric states of rotating quantum droplets under confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21395)
*S. Nikolaou,G. M. Kavoulakis,M. Ogren*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 研究受限二维量子液滴（quantum droplet）在旋转激发下的响应，发现超越广泛使用的单序参量模型，双组分系统在特定角动量半整数值附近会出现"异对称（heterosymmetric）"激发模式，其中两个组分携带不同的涡旋度（vorticities）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究受限二维量子液滴的旋转响应，该液滴产生于具有吸引相互作用的二元玻色混合物中，通过超越平均场效应（beyond-mean-field effects）稳定避免塌缩。研究特别关注超越广泛使用的"相位锁定（phase-locked）"单序参量模型，采用双序参量方法以揭示更丰富的物理行为。

Method: 采用双序参量模型分别描述两个组分，计算不同角动量值下的最低能量态。考虑两种外部约束势：谐波势（harmonic）和非谐波势（anharmonic）。研究包含粒子数平衡和轻微不平衡两种情况下的量子液滴行为。

Result: 对于粒子数平衡的量子液滴，在足够紧的约束下，接近特定半整数角动量值时，液滴以"异对称（heterosymmetric）"方式激发，两个组分携带不同的涡旋度。这种模式在单序参量模型中自然被忽略。轻微粒子数不平衡不仅导致能量增加，还解除了异对称态的双重简并性，该简并性原本表征具有$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性的平衡液滴。

Conclusion: 异对称激发模式受到混合物中超越平均场效应能量项的有利支持。研究揭示了双序参量模型相比单序参量模型能捕捉到更丰富的物理现象，特别是在受限量子液滴的旋转响应中出现的异对称激发态。

Abstract: We investigate the rotational response of a confined, two-dimensional quantum droplet, which emerges in an attractive binary Bose mixture that is stabilized against collapse by beyond-mean-field effects. We consider both a harmonic and an anharmonic form for the external confining potential. We go beyond the widely employed ``phase-locked" single-order-parameter model, maintaining two separate order parameters for the two components, and calculating the lowest-energy state for various values of the angular momentum. For a population-balanced quantum droplet and sufficiently tight confinement, we find that near certain half-integer values of the angular momentum the droplet is excited in a ``heterosymmetric" manner, with the two components carrying different vorticities. This mode is naturally missed by the single-order-parameter model. We additionally investigate the effects of a small population imbalance in the droplet. Apart from an energy increase associated with the population difference, the imbalance also lifts the double degeneracy of the heterosymmetric states, which characterizes the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric balanced droplet. The heterosymmetric mode is found to be favored by the energy term which captures the beyond-mean-field effects in the mixture.

### [169] [Critical dynamics of the superfluid phase transition in Model F](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21479)
*Chandrodoy Chattopadhyay,Robert Maguire,Josh Ott,Thomas Schaefer,Vladimir V. Skokov*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于Hohenberg-Halperin分类中模型F（model F）随机流体动力学理论的数值模拟，使用先前应用于普通流体液-气相变临界端点的Metropolis算法，并在模型E（model E）截断下进行计算。

Result: 在模型E截断下获得了预期的动力学指数z≈3/2，观察到相变处出现传播的第二声模式（second sound mode），第二声扩散率Ds符合标度关系Ds∼ξ^xκ，其中ξ为关联长度（correlation length），xκ=1/2。

Conclusion: 数值模拟验证了模型F理论在描述超流相变临界动力学方面的有效性，特别是在模型E截断下获得了符合预期的动力学指数，并证实了第二声模式的标度行为。

Abstract: We describe numerical simulations of the critical dynamics near the superfluid phase transition. The calculations are based on an implementation of a stochastic hydrodynamic theory known as model F in the classification of Hohenberg and Halperin. This theory is expected to describe dynamic scaling near the lambda transition in liquid $^4$He, Bose-Einstein condensation in ultracold atomic gases, and the superfluid transition in the unitary Fermi gas. Our simulation is based on a Metropolis algorithm previously applied to the critical endpoint of the liquid-gas phase transition in ordinary fluids. In the model E truncation of model F we obtain the expected dynamical exponent $z\simeq 3/2$. We observe the emergence of a propagating second sound mode at the phase transition. The second sound diffusivity $D_s$ is consistent with the scaling relation $D_s\sim ξ^{x_κ}$, where $ξ$ is the correlation length and $x_κ=1/2$.

The driven-dissipative condensate exhibits a long-lived, metastable plateau stabilized by a ghost attractor, a fixed point that lies outside the physical domain in configuration space, yet stalls the condensate dynamics for exceedingly long times before it dephases to zero [Phys. Rev. Lett. 135, 053402 (2025)]. Despite the nonequilibrium origin of this dynamical stabilization, the condensate exhibits quasithermal fluctuations in the plateau in that the relative order-parameter fluctuations scale as the inverse square root of the system size. A linear stability analysis further reveals the presence of exceptional points, resulting in multiple non-Hermitian phase transitions associated with the relaxation dynamics into and out of the metastable condensate.

### [171] [A two-dimensional realization of the parity anomaly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22173)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子反常（quantum anomalies）在经典理论对称性无法在量子化后保持时出现，但单层二维狄拉克费米子的宇称反常（parity anomaly）在真实二维系统中一直难以实现。本研究旨在通过合成量子系统观测这一效应。

Method: 利用超冷镝原子构建合成二维系统，将连续空间维度与原子自旋态编码的有限合成维度耦合，设计出可调谐的陈数（Chern number）为0和1的陈带（Chern bands）。在量子霍尔拓扑相变临界点，体带隙在单个狄拉克点闭合。

Result: 在临界点观测到鲁棒的半量子化霍尔漂移（half-quantized Hall drift），即使存在强非绝热激发。该响应源于能带拓扑的全局结构，受临界点涌现的宇称对称性保护，当宇称对称性被显式破坏时消失。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了合成量子系统作为研究量子反常及其与拓扑和非平衡动力学相互作用的强大平台，首次在真实二维系统中实现了宇称反常霍尔响应。

Abstract: Quantum anomalies arise when symmetries of a classical theory cannot be preserved upon quantization, leading to unconventional topological responses. A prominent example is the parity anomaly of a single two-dimensional Dirac fermion, which enforces a half-quantized Hall response. Anomaly inflow mechanism allows this effect to be observed at the surfaces of three-dimensional topological insulators, however, its realization in a genuinely two-dimensional system has remained elusive. Here we report the observation of a parity-anomalous Hall response at the critical point of a quantum Hall topological phase transition in a synthetic two-dimensional system of ultracold dysprosium atoms. By coupling a continuous spatial dimension to a finite synthetic dimension encoded in atomic spin states, we engineer tunable Chern bands with C = 0 and 1. At the transition, the bulk gap closes at a single Dirac point, where we observe a robust half-quantized Hall drift despite strong non-adiabatic excitations. We show that this response originates from the global structure of the band topology, is protected by an emergent parity symmetry at criticality, and disappears when parity is explicitly broken. Our work establishes synthetic quantum systems as a powerful platform to probe quantum anomalies and their interplay with topology and non-equilibrium dynamics.

</details>

### [172] [Cherenkov Neutrino Telescopes: Recent Progress and Next Steps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21685)
*Aya Ishihara*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文综述了中微子望远镜（neutrino telescopes）在天体物理学中的独特价值，探讨了其设计策略、科学目标及其在多信使天文学（multimessenger astronomy）中的关键作用，特别关注其在宇宙线（cosmic rays）起源研究中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子望远镜为研究高能宇宙提供了独特的观测窗口，能够探索传统高能信使无法触及的宇宙加速器和极端环境。其科学目标与粒子物理中的中微子实验虽有共同探测原理（如切伦科夫辐射观测），但在研究重点和运行约束上存在显著差异。

Method: 论文回顾了天体物理中微子探测的基本原理，概述了在不同介质和部署环境中的关键设计策略。重点分析了中微子望远镜如何利用切伦科夫辐射（Cherenkov radiation）等核心探测技术，并探讨了各种实验设计的适应性。

Result: 中微子望远镜在多信使天文学中扮演关键角色，能够揭示宇宙中最极端高能现象的驱动机制。特别强调其在阐明宇宙线起源方面的潜力，为理解高能宇宙现象提供了独特视角。

Conclusion: 中微子望远镜作为高能天体物理研究的重要工具，通过独特的观测能力填补了多信使天文学的关键空白。其在探测宇宙加速器和极端环境方面的优势，使其成为研究宇宙线起源和宇宙高能现象机制不可或缺的观测手段。

Abstract: Neutrino telescopes provide a unique observational gateway to the high-energy universe, enabling the study of cosmic accelerators and extreme environments that remain inaccessible to the other high-energy messengers. Although they share core detection principles with neutrino experiments in particle physics, such as the observation of Cherenkov radiation, their scientific objectives and operational constraints diverge markedly. This paper reviews the motivations behind astrophysical neutrino detection, outlines key design strategies across various media and deployment environments, and highlights the critical role of neutrino telescopes in the context of multimessenger astronomy. In particular, we emphasize their potential to illuminate the origins of cosmic rays and to probe the mechanisms driving the most energetic phenomena in the universe.

</details>


### [173] [Degeneracy in Accretion Disk Spectra from Naked Singularities and Kerr Black Holes: Application to the AGN MCG-06-30-15](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20282)
*Vishva Patel,Sayantan Bhattacharya,Sudip Bhattacharyya,Pankaj S. Joshi*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了相对论性吸积盘光谱能否区分黑洞与裸奇点（naked singularity），发现克尔（Kerr）黑洞与JMN-1裸奇点模型在光谱拟合上存在简并性（degeneracy），可能导致基于吸积盘光谱的自旋测量出现错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理论研究预测引力坍缩可能形成黑洞或可见的裸奇点（naked singularity），但区分这两类坍缩天体的观测特征仍是物理学的重要目标。本研究旨在检验相对论性吸积盘光谱是否能够提供这样的区分测试。

Method: 研究构建了JMN-1裸奇点几何中的薄吸积盘（thin accretion disk）加性表格模型，该模型与史瓦西（Schwarzschild）外部匹配，并利用NuSTAR X射线数据对活动星系核MCG-06-30-15进行拟合。同时与标准的克尔（Kerr）和史瓦西（Schwarzschild）黑洞模型进行比较，并包含了相对论反射光谱成分relxill。

Result: 尽管具有不同的基础几何结构，但自旋的克尔（Kerr）黑洞与非自旋的JMN-1裸奇点提供了相似的光谱拟合结果，且这些拟合显著优于史瓦西（Schwarzschild）黑洞模型。这种裸奇点与克尔黑洞之间的简并性（degeneracy）可能导致基于吸积盘光谱的坍缩天体自旋测量出现错误。

Conclusion: 这种简并性（degeneracy）可以通过独立的自旋测量来打破，这也有助于识别裸奇点（naked singularity）。研究结果还可能对引力波源和X射线双星测量的坍缩天体自旋分布差异产生影响。

Abstract: Theoretical studies suggest that gravitational collapse can form either a black hole or a visible (naked) singularity. Identifying observational signatures that distinguish these two types of collapsed objects is a holy grail of physics. Here, we examine whether relativistic accretion disk spectra can provide such a test. We construct an additive table model for a thin accretion disk in the Joshi-Malafarina-Narayan (JMN-1) naked singularity geometry matched to a Schwarzschild exterior and fit it to NuSTAR X-ray data from the AGN MCG-06-30-15. Our results are compared with standard Kerr and Schwarzschild black hole models. We also include the relativistic reflection spectral component relxill. Despite their different underlying geometries, the spinning (Kerr) black hole and the non-spinning JMN-1 naked singularity provide similar spectral fits, which are significantly better fits than the Schwarzschild black hole. This degeneracy between the naked singularity and the Kerr black hole could lead to incorrect spin measurements of collapsed objects using disk spectra. The degeneracy could be broken with an independent spin measurement, which could also help identify a naked singularity. Our results could also have a role in different spin distributions of collapsed objects measured from gravitational-wave sources and X-ray binaries.

### [174] [Accurate and efficient simulation-based inference for massive black-hole binaries with LISA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20431)
*Alice Spadaro,Jonathan Gair,Davide Gerosa,Stephen R. Green,Riccardo Buscicchio,Nihar Gupte,Rodrigo Tenorio,Samuel Clyne,Michael Pürrer,Natalia Korsakova*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个用于LISA可观测高质量黑洞双星（质量≳10⁷ M☉）的精确模拟推理框架，该框架基于DINGO引力波参数估计代码，通过归一化流模型实现快速全参数估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对LISA可观测的高质量黑洞双星（质量大于约10⁷太阳质量），需要开发精确的模拟推理框架进行参数估计。现有方法需要扩展到LISA频段，以处理该频段特有的观测挑战。

Method: 方法基于DINGO引力波参数估计代码，扩展到LISA频段。使用对齐自旋高阶模式波形模型和探测器响应的低频近似训练归一化流模型。采样后通过重要性采样获得真实后验分布。

Result: 在LISA观测相关的信噪比范围内验证性能，与标准方法对比显示后验分布一致，信噪比高达~500时结果稳健。信噪比~1000时采样效率降低，但仍能产生无偏且紧致的后验分布。训练后的流模型可在不到一分钟内生成2万个后验样本。

Conclusion: DINGO成为LISA频段大质量黑洞双星快速全参数估计的有前景的神经推理框架。该无似然方法便于推广，可处理时变探测器响应、非平稳噪声伪影（如数据间隙和毛刺）以及低延迟参数估计。

Abstract: We develop an accurate simulation-based inference framework for high-mass ($\gtrsim\!10^7 \rm{M_\odot}$) black-hole binaries observable by LISA. The method is implemented within the DINGO gravitational-wave parameter-estimation code, extending its application from ground-based detectors to the LISA band. We train a normalizing-flow model using aligned-spin higher-mode waveform models and a low-frequency approximation of the detector response. After sampling, we importance-sample to the true posterior. We validate performance on simulated signals spanning the signal-to-noise regimes relevant for LISA observations and benchmark our new DINGO implementation against standard methods. We report robust agreement in the inferred posterior distributions up to signal-to-noise ratios of $\sim\!500$. At higher signal-to-noise ratios of $\sim\!1000$, we observe a reduction in sampling efficiency, while still yielding unbiased and tightly localized posteriors that can be used as a starting point for follow-up with traditional methods.The trained flow can generate 20 thousand posterior samples in less than a minute, establishing DINGO as a promising neural inference framework for rapid full-parameter estimation of massive black-hole binaries in the LISA band. The likelihood-free nature of this approach allows for straightforward generalizations, including a time-dependent detector response, non-stationary noise artifacts such as gaps and glitches, and low-latency parameter estimations.

### [175] [A robust method for classification of chimera states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22026)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇美拉态（chimera states）作为非线性动力学中最引人注目的现象之一，其可靠且系统性的分类方法仍具挑战性。现有方法通常适用范围有限且缺乏鲁棒性（robustness），因此需要开发更有效的分类工具。

Method: 本文提出了一种结合傅里叶分析（Fourier analysis）与统计分类（statistical classification）的方法，用于表征奇美拉行为。该方法应用于通过狄拉克算子（Dirac operator）耦合的拓扑信号（topological signals）系统。

Result: 该方法成功捕捉了模型所展现的丰富动力学状态（dynamical regimes），并证明其对网络拓扑（network topology）和系统参数（system parameters）的变化具有鲁棒性（robustness）。

Conclusion: 该框架不仅适用于特定模型，还为复杂系统中不同动力学状态（dynamical regimes）的区分提供了一个通用且自动化的工具。

Abstract: Chimera states are one of the most intriguing phenomena in nonlinear dynamics, characterized by the coexistence of coherent and incoherent behavior in systems of coupled identical oscillators. Despite extensive studies and numerous observations in different settings, the development of reliable and systematic methods to classify chimera states and distinguish them from other dynamical patterns remains a challenging task. Existing approaches are often limited in scope and lack robustness. In this work, we propose a method based on Fourier analysis combined with statistical classification to characterize chimera behavior. The method is applied to a system of topological signals coupled via the Dirac operator, where it successfully captures the rich dynamical regimes exhibited by the model. We demonstrate that the proposed approach is robust with respect to variations in network topology and system parameters. Beyond the specific model considered, the framework provides a general and automated tool for distinguishing different dynamical regimes in complex systems.

### [176] [Geometric helices on del Pezzo surfaces from tilting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22065)
*Pierrick Bousseau*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 证明了del Pezzo曲面上所有几何螺旋（geometric helices）可通过基本操作序列相互关联，从而得出其仿射锥（affine cone）的非交换crepant解消（non-commutative crepant resolutions）可通过突变（mutations）相互关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究del Pezzo曲面上几何螺旋之间的关系，以及由此导出的非交换crepant解消之间的关联性。这涉及导出范畴（derived category）中对象的结构和变换。

Method: 通过一系列基本操作（旋转、平移、正交重排、导出对偶、线丛张量积、倾斜）来分析几何螺旋的关系。证明依赖于将倾斜操作几何解释为作用于对数Calabi-Yau曲面（log Calabi-Yau surface）的簇变换（cluster transformations）。

Result: 证明了del Pezzo曲面上所有几何螺旋可通过基本操作序列相互关联。作为推论，得出del Pezzo曲面仿射锥的任何两个非交换crepant解消都可通过突变相互关联。

Conclusion: 建立了del Pezzo曲面上几何螺旋之间的系统联系，并将倾斜操作与簇变换的几何解释联系起来，为理解非交换crepant解消的等价性提供了新视角。

Abstract: We prove that all geometric helices in the derived category of coherent sheaves on a del Pezzo surface are related by a sequence of elementary operations: rotation, shifting, orthogonal reordering, derived dualization, tensoring by a line bundle, and tilting. As a consequence, any two non-commutative crepant resolutions of the affine cone over a del Pezzo surface are related by mutations. The proof relies on a geometric interpretation of tilting operations as cluster transformations acting on toric models of a log Calabi--Yau surface mirror to the del Pezzo surface.

### [177] [Gate-Drain Leakage Enhanced by Drain-Induced Dielectric Barrier Lowering in Gate-All-Around Field Effect Transistors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21015)
*Juan P. Mendez,Coleman Cariker,Michael Titze,Alex A. Belianinov,Denis Mamaluy*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究通过第一性原理模拟揭示了环绕栅场效应晶体管（GAAFETs）在负栅压下的漏电流源于栅极-漏极隧穿效应，该效应因漏极诱导的介质势垒降低而显著增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环绕栅场效应晶体管（Gate-All-Around Field-Effect Transistors, GAAFETs）作为鳍式场效应晶体管（FinFET）的继任技术已进入大规模生产，但存在负栅压下漏电流偏离热离子依赖性的问题。理解该泄漏电流的起源对于确定GAAFETs的缩放极限、指导器件和材料优化以抑制关态电流至关重要。

Method: 研究采用预测性第一性原理模拟（predictive first-principles simulations）来分析GAAFETs在负栅压下的泄漏机制。

Result: 模拟结果表明，观察到的负栅压下泄漏电流源于栅极-漏极隧穿（gate-to-drain tunneling），该隧穿效应因漏极诱导的介质势垒降低（drain-induced dielectric barrier lowering）而显著增强。此外，实验测量显示辐射诱导缺陷在负栅压区的影响增加，而在正栅压下其影响基本可忽略。

Conclusion: 该研究明确了GAAFETs负栅压下泄漏电流的物理机制，为确定器件缩放极限和优化设计提供了关键见解，有助于指导抑制关态电流的器件和材料优化策略。

Abstract: Gate-All-Around Field-Effect Transistors (GAAFETs), now entering high-volume production as successors to fin field-effect transistor technology, are enabling continued scaling and enhanced performance in advanced semiconductor nodes. However, the drain-current in GAAFETs strongly deviates from the thermionic dependence at negative gate voltages, exhibiting the existence of leakage that is additionally enhanced at high applied biases. Understanding the origin of this leakage is essential for determining the scaling limits of GAAFETs and for guiding device and material optimizations aimed at suppressing the off-state current. Additionally, recent experimental measurements have revealed the increased influence of radiation-induced defects in the negative gate voltage regime, with their impact remaining largely negligible for positive gate voltages. Through predictive first-principles simulations, we demonstrate that the observed leakage current at negative gate voltages originates from gate-to-drain tunneling, which is significantly enhanced by drain-induced dielectric barrier lowering between the gate and drain.

### [178] [A quiet quantum revolution in Earth's deep interior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20812)
*Renata Wentzcovitch,Laura Cobden,Christine Houser,Grace Shephard,Jingyi Zhuang*

Main category: physics.geo-ph

TL;DR: 地球下地幔中铁离子的压力诱导自旋交叉（spin crossover）是一种量子现象，通过改变矿物弹性性质影响地震波传播，为三维地震成像与矿物物理学的整合提供了关键解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在阐明地球下地幔中铁离子自旋交叉（spin crossover）的地球物理意义，该量子现象虽已被实验和理论确认，但其对地震结构的影响直到最近才通过矿物物理学与三维地震成像的整合得以明确。

Method: 通过整合矿物物理学（mineral physics）与三维地震成像（three-dimensional seismic imaging）技术，分析铁离子自旋交叉对弹性性质的影响，并将其与全球地震层析成像（global tomography）观测结果进行对比。

Result: 自旋交叉降低了体积模量（bulk modulus）和P波速度，但对S波速度影响较小，导致P波与S波异常之间的解耦（decoupling）。这一特征在全球层析成像中观测到，并与实际地幔温度和成分相吻合。

Conclusion: 自旋交叉并非形成尖锐边界，而是延伸至大部分下地幔，作为地震结构的弥散但关键的控制因素。该工作强调了量子尺度电子跃迁如何影响行星尺度动力学和地球深部解释。

Abstract: The Earth's lower mantle hosts a subtle but pervasive quantum phenomenon: the pressure-induced spin crossover of iron in its dominant minerals, bridgmanite and ferropericlase. In this transition, iron ions gradually shift from high-spin to low-spin electronic states without structural change, altering their volume, compressibility, and elastic properties. Although long recognized experimentally and theoretically, its geophysical significance has only recently become clear through the integration of mineral physics and three-dimensional seismic imaging. The spin crossover reduces bulk modulus and P-wave velocities while leaving S-wave speeds largely unaffected, producing a distinctive decoupling between P- and S-wave anomalies. This signature is now observed in global tomography and reconciles seismic observations with realistic mantle temperatures and compositions. Rather than forming a sharp boundary, the crossover extends across most of the lower mantle, acting as a diffuse yet essential control on seismic structure. This work highlights how quantum-scale electronic transitions influence planetary-scale dynamics and interpretations of Earth's deep interior.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

### [180] [Variations on a theme of MacDowell-Mansouri](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21930)
*P. D. Alvarez,K. Krasnov*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了一类四维规范理论泛函，通过插入矩阵打破规范群对称性，证明了其临界点对应于常标量曲率近凯勒（almost-Kähler）4-流形，在紧致流形和特定条件下进一步简化为凯勒-爱因斯坦（Kähler-Einstein）4-流形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于四维广义相对论的MacDowell-Mansouri表述，旨在探索一类通过插入矩阵打破规范群对称性而获得的四维规范理论泛函。

Method: 方法基于庞特里亚金密度（Pontryagin density），通过插入矩阵将规范群G（具体为SU(3)）破缺到子群H（具体为U(2)），构造相应的泛函并分析其临界点性质。

Result: 结果表明，所得泛函的临界点对应于常标量曲率近凯勒（almost-Kähler）4-流形。在紧致4-流形上，若附加标量曲率非负且第一陈类（first Chern class）满足爱因斯坦度量存在条件，则临界点进一步简化为凯勒-爱因斯坦（Kähler-Einstein）4-流形。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了规范理论泛函与几何结构间的深刻联系，揭示了通过规范群破缺构造的泛函其临界点具有特定的几何特征，为理解四维流形的几何与物理性质提供了新视角。

Abstract: Inspired by the MacDowell-Mansouri formulation of four-dimensional General Relativity, we study a class of four-dimensional gauge-theoretic functionals obtained from the Pontryagin density of a G-connection by inserting, under the trace, a matrix that breaks the gauge group G to a subgroup H. Concretely, we study the model with the pair (G,H) given by (SU(3), U(2)). We show that the critical points of the resulting functional are constant scalar curvature almost-Kahler 4-manifolds. On compact 4-manifolds, a stronger conclusion holds under the additional assumption that the scalar curvature is non-negative and the first Chern class is such that an Einstein metric can exist. In this case, results in the literature imply that the critical points are Kahler-Einstein 4-manifolds.

</details>

### [181] [From the Stochastic Embedding Sufficiency Theorem to a Superspace Diffusion Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20423)
*Carolina Garcia,Lucía Perea Durán,Agnese Venezia,Alex Conradie*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种通用的随机嵌入充分性定理（Stochastic Embedding Sufficiency Theorem），能够从标量时间序列中非参数地恢复漂移和扩散场，无需事先假设物理规律。该方法在九个物理领域中成功恢复了控制方程，误差范围在0.026%至约1%之间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一个多世纪以来，各物理领域中的随机微分方程正向推导一直独立进行，缺乏跨学科的一般化方法。该研究旨在填补这一空白，通过逆向方法实现跨物理领域的统一框架。

Method: 提出随机嵌入充分性定理作为Takens嵌入定理在随机系统中的推广，建立了一种盲恢复协议（blind recovery protocol）。该方法仅接收原始时间序列和采样间隔，无需任何物理先验假设，即可非参数地恢复漂移和扩散场。

Result: 该方法在九个物理领域中成功恢复了控制方程：经典力学、统计力学、核物理、量子力学、化学动力学、电磁学、相对论量子力学、量子谐振子动力学和量子电动力学。恢复误差范围在0.026%至约1%之间，所有零假设在5%水平上均未被拒绝。物理常数在两个通道中自然涌现，无需事先指定。

Conclusion: 恢复的扩散系数构成了一个经验模式——σ连续统（σ-continuum），其中普朗克常数、玻尔兹曼常数和光速扮演着结构上不同的角色。四个规范公理形式化了该框架，物理时间作为随机演化的单调泛函涌现。在短记忆极限下，漂移、协方差算子和涨落幅度都被确定，由此产生的超空间扩散假说生成了非参数、第一性原理、可证伪的预测。

Abstract: The forward derivation of stochastic differential equations in individual physical domains has proceeded independently for over a century without generalising across disciplines. A generalisation of Takens' embedding theorem to stochastic systems, the Stochastic Embedding Sufficiency Theorem, closes this gap as an inverse methodology enabling non-parametric recovery of drift and diffusion fields from scalar time series without prior assumptions about the governing physics.
  A blind recovery protocol, receiving only raw time series and sampling interval, is applied to nine domains: classical mechanics, statistical mechanics, nuclear physics, quantum mechanics, chemical kinetics, electromagnetism, relativistic quantum mechanics, quantum harmonic oscillator dynamics, and quantum electrodynamics. The pipeline recovers the governing equations of each domain with errors from 0.026% to ~1%, with no null hypothesis rejected at the 5% level. Physical constants emerge in both channels without prior specification.
  The recovered diffusion coefficients constitute an empirical pattern, the σ-continuum, in which the Planck constant, Boltzmann constant, and speed of light play structurally distinct roles. Three independent uniqueness arguments determine the gravitational diffusion coefficient as one Planck length per square root of Planck time, non-parametrically derived from first principles.
  Four canonical axioms formalise the framework. Physical time emerges as a monotone functional of the stochastic evolution. Within these axioms and the short-memory limit, the drift, covariance operator, and fluctuation amplitude are all fixed. The resulting superspace diffusion hypothesis generates non-parametric, first-principles, falsifiable predictions against galactic kinematic data as developed in a companion paper (Part II).

</details>


### [182] [Quantum Chaos in Many-Body Systems Without a Classical Analogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20540)
*Fotis I. Giasemis*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文研究PXP自旋链模型中弱破坏遍历性（weak breaking of ergodicity）的中间行为，通过分析本征态热化假设（ETH）违反、能级间距统计、本征向量分量统计以及淬火动力学，揭示了该模型介于遍历性和局域化之间的量子混沌特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子系统中从规则到混沌动力学的转变通过谱统计变化表征，而量子混沌系统具有遍历性（ergodicity），可探索希尔伯特空间所有允许构型。本论文旨在研究遍历性与局域化之间的中间行为，即弱破坏遍历性现象。

Method: 研究采用PXP自旋链模型（PXP spin chain model），该模型在特定动力学约束下允许自旋翻转。方法包括：分析本征态热化假设（ETH）违反情况；研究能级间距统计（level-spacing statistics）；检验本征向量分量统计（eigenvector component statistics）；通过淬火（quench）实验研究能量在系统中的传播。

Result: 在PXP谱中发现少量违反ETH的状态；能级间距统计接近半泊松分布（semi-Poisson），大系统尺寸下趋近维格纳-戴森统计（Wigner--Dyson statistics）；本征向量分量统计呈现非高斯分布；淬火实验观察到弹道前沿（ballistic fronts）的能量传播模式。

Conclusion: PXP自旋链模型展示了弱破坏遍历性的中间行为特征，其量子混沌诊断指标介于完全遍历系统和强局域化系统之间，为理解量子多体系统中遍历性破坏的中间状态提供了重要案例。

Abstract: In classical systems, chaos is clearly defined via the behavior of trajectories. In quantum systems with a classical analogue one finds that the transition from regular to chaotic dynamics is signified by a change in the spectral statistics. This has been found to remain true for quantum systems with no classical analogue, including many-body systems. Furthermore, quantum chaotic systems explore all the allowed configurations in the Hilbert space, i.e. they are ergodic, while integrable systems, and systems in the many-body localized phase, are restricted to a certain subspace of the available phase space, and hence strongly break ergodicity. In this dissertation, we study the intermediate behavior between ergodicity and localization, i.e. the weak breaking of ergodicity. The model examined is the PXP spin chain model, where spins are allowed to flip only under certain kinetic constraints. We start by reproducing some already established results. First, we explore the eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (ETH) for this model and demonstrate the existence of a small number of states, throughout the PXP spectrum, that violate the ETH. Then we study the level-spacing statistics of the model, a well-known quantum chaos diagnostic, which turns out to be close to semi-Poisson and approach Wigner--Dyson statistics for large system sizes. Moreover, we examine various aspects of the model that have not been studied before. For example, the eigenvector component statistics, another quantum chaos diagnostic, for the PXP model turn out to be non-Gaussian. Finally, we perform a quench, in order to study how the energy spreads throughout the system, and observe ballistic fronts.

</details>


### [183] [Multiscale Violation of Onsager Reciprocity: Thermomechanical Proof, Atomic Evidence, and Graphene Predictions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20773)
*Monty Dabas*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究发展了一个几何框架，通过熵加权（entropy-weighted）重参数化热力学响应函数，在微观昂萨格互易性（Onsager reciprocity）不违反的前提下，产生有效的交叉耦合不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于热容（heat capacities）$C_p$和$C_v$的平行结构，旨在理解如何在微观时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）约束下，通过熵加权方法产生有效的热力学耦合不对称性。

Method: 方法包括引入熵加权响应变量$λ_p$、$λ_v$、$λ_s$和$λ_t$，构建热力学不变量$Γ_c=λ_p/λ_v=C_v/C_p$和$Γ_m=λ_s/λ_t=κ_T/κ_S$。在热力学状态空间的微分形式表示中，非平衡过程产生曲率$Ω=dω$，导致变换后耦合矩阵的有效不对称性。

Result: 微观定理表明，具有时间反演不对称性$χ(Γ)=W(ΘΓ)/W(Γ)\neq1$的熵加权统计系综，会在格林-久保（Green--Kubo）输运矩阵中产生反对称贡献。原子尺度分析显示3d过渡金属系列存在交叉导数不对称性，在Cr和Cu的构型异常处达到峰值。单层石墨烯的温度依赖拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）显示出统计显著的热滞回线（hysteresis loops），为热力学曲率提供了实验证据。

Conclusion: 研究结果在熵加权热力学耦合的几何解释框架下，统一了微观不可逆性（microscopic irreversibility）、原子结构异常和宏观热滞现象，为理解非平衡热力学过程提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Onsager reciprocity $L_{ij}=L_{ji}$ is a cornerstone of near-equilibrium thermodynamics derived from microscopic time-reversal symmetry. We develop a geometric framework in which entropy-weighted reparameterization of thermodynamic response functions leads to an effective asymmetry in cross-couplings without violating the microscopic Onsager theorem. Motivated by the parallel structure of heat capacities $C_p$ and $C_v$, we introduce entropy-weighted response variables $λ_p$, $λ_v$, $λ_s$, and $λ_t$. Their ratios $Γ_c=λ_p/λ_v=C_v/C_p$ and $Γ_m=λ_s/λ_t=κ_T/κ_S$ form thermodynamic invariants whose product equals unity in equilibrium.
  Within a differential-form representation of thermodynamic state space, equilibrium corresponds to exactness of the accessibility form $ω=λ_p\,dp+λ_v\,dv$ with $dω=0$, while non-equilibrium processes generate curvature $Ω=dω$, producing an effective asymmetry in the transformed coupling matrix. A microscopic theorem shows that entropy-weighted statistical ensembles with time-reversal asymmetry $χ(Γ)=W(ΘΓ)/W(Γ)\neq1$ generate an antisymmetric contribution to the Green--Kubo transport matrix.
  Atomic-scale analysis using the Transforma model reveals cross-derivative asymmetries across the $3d$ transition series, peaking at configuration anomalies in Cr and Cu. Temperature-dependent Raman spectroscopy of monolayer graphene exhibits statistically significant hysteresis loops (up to $30σ$), providing experimental evidence for thermodynamic curvature. These results unify microscopic irreversibility, atomic structure anomalies, and macroscopic hysteresis within a geometric interpretation of entropy-weighted thermodynamic coupling.

### [184] [Dissipative free fermions in disguise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22163)
*Kohei Fukai,Hironobu Yoshida,Hosho Katsura*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期发现的"伪装自由费米子"自旋链具有隐藏的自由费米子谱，但标准Jordan-Wigner变换无法求解。本研究旨在将这一FFD框架扩展到由GKSL方程描述的开放量子系统。

Method: 研究建立了FFD框架下的一般可精确求解开放量子系统类别：如果Liouvillian frustration graph是无爪的且具有单纯团，则Liouvillian具有隐藏的自由费米子谱。特别地，(偶洞，无爪)条件自动保证这一性质。

Result: 该框架使得能够精确计算Liouvillian gap和无限温度自关联函数。这是首次在开放量子系统中实现FFD机制，为开放系统的精确求解提供了新途径。

Conclusion: 研究成功将FFD框架扩展到开放量子系统，建立了基于图论条件的可精确求解系统类别，为开放量子系统的理论研究提供了新的分析工具和精确计算方法。

Abstract: Recently, a class of spin chains known as ``free fermions in disguise'' (FFD) has been discovered, which possess hidden free-fermion spectra even though they are not solvable via the standard Jordan-Wigner transformation. In this work, we extend this FFD framework to open quantum systems governed by the Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad (GKSL) equation. We establish a general class of exactly solvable open quantum systems within the FFD framework: if the Liouvillian frustration graph is claw-free and has a simplicial clique, the Liouvillian possesses a hidden free-fermion spectrum. In particular, the (even-hole, claw)-free condition automatically guarantees this, enabling exact computation of the Liouvillian gap and an infinite-temperature autocorrelation function. Our results provide the first realization of the FFD mechanism in open quantum systems.

### [185] [Timescale Coalescence Makes Hidden Persistent Forcing Spectrally Dark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20917)
*Yuda Bi,Chenyu Zhang,Vince D Calhoun*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 在粗粒度观测下，未解析慢强迫的可检测性受投影控制：只有隐藏诱导变形在简化零流形法向上的分量保持局部可见。通过可解的驱动AR(1)-by-AR(1)基准测试，发现局部Whittle/Kullback-Leibler距离以λ⁴阶变化，而非观测谱本身的λ²阶扰动，表明可检测性为四次方而非二次方耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在粗粒度观测条件下，未解析慢强迫的可检测性问题。探讨隐藏动力学的局部可见性如何受投影控制，特别是变形分量相对于简化零流形（reduced null manifold）的方向性影响。

Method: 建立可解的驱动AR(1)-by-AR(1)基准测试模型。通过分析局部Whittle/Kullback-Leibler距离从真实谱到最佳邻近单极点替代谱的行为，量化可检测性。推导封闭形式的系数C，并识别谱暗区（spectrally dark regime）。

Result: 局部Whittle/Kullback-Leibler距离遵循D_loc(λ)=Cλ⁴+O(λ⁶)，尽管观测谱本身在O(λ²)阶受扰动，表明可检测性为四次方而非二次方耦合。系数C以封闭形式获得，当隐藏与内在时间尺度重合时以(a-b)²消失，识别出谱暗区。得到总体边界ℓ_c^pop(N)∝(log N/N)^{1/4}，Whittle-BIC交叉点接近该尺度。

Conclusion: 该基准测试揭示了简化推断中的更广泛几何原理：切向隐藏效应通过重新参数化被吸收，而只有存活的法向分量控制局部可区分性。这为理解粗粒度观测下隐藏动力学的可检测性提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Under coarse observation, detectability of unresolved slow forcing can be projection-controlled: only the component of the hidden-induced deformation normal to a reduced null manifold remains locally visible. We establish this exactly in a solvable driven AR$(1)$-by-AR$(1)$ benchmark. The local Whittle/Kullback--Leibler distance from the true spectrum to the best nearby one-pole surrogate obeys $\Dloc(λ)=Cλ^4+O(λ^6)$, even though the observed spectrum itself is perturbed at $O(λ^2)$; detectability is therefore quartic, not quadratic, in coupling. The coefficient $C$ is obtained in closed form and vanishes as $(a-b)^2$ when the hidden and intrinsic timescales coalesce, identifying a spectrally \emph{dark} regime in which the leading perturbation is tangent to the reduced manifold. This yields a population boundary $\lcpop(N)\propto(\log N/N)^{1/4}$, with Whittle-BIC crossover near that scale. The benchmark exposes a broader geometric principle in reduced inference: tangent hidden effects are absorbed by reparametrization, whereas only surviving normal components control local distinguishability.

</details>

Abstract: We introduce a new approach to disordered two-dimensional Ising models based on the extension of the combinatorial solution to randomized supercells. ### [187] [Taming of free volume in statistical mechanics of the hard disks model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21324)
*Victor M. Pergamenshchik,Taras Bryk,Andrij Trokhymchuk*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究将硬碟模型（hard disk model）中自由体积（free volume）的长期难题转化为精确解析公式，建立了统计力学框架，通过蒙特卡洛模拟获得熵和压力，在接近密堆积的整个密度范围内重现了已知状态方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决硬碟模型中自由体积的长期难题，该自由体积具有高度不规则形状，阻碍了精确的统计力学分析。

Method: 将自由体积精确表达为最多五个排斥圆（exclusion circles）的交集面积函数，这些函数可解析计算为圆盘坐标的函数；配分函数（partition function）可分解为自由体积的乘积，并具有气态和液态两种精确极限形式。

Result: 通过蒙特卡洛生成的圆盘坐标，解析获得熵和压力，在接近密堆积（close packing）的几乎整个密度范围内重现了硬碟的已知状态方程（equation of state）；在中间密度下，理论揭示了与六角有序化（hexagonal ordering）前的缺陷形成相关的混合液态区域。

Conclusion: 五个圆盘的交集面积可作为局部六角有序（local hexagonal order）的标量度量；该理论可直接应用于硬球模型（hard sphere model）。

Abstract: We turn the long time puzzle of the free volume, known for its highly irregular form, into exact analytical formulae and develop statistical mechanics of the hard disk model. The free volume is exactly expressed in terms of the intersection areas of up to five exclusion circles, which can be computed analytically as functions of disk coordinates. In turn, the free volume determines the partition function and entropy. The partition function is shown to factorize into a product of free volumes and admits two exact limiting forms corresponding to gaslike and liquidlike regimes. From this construction, using Monte Carlo-generated disk coordinates, the entropy and pressure are obtained analytically and recover the known equation of state of hard disks in almost entire density range up to the close packing. At intermediate densities, the theory reveals a mixed liquid regime associated with defect formation preceding the hexagonal ordering. The intersection area of five disks emerges as a scalar measure of the local hexagonal order. The theory can be directly adopted for the hard sphere model.

</details>


### [188] [Strict Entropy Decrease of Clausius Entropy in an Isolated System with Energy-Form Conversion: Theoretical Proof, Numerical Illustration, and Critical Examination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21765)
*Ting Peng*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文在克劳修斯（Clausius）框架内对热力学第二定律（second law）主张进行严格压力测试，通过能量形式转换的孤立复合系统分析，发现理想情况下克劳修斯熵（Clausius entropy）可能为负值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在基于明确陈述的物理假设和严格逻辑推理，在克劳修斯（Clausius）框架内对热力学第二定律（second law）主张进行严格的压力测试（stress test）。

Method: 直接采用克劳修斯熵定义（Clausius's entropy definition）分析具有能量形式转换的孤立复合系统，热量从具有较小热容的冷释放子系统提取，转换为电能，然后作为热量传递给较热的子系统。

Result: 在理想极限下，电路部分对克劳修斯熵计算贡献可忽略，模型化储热器的克劳修斯熵和为负值：ΔS_Cl = Q(1/T_B - 1/T_A) < 0。

Conclusion: 任何声称的矛盾应解释为不同公理集之间的兼容性问题，而非上述克劳修斯簿记（Clausius bookkeeping）中的代数错误，论文提供了推导、数值示例和范围分析。

Abstract: This paper is accountable only to explicitly stated physical assumptions and strict logical inference. Its goal is to run a rigorous stress test of second-law claims within the Clausius framework. We work directly with \textbf{Clausius's entropy definition} for an isolated composite with energy-form conversion. Heat is withdrawn from a cold releasing subsystem with relatively small heat capacity, converted to electrical energy, and then delivered as heat to a hotter subsystem. In the ideal limit, the electrical leg contributes negligibly to Clausius entropy accounting, so the modeled reservoir Clausius sum is \[ ΔS_{\mathrm{Cl}} = Q\!\left(\frac{1}{T_B}-\frac{1}{T_A}\right) < 0. \] The paper provides a derivation, numerical illustrations, and a scope analysis; any claimed contradiction should be interpreted as a compatibility issue between different axiom sets, not as an algebraic error in the Clausius bookkeeping above.

</details>


### [189] [Materials Beyond Hamiltonian Limits -- Quantum Measurement as a Resource for Material Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21769)

Method: 论文探索了幺正-投影电子动力学的基础理论，并通过模型计算展示了被动介观结构、新型磁性材料以及能量收集与转换平台的设计原理。这些系统将哈密顿演化与投影诱导的状态更新交织进行。

Conclusion: 幺正-投影动力学突破了纯幺正演化的约束，为量子材料及其功能开辟了新领域。这一理论框架为设计具有新型功能特性的材料和器件提供了基础，包括非互易传输、新型磁性和高效能量转换等应用。

Abstract: Recent studies have identified materials and devices whose behavior lies beyond the scope of conventional electronic-structure theory. Such theories are formulated entirely in terms of Hamiltonian evolution and therefore describe only unitary dynamics and thus only a restricted class of quantum systems.
  In contrast, electron systems that incorporate quantum measurement as an intrinsic dynamical element undergo Hamiltonian evolution interleaved with projection-induced state updates. This unitary-projective dynamics breaks constraints imposed by purely unitary evolution and permits stochastic population transfer between symmetry-related transport channels, thereby enabling fundamentally new material functionalities. This insight motivates the deliberate design of materials and devices that harness unitary-projective dynamics.
  This article explores the foundations of unitary-projective electron dynamics and charts the resulting landscape of quantum materials and their functionalities. Model calculations demonstrate passive mesoscopic structures with intrinsic nonreciprocal single-electron transmission, materials exhibiting a novel category of magnetism, and possible platforms for energy harvesting and conversion with efficiencies that exceed the standard Carnot limit.

Abstract: Landau theory usually treats free-energy coefficients as intrinsic parameters fixed by thermodynamic variables. ### [191] [Comment on: Discontinuous codimension-two bifurcation in a Vlasov equation (arXiv:2212.01250)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22066)
*Tarcísio N. Teles,Renato Pakter,Yan Levin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文对Yamaguchi和Barré的研究提出评论，指出其基于Vlasov方程线性稳定性分析的方法无法准确预测广义哈密顿平均场模型中准稳态相变的位置和性质。通过大规模分子动力学模拟发现，初始稳态分布的分岔分析与实际相变行为存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在评论Yamaguchi和Barré最近的工作，该工作使用Vlasov方程的线性稳定性分析来表征广义哈密顿平均场模型中的相变。作者认为这种分岔分析方法不足以预测准稳态相变的位置和性质。

Method: 采用大规模分子动力学模拟方法，使用N=10^8个粒子进行广泛模拟。通过分析双峰动量分布下的系统行为，对比线性稳定性分析预测与实际观测结果。

Result: 研究发现，Yamaguchi和Barré识别的失稳阈值并不对应铁磁相变；系统实际上保持在顺磁态，其特征是磁化强度具有零时间平均的振荡。真正的顺磁-铁磁相变是不连续（一级）的，发生在显著更大的耦合强度处，并表现出清晰的状态共存现象。

Conclusion: 在线性分岔和对称性破缺相变在长程相互作用系统中是不同现象，线性分岔分析缺乏预测系统长期命运的能力。这表明需要更全面的分析方法来理解这类系统中的相变行为。

Abstract: We comment on the recent work by Yamaguchi and Barré [Phys. Rev. E 107, 054203 (2023)], which uses linear stability analysis of the Vlasov equation to characterize phase transitions in a generalized Hamiltonian Mean Field (gHMF) model. By performing extensive molecular dynamics simulations with $N=10^8$ particles, we demonstrate that the bifurcation analysis of the initial stationary distribution is insufficient to predict either the location or the nature of the phase transition to a quasi-stationary state (qSS). Specifically, we show that for bimodal momentum distributions, the instability threshold identified by the authors does not correspond to a ferromagnetic transition; instead, the system remains in a paramagnetic state characterized by magnetization oscillations with a zero time-average. We find that the true paramagnetic-ferromagnetic transition is discontinuous (first-order) and occurs at significantly larger coupling strengths, characterized by a clear coexistence of states. These results indicate that linear bifurcation and symmetry-breaking phase transitions are distinct phenomena in long-range interacting systems, and that the former lacks the predictive power to describe the long-time fate of the system.

### [192] [Feedback percolation on complex networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22089)
*Hoseung Jang,Ginestra Bianconi,Byungjoon Min*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出反馈渗流（feedback percolation）框架，通过将微观激活概率与宏观巨分量（giant component）尺寸动态耦合，揭示了经典渗流理论中不存在的丰富动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统渗流理论（percolation theory）假设静态微观规则，无法充分描述现实复杂系统中宏观秩序主动调节局部相互作用的现象。需要建立能够反映这种宏观-微观动态耦合的理论框架。

Method: 引入反馈渗流统一框架，将微观激活概率与宏观巨分量尺寸进行动态耦合。通过分析方法和数值模拟研究不同反馈函数下的系统行为。

Result: 该反馈机制产生丰富多样的行为：爆炸性不连续跳跃（explosive discontinuous jumps）、混合相变（hybrid transitions）、极限环振荡（limit-cycle oscillations）和通向混沌的路径（routes to chaos）。这些现象在经典渗流中均不存在。

Conclusion: 宏观反馈为从自调节振荡到系统性基础设施崩溃等一系列现象提供了统一的物理机制。反馈渗流框架扩展了传统渗流理论，能够更好地描述现实复杂系统的动力学行为。

Abstract: Traditional percolation theory assumes static microscopic rules, limiting its ability to describe real-world complex systems where macroscopic order actively regulates local interactions. Here, we introduce feedback percolation, an unified framework that dynamically couples the microscopic activation probability to the macroscopic size of the giant component. We show that this simple feedback mechanism produces a rich variety of behaviors both analytically and numerically. Depending on the feedback functions, the system exhibits explosive discontinuous jumps, hybrid transitions, limit-cycle oscillations, and routes to chaos, absent in classical percolation. Our findings establish that macroscopic feedback provides a unifying physical mechanism for phenomena ranging from self-regulating oscillations to systemic infrastructure collapse.

### [193] [A Mathematical Framework for Linear Response Theory for Nonautonomous Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19509)
*Stefano Galatolo,Valerio Lucarini*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文为一大类确定性和随机非自治系统建立了严格的线性响应理论，通过将序列动力学重构为扩展序列空间上全局转移算子的不动点问题，推导出可预测小扰动对时间依赖统计状态影响的显式公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性响应理论主要研究自治系统，但物理、自然和社会科学中的许多系统本质上是非自治的，在外部强迫下随时间演化。需要理解当施加额外微小强迫时，系统时间依赖的统计特性如何变化，这一问题具有实际重要性但数学上仅针对少数特定系统/扰动进行了研究。

Method: 主要策略是将序列动力学重构为作用于扩展序列空间上全局转移算子的不动点问题。理论适用于满足特定假设的确定性和随机非自治系统，核心要素是快速记忆丧失（即沿非自治演化对初始条件的充分快速遗忘）。

Result: 推导出显式且易于实现的响应公式，用于预测小扰动对时间依赖统计状态的影响。理论在两类代表性系统上得到验证：C3扩张映射的序列组合以及噪声随机映射的序列组合，其中噪声的一致正性诱导了指数的记忆丧失。

Conclusion: 本文为相当广泛的非自治系统类别提供了严格的线性响应理论，扩展了自治系统中的标准假设，通过全局转移算子方法获得了实用的响应公式，并在典型系统类别中展示了理论的有效性。

Abstract: Linear Response theory aims to predict how added forcing alters the statistical properties of an unforced system. These kinds of questions have been studied predominantly for autonomous dynamical systems, yet many systems in the physical, natural, and social sciences are inherently nonautonomous, evolving in time under external forcings of various kinds (a canonical example being the climate system). In such settings, one would like to understand how the system's time dependent statistical properties change when additional infinitesimal forcings are applied. This question is of clear practical relevance, but from a rigorous mathematical viewpoint it has been addressed only for a few specific classes of systems/perturbations. Here we provide a rigorous linear response theory for a rather general class of deterministic and random nonautonomous systems satisfying a specific set of assumptions that in some sense extend the standard assumptions used in the autonomous setting. A central ingredient is rapid loss of memory, i.e. sufficiently fast forgetting of initial conditions along the nonautonomous evolution. Our main strategy is to reformulate the sequential dynamics as a fixed-point problem for a global transfer operator acting on an extended sequence space of measures. This yields explicit and readily implementable response formulas for predicting the effect of small perturbations on time-dependent statistical states. We illustrate the theory on two representative classes: sequential compositions of C3 expanding maps and sequential compositions of noisy random maps, where uniform positivity of the noise induces exponential loss of memory.

### [194] [Isometric Incompatibility in Growing Elastic Sheets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21112)
*Yafei Zhang,Michael Moshe,Eran Sharon*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的高斯（Gauss）和Mainardi-Codazzi-Peterson（MCP）不相容性虽然解释了自然界中的许多模式，但并未穷尽薄弹性片材中所有导致几何阻挫（frustration）的机制。需要识别新的不相容性来理解更广泛的形状形成现象。

Method: 通过表面生长（surface growth）模型研究具有正高斯曲率（positive Gaussian curvature）的弹性片材，结合实验、模拟和理论分析来验证新发现的几何不相容性。

Result: 研究发现了一种新的几何不相容性，即使在局部满足高斯和MCP相容条件的情况下，这种不相容性仍会阻止任何无拉伸配置的实现。在正高斯曲率的表面生长模型中，几何视界（geometric horizon）的形成导致阻挫，片材通过成核周期性d-cone状凹陷（d-cone-like dimples）来响应。

Conclusion: 这种对无拉伸配置的阻碍具有拓扑性质（topological），研究指出了关于阻挫起源的开放性问题，为理解薄片材形状形成机制提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Geometric incompatibility, the inability of a material's rest state to be realized in Euclidean space, underlies shape formation in natural and synthetic thin sheets. Classical Gauss and Mainardi-Codazzi-Peterson (MCP) incompatibilities explain many patterns in nature, but they do not exhaust the mechanisms that frustrate thin elastic sheets. We identify a new incompatibility that forbids any stretching-free configuration, even when the rest state of the elastic sheet locally satisfies the Gauss and MCP compatibility conditions. We demonstrate this principle in a model of surface growth with positive Gaussian curvature, where a geometric horizon forms, leading to the onset of frustration. Experiments, simulations, and theory show that the sheet responds by nucleating periodic d-cone-like dimples. We show that this obstruction to stretching-free configurations is topological, and we point to open questions concerning the origin of frustration.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用二维气泡模型（two-dimensional bubble model）进行数值模拟，系统改变系统的多分散性（polydispersity）、外驱动力（external driving force）和堆积分数（packing fraction）。

Conclusion: 研究结果为理解泡沫流动中无序性、驱动和障碍物存在之间的相互作用提供了一个综合框架，揭示了塑性流动机制从类晶体行为到类非晶行为的转变条件。

Abstract: We numerically study confined channel foam flow around an obstacle using a two-dimensional bubble model, inspired by experiments performed in the same geometry. We systematically vary the polydispersity, the external driving force, and the packing fraction of the system. Our simulations capture a broad range of plastic flow phenomenologies, from highly directional, sliding-like motion characteristic of crystalline materials to more isotropic and localized rearrangements typical of amorphous systems. We identify a threshold value of polydispersity that marks the crossover between crystalline-like and amorphous-like plasticity. In addition, we observe the existence of a critical external force, associated with the phenomenon of yield drag, above which the system reaches steady flow and below which it remains arrested. We determine a critical packing fraction above which such yield-drag behavior emerges. Our results provide a comprehensive framework for understanding the interplay between disorder, driving, and the presence of an obstacle in foam flows.

### [196] [Regulation of propulsion in assemblies of thermophoretic nanomotors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20753)
*Yoann De Figueiredo,Ulysse Delabre,Sébastien Cassagnère,Martin Romanus,Jean-Pierre Delville,Marie-Hélène Delville,Antoine Aubret*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前合成颗粒缺乏传感和适应机制，而活性颗粒（active particles）能够将能量局部转换为运动，产生异常和涌现行为。本研究旨在探索通过热泳推进和纳米构建块相结合的新型调控途径。

Method: 构建了由人工纳米马达（artificial nanomotors）组成的活性流体（active fluid），研究其三维动力学。利用激光诱导的光热效应（photo-thermal effect）驱动纳米颗粒，并在组装体中探测其自推进（self-propulsion）行为。

Result: 尽管纳米尺度存在显著热涨落（thermal fluctuations），但热泳推进强烈依赖于纳米马达的浓度，导致超快速度达~800 μm/s。这种独特行为源于纳米马达局部浓度与温度场的强耦合，反馈影响纳米颗粒的热泳迁移率（thermophoretic mobility）。

Conclusion: 通过独立建模所有热效应并考虑热泳自推进的非线性特性，研究结果为通过热过程设计和自调节三维活性流体开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Active particles locally transduce energy into motion, leading to unusual and emergent behaviors. However, current synthetic particles lack sensing and adaptation mechanisms. Here, we demonstrate a novel regulation pathway, through the combined use of thermophoretic propulsion and nanometric building blocks. We build an active fluid composed of artificial nanomotors and study its three-dimensional (3D) dynamics. We use laser-induced photo-thermal effect to actuate nanoparticles, and probe their self-propulsion within assemblies. Despite significant thermal fluctuations at the nanoscale, our results reveal a strong dependence of the thermophoretic propulsion on the concentration of nanomotors, leading to ultrafast velocities of up to ~ 800 um/s. This unique behavior originates from a strong coupling of the local concentration of nanomotors and the temperature field, which feeds back on the thermophoretic mobility of the nanoparticles. We rationalize our results from independent modeling of all thermal effects, accounting for nonlinearities of thermophoretic self-propulsion. Our results open novel routes for the design and self-regulation of 3D active fluids by thermal processes.

Motivation: 前沿聚合（FP）通过自持热波实现热固性材料的快速固化，但其传播机制随加工条件显著变化。本研究旨在探究触发方向和单体粘度（通过保持时间控制）对二环戊二烯（DCPD）前沿开环复分解聚合（FROMP）中前沿速度的影响。

Method: 通过实验研究不同保持时间下单体粘度的变化，比较顶部触发和底部触发对前沿速度的影响。同时采用包含浮力驱动平流（buoyancy-driven advection）的互补模拟来重现观察到的趋势。

Result: 实验表明，在低粘度条件下，底部触发的前沿聚合（FP）前沿传播速度显著更快（比顶部触发快约50%），这是由于浮力增强对流（buoyancy-enhanced convection）预热了前沿前方的未反应单体。随着保持时间增加，单体粘度急剧上升，抑制了对流，导致顶部和底部触发的前沿速度趋于一致。

Conclusion: 该行为反映了前沿聚合（FP）过程中热输运从对流到传导（热扩散）的转变。这些结果为理解前沿聚合中热-流体-化学耦合机制提供了新见解，并提供了通过粘度和引发几何形状调控前沿行为的策略。

Abstract: Frontal polymerization (FP) enables rapid curing of thermosets via a self-sustaining thermal wave, but its propagation mechanism can shift dramatically depending on processing conditions. In this study, we investigate the effect of trigger direction and monomer viscosity - controlled via hold time - on the front velocity in frontal ring-opening metathesis polymerization (FROMP) of dicyclopentadiene (DCPD). Our experiments reveal that at low viscosities, bottom-triggered FP fronts propagate significantly faster, ~50% faster front speed compared to top-triggered ones, driven by buoyancy-enhanced convection that preheats the unreacted monomer ahead of the front, that can have important implications for manufacturing applications. However, with increasing hold time, the monomer viscosity rises steeply, suppressing convection and causing the front velocity for top and bottom triggering to converge. This behavior reflects a convection-to-conduction (thermal-diffusion) transition in heat transport during FP. Complementary simulations incorporating buoyancy-driven advection reproduce the observed trends and highlight the importance of fluid flow in front dynamics. These results provide new insight into the coupled thermo-fluid-chemical mechanisms in FP offer strategies to tailor front behavior through viscosity and initiation geometry.

</details>


### [198] [Disorder-induced persistent random motion and trapping of microswimmers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21285)
*Mirko Residori,Sebastian Aland,Christina Kurzthaler*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过有限元模拟揭示了微游动体在二维无序多孔介质中的输运行为，发现活性、流体动力学和无序环境之间的确定性耦合足以产生有效扩散输运，并观察到显著的推拉不对称性和"跳跃-捕获"动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微生物常在受限、无序环境中运动，其中流体动力学耦合会改变其输运行为。研究旨在探究微游动体在无序多孔介质中的动力学特性，特别是活性、流体动力学和无序环境之间的相互作用如何影响输运过程。

Method: 采用广泛的有限元模拟（finite-element simulations），将微游动体建模为蠕动体（squirmer），在二维无序多孔介质中解析完整的流体动力学相互作用（full hydrodynamic interactions）。

Result: 研究发现活性、流体动力学和无序之间的确定性耦合足以产生有效扩散输运。强推体（strong pushers）和拉体（pullers）通过角落捕获或动态捕获（dynamic trapping）在介质中定位，具体取决于游动体类型和障碍物填充分数。蠕动体可从动态陷阱中逃脱，形成显著的"跳跃-捕获"动力学（hopping-and-trapping dynamics）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了推拉不对称性（pusher-puller asymmetry）在捕获概率中的存在，这种不对称性可通过短程游动体-障碍物相互作用（short-range swimmer-obstacle interactions）逆转，突显了输运过程对近场效应（near-field effects）的高度敏感性。

Abstract: Microorganisms ofter move in confined, disordered environments, where hydrodynamic couplings can modify their transport behavior. Using extensive finite-element simulations, we investigate the dynamics of microswimmers -- modeled as squirmers -- in two-dimensional disordered porous media by resolving the full hydrodynamic interactions. We reveal that the deterministic coupling between activity, hydrodynamics, and disorder is sufficient to generate effective diffusive transport. Strong pushers and pullers become localised in the porous medium either by trapping at corners or dynamic trapping, depending on swimmer type and obstacle packing fraction. Squirmers can escape from dynamic traps, leading to a prominent ``hopping-and--trapping'' dynamics. Strikingly, we find a pusher-puller asymmetry in the trapping probability that can be reversed by short-range swimmer-obstacle interactions, highlighting the sensitivity of transport to near-field effects.

### [199] [Non-Hermitian chiral surface waves in disordered odd solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21312)
*Cheng-Tai Lee,Tomer Markovich*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了扭矩驱动无序奇弹性固体中的非厄米手性表面波（NHCSW），发现其具有更强的表面局域性和稳定的边界速度，为通过主动扭矩控制NHCSW提供了新策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性表面波（chiral surface waves）最初在量子系统中发现，最近在经典超材料中的奇弹性（odd elasticity）条件下出现。然而，现有研究主要关注有序结构，无序材料是否能支持非厄米手性表面波（NHCSW）尚不清楚。扭矩驱动无序奇弹性固体在生物凝胶和磁性胶体凝胶等系统中广泛存在，需要探索其NHCSW特性。

Method: 采用扭矩驱动无序奇弹性固体（torque-driven disordered odd solids）的最小模型进行研究。这种模型适用于从细胞骨架等生物凝胶到磁性胶体凝胶等多种系统，通过分析边界扭矩与奇弹性的内在相互作用来探索NHCSW特性。

Result: 研究发现扭矩驱动无序奇弹性固体具有独特的NHCSW，表现出比先前晶格模型更强的表面局域性和稳定的边界速度。这些特征源于扭矩驱动奇弹性固体中边界扭矩与奇弹性的内在相互作用（intrinsic interplay）。

Conclusion: 研究结果为通过主动扭矩（active torques）控制非厄米手性表面波提供了新策略，揭示了无序奇弹性材料中NHCSW的独特性质，扩展了对非厄米手性表面波在复杂材料中行为的理解。

Abstract: Chiral surface waves are surface-localized modes that propagate unidirectionally along a boundary, enabling directed transport and minimal back-scattering. While first identified in quantum systems, they were recently shown to emerge in classical metamaterials in the presence of `odd elasticity'. Owing to the non-reciprocality of odd elasticity, these waves exhibit growing amplitudes during propagation, reminiscent of the non-Hermitian skin effect. To date, studies of odd elastic systems have mainly focused on ordered structures. Whether structurally-disordered materials can host non-Hermitian chiral surface waves (NHCSW) remains unexplored. We address this question using a minimal model of torque-driven disordered odd solids. Such solids are abundant, from biological gels such as the cytoskeleton driven by motor-proteins to synthesized systems such as magnetic colloidal gels. We find that torque-driven disordered odd solids have unique NHCSW with stronger surface localization and stable boundary velocity, in contrast to previous lattice models of odd solids. These distinct features stem from an intrinsic interplay between boundary torques and odd elasticity in torque-driven odd solids. Our results offer a new strategy to control NHCSW using active torques.

### [200] [Deformed states in paraelectric and ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21338)
*Oleg D. Lavrentovich*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 这篇综述探讨了取向有序材料（从固体铁磁体、铁电体到液晶）中空间变化矢量序参量的形成机制，重点分析了分子形状、手性和极性以及空间限制如何诱导液晶中的变形平衡态和多畴态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解从固体铁磁体、铁电体到液晶等具有取向有序的材料中，由内在因素（如构建单元形状）或限制几何结构引起的空间变化矢量序参量的形成机制。

Method: 通过综述分析，探讨分子形状、手性（chirality）、极性（polarity）和空间限制（spatial confinement）如何诱导顺电（paraelectric）和铁电（ferroelectric）向列相液晶中的变形平衡态和多畴态。

Result: 发现手性分子可替代顺电向列相中能量代价高的展曲（splay）和弯曲（bend）变形，而铁电向列相中的宇称破缺（parity breaking）则响应退极化场（depolarization field）。两种液晶都表现出展曲抵消效应（splay cancellation effect）。

Conclusion: 分子特性和空间限制共同决定了液晶中序参量的变形模式，包括宇称破缺、展曲、弯曲和扭曲-弯曲（twist-bend）变形，这些机制在不同类型的向列相液晶中表现出相似性和差异性。

Abstract: Ground states of materials with orientational order ranging from solid ferromagnets and ferroelectrics to liquid crystals often contain spatially varying vector-like order parameter caused by inner factors such as the shape of building units or by the geometry of confinement. This review presents examples of how the shapes, chirality, and polarity of molecules and spatial confinement induce deformed equilibrium and polydomain states with parity breaking, splay, bend, and twist-bend deformations of the order parameter in paraelectric and ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals. Parity breaking results either from chirality of the constituent molecules, as a replacement of energetically costly splay and bend in paraelectric nematics, or in response to depolarization field in the ferroelectric nematic. Both paraelectric and ferroelectric nematics exhibit a splay cancellation effect, in which the elastic and electrostatic energies of splay along one direction are reduced by an additional splay along orthogonal directions.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确描述参考系统是液态理论中研究更复杂系统的核心任务。现有方法在描述硬球流体在尺寸多分散硬球随机多孔介质中的热力学性质时，需要扩展到更高的基质堆积分数范围。

Method: 采用标度粒子理论（scaled particle theory, SPT）推导了硬球流体在尺寸多分散硬球随机多孔介质中热力学性质的完全解析描述。计算了广泛多孔基质参数下的化学势，包括基质堆积分数、多分散度和粒径分布。

Conclusion: 基于标度粒子理论建立的完全解析框架能够准确描述硬球流体在尺寸多分散硬球随机多孔介质中的热力学性质，特别是在较高基质堆积分数范围内与现有数值方法和理论结果吻合良好。

Abstract: Accurate descriptions of reference systems are a central task in liquid-state theories for the study of more complex systems. Using scaled particle theory (SPT), we derive a fully analytical description of the thermodynamic properties of a hard-sphere (HS) fluid confined in size-polydisperse HS random porous media, extending the existing approaches to higher matrix packing fractions. We calculate chemical potentials for a wide range of porous-matrix parameters, including the matrix packing fraction, degree of polydispersity, and particle-size distributions. Within the proposed framework, our results show excellent agreement with available Monte Carlo simulations and previous integral-equation theories over a broad range of matrix packing fractions, $0.1 \leqslant η_0 \leqslant 0.3$, and degrees of polydispersity.

### [202] [Emergent single-species non-reciprocity from bistable chemical dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21863)
*Jakob Metson,Ramin Golestanian*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在单物种化学活性胶体悬浮液中实现非互易（non-reciprocal）相互作用的新机制，通过非线性化学反应的双稳态化学动力学，使胶体能够动态切换为化学物质的有效生产者或消费者，从而产生丰富的涌现动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂系统中涌现对称性（emergent symmetries）的出现为设计和控制奇异相行为提供了机会，特别是通过利用相关的动力学对称破缺（dynamical symmetry breaking）。本文旨在探索化学活性胶体中非互易相互作用的涌现机制。

Method: 研究采用由半透性囊泡（semi-permeable vesicles）构成的单物种化学活性胶体悬浮液，囊泡内封装了催化非线性化学反应的酶。通过双稳态化学动力学（bistable chemical dynamics），胶体反应室根据内外化学浓度选择值，可作为化学物质的净生产者或消费者。

Result: 胶体能够自发且可逆地在有效消费者或生产者之间切换，从而以非互易方式动态切换忽略、吸引、排斥和追逐彼此的行为。通过调控参数可诱导化学动力学分岔（bifurcations），实现对相互作用模式的稳健控制，并产生丰富的涌现动力学，如自发的多体极性集群（polar swarming）。

Conclusion: 该机制展示了化学活性胶体系统中非互易相互作用的涌现能力，为通过操纵化学动力学参数控制相互作用模式和集体行为提供了新途径，具有设计复杂系统相行为的潜力。

Abstract: The appearance of emergent symmetries in complex systems with components that can form composite units provides us with opportunities for design and control of exotic phase behaviour, for example by exploiting the dynamical symmetry breaking associated with them. We present a novel mechanism for the emergence of non-reciprocal interactions in a single-species suspension of chemically active colloids made out of semi-permeable vesicles, which encapsulate enzymes that catalyze a non-linear chemical reaction. Bistable chemical dynamics enables the colloidal reaction chamber to act as a net producer or consumer of a chemical, depending on the selected values of the chemical concentrations inside and around it. Since the internal chemical state of the colloid depends on the dynamic chemical concentrations rather than the material parameters, two identically produced colloids can present different effective chemical interactions within the same system upon responding to the corresponding gradients via diffusiophoresis. Furthermore, the colloids can spontaneously and reversibly switch between being effective consumers or producers. As a consequence, the colloids can dynamically switch between ignoring, attracting, repelling, and chasing each other, in a non-reciprocal manner. This flexibility can be exploited by manipulation of tuning parameters to induce bifurcations in the chemical dynamics, resulting in a robust control over the interaction motifs, and rich emergent dynamics such as spontaneous many-body polar swarming.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Actin flow in the cortical cytoskeleton underneath the cell membrane generates mechanical stresses that shape the cell surface. We study this mechanism using an hydrodynamic model of a compressible active gel polymerising at the membrane and undergoing turnover. We determine how actin flow, density relaxation and friction of actin with the membrane generate stress on a corrugated membrane at the linear order in deformation. Analytical solutions in limiting regimes, combined with finite element methods in the general case, provide a map of normal and tangential stresses as functions of compressibility, interfacial friction and actin turnover, and determine the conditions under which actin polymerisation can render the membrane linearly unstable. The non-linear regime is also briefly discussed.

### [204] [Short-range electrostatic screening in ionic liquids as inferred by direct force measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22175)
*Benjamin Cross,Léo Garcia,Elisabeth Charlaix,Patrick Kékicheff*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过两种互补的表面力仪（Surface Force Apparatuses）揭示了离子液体（ionic liquids）中表观长程相互作用的动力学本质，发现测量速度对观察到的相互作用范围有决定性影响，从而解决了关于静电屏蔽范围的理论与实验矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前关于离子液体（ILs）中长程相互作用的实验报告与理论预测和数值模拟存在矛盾。为了解释文献中关于静电屏蔽（electrostatic screening）实验范围（声称比理论预测大几个数量级）的差异，需要深入研究限制在云母和硼硅酸盐表面之间的离子液体相互作用。

Method: 使用两种互补的先进表面力仪（Surface Force Apparatuses）研究限制在云母和硼硅酸盐表面之间的离子液体对相互作用。实验考虑了不同的限制几何结构（交叉圆柱、球-平面）、曲率半径（cm-mm）和测量技术（逐步vs连续接近），并实现了低至9 pm/s的速度和长达90秒的平衡时间。

Result: 无论几何结构和测量技术如何，都观察到两种始终存在的力机制：在小表面间距下，振荡力反映离子液体的结构化和分层；在此间隙外，相互作用是单调排斥的。两种机制的空间范围和力大小都关键依赖于运动条件。快速表面位移产生长程相互作用（超过数十个离子尺寸），造成异常欠屏蔽（anomalous underscreening）的假象；而逐渐减慢的速度会缩小排斥力的幅度和范围，其衰减长度最终收敛到与泊松-玻尔兹曼理论（Poisson-Boltzmann theory）一致的有限离子尺寸屏蔽长度。

Conclusion: 这些发现最终解决了关于力测量的十年争议，揭示了丰富的非平衡动力学（out-of-equilibrium dynamics）。从表观长程到短程屏蔽的转变在时间上跨越近两个数量级，显示出类似于老化现象（aging phenomena）的缓慢弛豫动力学。在测量过程中接近热力学平衡（thermodynamic equilibrium）至关重要，而流体动力学对净力的贡献在弛豫跨越时间尺度时尤为关键。

Abstract: Previous experimental reports of long-range interactions in ionic liquids (ILs) stand in contradiction with theoretical predictions and numerical simulations. To provide insights into the literature discrepancies regarding the experimental ranges of electrostatic screening, claimed with orders of magnitude larger, the interactions between pairs of mica and borosilicate surfaces confining ILs are investigated by two complementary advanced Surface Force Apparatuses. Regardless of differences in confinement geometries (crossed-cylinders, sphere-flat), radii of curvature (cm-mm), and measurement techniques (stepwise vs continuous approach), two ever present force regimes are evidenced. At small surface separations, oscillatory forces reflect IL structuration and layering, while outside this gap, the interaction is monotonic repulsive. In both regimes the spatial extent and force magnitude depend critically on motion conditions, as demonstrated by achieving velocities as low as 9 pm/s with equilibration times up to 90 s. At large separations, fast surface displacements generate long-range interactions (over tens of ion size) creating the illusion of anomalous underscreening, whereas increasingly slow ones shrink both magnitude and range of the repulsion with decay-lengths converging ultimately to a screening length consistent with Poisson-Boltzmann theory with finite ion sizes. The transition from apparent long-range to short-range screening unfolds over nearly two orders of magnitude in time, revealing slow relaxation dynamics reminiscent of aging phenomena. These findings definitely resolve a decade-old controversy on force measurements and reveal rich out-of-equilibrium dynamics. The hydrodynamic contribution to the net force is admittedly crucial to be reduced especially when relaxations span decades in time, but approaching thermodynamic equilibrium during measurements proves essential.

</details>

### [205] [Optically Activated Superconductivity in MgB2 via Electroluminescent GaP Inhomogeneous Phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20719)
*Yao Qi,Duo Chen,Qingyu Hai,Xiaoyan Li,Xiaopeng Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过引入GaP电致发光非均匀相并原位激活其发光，实现了MgB2超导性能的可调控增强，揭示了界面光-声子-电子协同机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索通过引入电致发光非均匀相来调控MgB2超导性能的新策略，旨在不改变主要化学成分的情况下增强传统声子介导超导系统的性能。

Method: 将GaP电致发光非均匀相引入MgB2中，并在测量过程中通过施加偏置电流原位激活其发光，利用界面产生的局域光场和电磁近场与Mg-B层的E2g声子模式耦合。

Result: 实验观察到界面光场驱动机制显著增强了电子-声子耦合常数λ，使超导转变温度Tc最大提升约1.4K；同时GaP非均匀相的纳米级分散分布增加了临界电流密度约69%（20K自场下）和Hirr约31.5%。

Conclusion: 电致发光非均匀相通过"原位近场增强配对"和"结构钉扎辅助磁通优化"两种机制协同增强MgB2超导性能，为构建可由内部光场激活的超导材料系统提供了新的设计策略。

Abstract: Experimental results demonstrate a viable strategy for tuning the superconducting properties of MgB2 through the incorporation of an electroluminescent inhomogeneous phase, revealing an interfacial light-phonon-electron synergistic mechanism that enhances superconductivity in conventional phonon-mediated systems. By introducing GaP electroluminescent inhomogeneous phases into MgB2 and activating their emission in situ through the application of a bias current during measurements, it is experimentally observed that the localized optical field and electromagnetic near field generated at the interface can effectively couple with the E2g phonon mode of the Mg-B layers, thereby significantly enhancing the electron-phonon interaction. As the emission intensity of the inhomogeneous phase increases, the interface light-field-driven mechanism markedly enhances the electron-phonon coupling constant lambda and leads to a gradual increase in the superconducting transition temperature Tc (with a maximum enhancement of approximately 1.4 K), enabling a tunable enhancement of the superconducting pairing channel in MgB2 without altering its primary chemical composition. In addition, the nanoscale dispersed distribution of the GaP inhomogeneous phase is expected to induce fine-scale defects that act as effective pinning centers and promote densification, resulting in an increase of the critical current density by approximately 69% at 20 K in the self-field and an enhancement of Hirr by about 31.5%. These results indicate that the electroluminescent inhomogeneous phase can synergistically enhance the superconducting performance of MgB2 through two mechanisms: "in situ near-field-enhanced pairing" and "structural pinning-assisted flux optimization", thereby providing a new design strategy for constructing superconducting material systems that can be activated by internal optical fields.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用电子束光刻（electron-beam lithography）和氯基干法刻蚀（chlorine-based dry etching）制备基于Nb/NbN和Nb/TiN超导堆栈的多层三维纳米桥结构。高电阻率氮化物层定义几何弱连接，顶部Nb层设定堆栈的整体临界温度和薄膜质量。

Conclusion: 通过结合材料选择性和三维几何结构，该平台为适用于超导电子学的无氧化物约瑟夫森结提供了一条可扩展的制备路线。

Abstract: We report the realization of multilayer three-dimensional nanobridge Josephson junctions based on Nb/NbN and Nb/TiN superconducting stacks fabricated using electron-beam lithography and chlorine-based dry etching. In this architecture, a high-resistivity nitride layer defines the geometrical weak link, while the top Nb layer sets the overall critical temperature and film quality of the stack. This multilayer design enables engineering of the superconducting gap and proximity effects without relying on focused ion beam milling or oxide tunnel barriers. The devices are successfully integrated into dc SQUIDs, demonstrating reliable circuit-level operation. By combining material selectivity with three-dimensional geometry, this platform provides a scalable route toward oxide-free Josephson junctions suitable for superconducting electronics.

### [207] [Pressure-Invariant Isotope Effect as Evidence for Electronically Driven Intertwined Order in Pr$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20871)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索三层Ruddlesden-Ppper镍酸盐中自旋密度波（SDW）转变的物理起源，特别是通过压力调控下的氧同位素效应来区分电子与声子机制对SDW转变的贡献。

Method: 采用μ子自旋转动（muon-spin rotation）技术测量Pr₄Ni₃O₁₀在不同静水压力下，¹⁶O和¹⁸O同位素样品的自旋密度波（SDW）转变温度TSDW及其压力依赖性。

Result: 常压下SDW转变存在有限同位素位移：¹⁶TSDW=158.04(5) K，¹⁸TSDW=159.81(6) K。压力下两种同位素成分的TSDW以几乎相同速率线性下降（d¹⁶TSDW/dp=-4.93(5) K/GPa，d¹⁸TSDW/dp=-4.90(7) K/GPa），同位素位移在压缩下基本保持不变。

Conclusion: 同位素效应未随压力增强表明SDW转变主要源于电子机制，这与最近的非弹性X射线散射结果一致，暗示三层RP镍酸盐中存在由强自旋相互作用稳定的新型交织序（intertwined order）体系。

Abstract: We report muon-spin rotation measurements of the pressure dependence of the oxygen-isotope ($^{16}$O/$^{18}$O) effect on the spin-density wave (SDW) transition in the trilayer Ruddlesden-Popper nickelate Pr$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$. At ambient pressure, the SDW transition shows a finite isotope shift, with $^{16}T_{\rm SDW}=158.04(5)$ K and $^{18}T_{\rm SDW}=159.81(6)$ K. Under hydrostatic pressure, $T_{\rm SDW}$ decreases linearly at nearly identical rates for the two isotope compositions, ${\rm d}\,^{16}T_{\rm SDW}/{\rm d}p=-4.93(5)$ K/GPa and ${\rm d}\,^{18}T_{\rm SDW}/{\rm d}p=-4.90(7)$ K/GPa, such that the isotope shift remains essentially unchanged under compression. The absence of pressure enhancement of the isotope effect points to a predominantly electronic origin of the SDW transition and is consistent with recent inelastic x-ray scattering results, suggesting a new regime of intertwined order in trilayer RP nickelates, which is stabilized by strong spin interactions.

### [208] [Hopping mechanism for superconductivity revealed by Density Functional Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21417)
*Jose A. Alarco,Ian D. R. Mackinnon*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文通过分析MgB2等超导材料中余弦形能带（cosine-shaped bands）的非对称性，揭示了其与超导能隙（superconducting gap）和费米面嵌套（Fermi surface nesting）的强相关性，为理解多元素化合物的超导机制提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在深入分析MgB2等超导材料中基于密度泛函理论（DFT）计算出现的余弦形能带结构，特别是其非对称性特征与超导机制之间的关联，为解释多元素化合物的超导性提供理论基础。

Method: 采用沿倒易空间（reciprocal space）高对称性G-A方向平行路径的能带计算，结合紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）方程（包括描述余弦形能带非对称性的修正项），并与无限线性原子链中两个s态布洛赫轨道（Bloch orbitals）的久期方程（secular equation）进行比较。

Result: 研究发现余弦形能带的非对称性与超导能隙和费米面嵌套强烈相关，折叠费米面（folded Fermi surfaces）与电子能带交叉（electronic band crossings）为电子提供了改变速度或动量的途径，导致嵌套相干行为的散射和破坏。该非对称性特征在CaC6和LaH10等其他二元超导体中也得到确认。

Conclusion: 余弦形能带非对称性的确定与跳跃机制（hopping mechanism）相关，这一发现对于解释许多多元素化合物的超导机制具有重要意义，为理解超导性中的电子配对和相干行为破坏提供了关键见解。

Abstract: Cosine-shaped bands that occur in DFT-based electronic band structures for MgB2 are further analyzed with calculations along reciprocal directions parallel to the high symmetry G-A direction at regular intervals along G-M. Band degeneracies in close proximity to the Fermi surface (offset from G-A), do not emulate the degenerate bands along G-A. At the Fermi surface, bands split and align favorably for electron-hole pairing with the nodal inflection point located at the Fermi level. Tight-binding equations, including corrections to describe the observed asymmetry of a cosine-shaped band, can be compared to the secular equation obtained for Bloch orbitals of an infinite linear chain of atoms with two s-states. These equations show unequivocally that a hopping mechanism is associated with the cosine-shaped band asymmetry, an asymmetry strongly correlated with the superconducting gap and Fermi surface nesting. Intersections of folded Fermi surfaces and electronic band crossings provide avenues or pathways for electrons from the nested collection to drastically change velocity or momentum, resulting in scattering and disruption of nested, coherent behavior. Determination of cosine band asymmetry, also established for other two element superconductors such as CaC6 and LaH10, is relevant for interpretation of superconductivity mechanisms in many other multi-element compounds.

</details>
