### [210] [Transparency-controlled multiple charge transfer in superconducting junctions with local shot-noise scanning tunneling spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22145)
*Yudai Sato,Maialen Ortego Larrazabal,Jian-Feng Ge,Ingmar Swart,Doohee Cho,Wolfgang Belzig,Juan Carlos Cuevas,Milan P. Allan,Jiasen Niu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过新开发的放大器实现了扫描隧道显微镜（STM）的散粒噪声测量，在Pb(111)表面观测到随着结透明度增加，电荷输运从单电子隧穿向多电荷转移机制的演变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导结中的电荷输运由安德烈夫反射（Andreev reflections）主导，包括多重安德烈夫反射（multiple Andreev reflections）过程。散粒噪声（shot noise）可直接量化多重电荷转移，但提取的有效电荷随结透明度（transparency）变化，而系统控制透明度在实验上具有挑战性。

Method: 研究采用新开发的放大器实现了噪声扫描隧道显微镜（noise-STM）测量，能够在Pb(111)表面于2.2K温度下进行可调透明度的散粒噪声测量，从而访问不同的透明度区域。

Result: 实验观测到随着透明度增加，散粒噪声从单电子隧穿（single electron tunneling）区域演变为多电荷转移（multiple charge transfer）区域。这些结果与单通道系统（single-channel system）的安德烈夫反射和多重安德烈夫反射理论模拟在定量上一致。

Conclusion: 研究确立了结透明度作为控制电荷输演变的关键参数，并证明噪声-STM是一个强大的平台，可在原子尺度上以可控的结透明度研究微观电荷输运机制。

Abstract: Charge transport in superconducting junctions at finite voltages is governed by Andreev reflections, including multiple Andreev reflections, which are processes that enable multiple charge transfer, a hallmark that shot noise can directly quantify. Since the effective charge extracted from shot noise measurements varies with the transparency of the junction, systematic control of transparency is essential but experimentally challenging. Here, we present shot noise scanning tunneling microscopy measurements enabled by a newly developed amplifier, allowing access to different transparency regimes. We perform shot noise measurements on Pb(111) with tunable transparency at 2.2 K and observe that the shot noise evolves from a single electron tunneling regime to multiple charge transfer regime as transparency increases. Our results are quantitatively consistent with theoretical simulations of Andreev reflections and multiple Andreev reflections for a single-channel system. These results establish junction transparency as the key parameter governing the evolution of charge transport and demonstrate that noise-STM is a powerful platform for investigating microscopic charge transport mechanisms with controlled junction transparency at the atomic scale.

### [211] [Thermodynamic evidence for a pressure-driven crossover from strong- to weak-coupling superconductivity in Pb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22178)
*Rustem Khasanov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过μ子自旋旋转/弛豫（muon-spin-rotation/relaxation）测量，报告了元素铅（Pb）在高达约2.3 GPa静水压下的热力学临界场B_c，发现B_c(0)的压力依赖性更接近超导能隙Δ(0)而非转变温度T_c，为铅中压力驱动的强耦合到弱耦合超导性（strong- to weak-coupling superconductivity）交叉提供了热力学证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热力学临界场B_c直接关联超导凝聚能，但其压力依赖性研究远少于转变温度T_c。该研究旨在通过高压下B_c的精确测量，揭示铅中超导耦合强度随压力的演化规律。

Method: 采用μ子自旋旋转/弛豫（muon-spin-rotation/relaxation）技术，测量元素铅在高达约2.3 GPa静水压下的热力学临界场B_c。通过中间态（intermediate state）的磁场分布确定B_c(T)，并提取不同压力下的B_c(0)。

Result: B_c(0)的压力依赖性比T_c更接近超导能隙Δ(0)。在较高压力下，B_c(0)和T_c的对数压力导数趋于一致，表明耦合强度比α=Δ(0)/k_BT_c几乎不随压力变化。

Conclusion: 该结果为铅中压力驱动的从强耦合到弱耦合超导性（strong- to weak-coupling superconductivity）的交叉提供了热力学证据，揭示了B_c(0)与Δ(0)的紧密关联性。

Abstract: The thermodynamic critical field $B_{\rm c}$ provides direct access to the superconducting condensation energy, yet its pressure dependence has been studied much less extensively than that of the transition temperature. Here, muon-spin-rotation/relaxation measurements of the thermodynamic critical field $B_{\rm c}$ of elemental Pb under hydrostatic pressure up to $\simeq2.3$ GPa are reported. From the magnetic-field distribution in the intermediate state, $B_{\rm c}(T)$ is determined and $B_{\rm c}(0)$ is extracted at different pressures. In combination with previously reported high-pressure data for $B_{\rm c}$ and $T_{\rm c}$, it is shown that the pressure dependence of $B_{\rm c}(0)$ follows that of the superconducting gap $Δ(0)$ more closely than that of the transition temperature $T_{\rm c}$. At higher pressures, the logarithmic pressure derivatives of $B_{\rm c}(0)$ and $T_{\rm c}$ are found to converge, indicating that the coupling strengths ratio $α=Δ(0)/k_{\rm B}T_{\rm c}$ becomes nearly pressure independent. This behavior is interpreted as thermodynamic evidence for a pressure-driven crossover from strong- to weak-coupling superconductivity in Pb.

### [212] [Conflict Avoidance in Pedestrian Merging in Controlled Experiments by Variance Indicator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20593)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要依赖密度、平均速度或流量指标，难以区分几何转向效应与交互作用引起的波动，特别是T型交叉口转向角度依赖的机制尚未解决。

Method: 通过分析300多个在L型走廊（仅转向）和T型走廊（转向与汇合）的控制实验，使用基于Voronoi的速度方差$V_s$和速度矢量方差$V_v$系统比较几何与交互效应。

Result: $V_s$有效捕捉交互驱动的不稳定性，而$V_v$反映几何引起的方向调整；比较揭示了不同的波动机制，并识别出90°转角附近存在临界转变。

Abstract: Pedestrian congestion at corridor intersections often originates from localized fluctuations in motion rather than from a macroscopic collapse of flow. Understanding pedestrian instability at corridor intersections remains challenging because existing studies mainly rely on density, average speed, or flow-based measures and limited datasets, making it difficult to separate geometric turning effects from interaction induced fluctuations in merging flows. In particular, the mechanism underlying the turning angle dependence in T junctions has not been resolved. Here, we analyze more than 300 controlled experiments conducted in L corridors with turning only and T corridors with turning and merging. Using Voronoi-based speed variance $V_s$ and velocity variance $V_v$, we systematically compare geometric and interaction effects. $V_s$ effectively captures interaction driven instability, while $V_v$ reflects directional adjustments due to geometry. The comparison reveals distinct fluctuation mechanisms and identifies a critical transition near $90°$, demonstrating the advantage of variance-based indicators for diagnosing pedestrian dynamics.

### [213] [Physical manifestation of replica symmetry breaking in a quantum glass of bosons with off-diagonal disorder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20949)
*Anna M. Piekarska,Tadeusz K. Kopeć*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析具有随机跃迁的强相互作用玻色子系统中出现的非对角玻璃态（off-diagonal glassiness），建立了基于相位的玻璃序与可测量的压缩率之间的直接对应关系，为实验识别此类量子玻璃相提供了新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在相互作用玻色子系统中，由无序和阻挫导致的玻璃态涉及量子自由度（局部相位），但实验识别困难，因为需要极长测量时间或难以捉摸的Edwards-Anderson序参量。此外，相位的非对角特性使其更难通过典型可观测量捕捉。

Method: 研究采用从自旋玻璃理论借鉴的框架，包括在一阶副本对称破缺（one-step RSB）方案内使用副本技巧（replica trick），分析具有随机跃迁的强相互作用玻色子系统。该方法能够获得玻璃相中有意义的结果，并表征序参量、RSB结构、慢弛豫和压缩率。

Result: 研究发现玻璃相是可压缩的，这将其与莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）区分开来。研究建立了基于相位的玻璃序与可测量的密度热力学可观测量之间的直接对应关系，表明非对角玻璃态表现出副本对称破缺（replica symmetry breaking, RSB）。

Conclusion: 粒子系统中的玻璃态可以通过压缩率测量进行实验识别，例如探测密度涨落或粒子数对囚禁势的响应。该研究为实验观测量子玻璃相提供了基于热力学观测量的实用方法。

Abstract: Glassiness occurs when disorder and frustration cause local degrees of freedom to freeze despite the lack of long-range order. In systems of interacting bosons, such glassiness may involve a purely quantum degree of freedom$\unicode{x2014}$local phases of particle wave functions$\unicode{x2014}$partly analogous to spins in spin glasses. However, experimental identification of such phases is difficult because it requires prohibitively long measurement times or recourse to the elusive Edwards-Anderson order parameter. Moreover, the off-diagonal character of the phase makes it seemingly even harder to capture via typical observables. To address this issue, we study a system of strongly interacting bosons with random hoppings that features off-diagonal glassiness exhibiting replica symmetry breaking (RSB). We find that the glass phase is compressible, which distinguishes it from the Mott insulator. Thus, we establish a direct correspondence between phase-based glassy order and a measurable density-based thermodynamic observable. We use a framework adopted from spin glasses, including the replica trick within the one-step RSB scheme, to obtain meaningful results in the glass phase and to characterize the order parameters, RSB structure, slow relaxation, and compressibility. Glassiness in particle systems could thus be experimentally identified via measurements of compressibility, such as probing density fluctuations or the particle-number response to a trapping potential.

</details>


### [214] [Signatures of Nonergodicity in Sparse Random Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21369)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相互作用多体系统中稀疏性的普遍存在，促使研究者探究具有在位无序的稀疏随机矩阵的谱统计特性。这有助于理解此类系统中的局域化-退局域化转变机制。

Method: 采用数值方法分析基态统计性质以识别安德森转变。通过解析推导能量矩（energy moments）并计算偏移峰度（shifted kurtosis），估算局域化-退局域化转变的临界稀疏阈值。

Result: 体谱中的短程能量关联表明无限温度下的安德森转变与量子相变（quantum phase transition）一致。体谱中的长程能量关联揭示了Thouless能量尺度，表明在退局域化相中存在广泛的非遍历（nonergodic）区域。

Conclusion: 研究证实了通过基态统计性质识别安德森转变的可行性，并揭示了退局域化相中存在的非遍历区域，为理解稀疏相互作用系统中的局域化现象提供了新视角。

Abstract: The prevalence of sparsity in interacting many-body systems motivates an investigation into the spectral statistics of sparse random matrices with on-site disorder. We numerically demonstrate that the Anderson transition can be identified through the statistical properties of the ground state. By analytically deriving the energy moments and calculating the shifted kurtosis, we estimate the critical sparsity threshold for this localization-delocalization transition. The short-range energy correlation in the bulk indicates that the Anderson transition at infinite temperature coincides with the quantum phase transition. Furthermore, long-range energy correlations in the bulk spectrum reveal a Thouless energy scale, suggesting a broad nonergodic regime within the delocalized phase.

### [215] [Impact of heavy-tailed synaptic strength distributions on self-sustained activity in networks of spiking neurons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21781)
*Ralf Tönjes,Chunming Zheng,Wenping Cui,Benjamin Lindner*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究使用随机平均场理论分析随机耦合二次整合发放神经元的稳态活动，发现高斯和柯西耦合下均可出现低活动与高活动状态的双稳态。柯西耦合系统存在定向渗流阈值，但转变类型取决于网络的兴奋-抑制平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在分析随机耦合二次整合发放（quadratic integrate-and-fire）神经元中稳态活动的特性，特别关注高斯（Gaussian）随机耦合和柯西（Cauchy）随机耦合这两种代表性系统，它们分别对应轻尾和重尾突触强度分布。

Method: 采用随机平均场理论（stochastic mean-field theory）分析随机耦合的二次整合发放神经元系统，分别研究高斯随机耦合和柯西随机耦合两种情况。

Result: 高斯和柯西耦合下，可兴奋神经元均可能出现低活动与高活动状态的双稳态（bistability）。柯西耦合系统中存在定向渗流阈值（directed percolation threshold），超过该阈值时活动可从少数发放单元渗流至整个网络。转变类型（连续或间断）取决于网络的兴奋-抑制不平衡程度。

Conclusion: 柯西耦合系统存在定向渗流阈值，与先前关于重尾突触强度分布的数值结果一致。然而，高斯耦合系统及带有附加加性噪声的柯西耦合系统在热力学极限下缺乏渗流转变。

Abstract: We analyze states of stationary activity in randomly coupled quadratic integrate-and-fire neurons using stochastic mean-field theory. Specifically, we consider the two cases of Gaussian random coupling and Cauchy random coupling, which are representative of systems with light- or with heavy-tailed synaptic strength distributions. For both, Gaussian and Cauchy coupling, bistability between a low activity and a high activity state of self-sustained firing is possible in excitable neurons. In the system with Cauchy coupling we find analytically a directed percolation threshold, i.e., above a critical value of the synaptic strength, activity percolates through the whole network starting from a few spiking units only. The existence of the directed percolation threshold is in agreement with previous numerical results in the literature for integrate-and-fire neurons with heavy-tailed synaptic strength distribution. However, we have found that the transition can be continuous or discontinuous, depending on the excitatory-inhibitory imbalance in the network. Networks with Gaussian coupling and networks with Cauchy coupling and additional additive noise lack the percolation transition in the thermodynamic limit.

### [216] [Many-body mobility edges in one dimension revealed by efficient and interpretable feature-based learning with Kolmogorov-Arnold Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21807)
*Siqi Dai,Tian-Cheng Yi,Xingbo Wei,Yunbo Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于物理启发特征和Kolmogorov-Arnold网络（KAN）分类器的机器学习框架，用于识别一维无序晶格中相互作用费米子系统的多体局域化（MBL）转变。该方法通过四个物理可观测量构建紧凑特征表示，实现了高精度分类，并揭示了清晰的能谱分辨相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法基于物理启发的机器学习框架，构建了包含四个物理可观测量（inverse participation ratio, Shannon entropy, many-body hybridization parameter, mean level-spacing ratio）的紧凑特征表示。使用这些特征训练Kolmogorov-Arnold网络（KAN）分类器，在弱无序和强无序区域的本征态上进行训练。

Result: 训练后的KAN分类器验证准确率超过99.9%，与直接在高维波函数数据上训练的卷积神经网络相当，但输入维度显著降低且训练时间大幅缩短。应用该分类器于整个能谱，获得了能谱分辨的相图，揭示了清晰的多体迁移率边（many-body mobility edge），并提供了一致的临界无序强度估计。

Conclusion: 基于特征的KAN学习方法为识别多体局域化转变提供了一种高效、可扩展且可解释的方法论。该方法具有固有可扩展性，可在不改变整体架构的情况下系统性地将额外物理相关可观测量纳入特征空间，为基于原始数据的神经网络方法提供了实用的替代方案。

Abstract: We study the many-body localization (MBL) transition in interacting fermionic systems on disordered one-dimensional lattices using a physics-informed machine-learning framework. Instead of feeding full many-body wave functions into the model, we construct a compact feature representation based on four physically motivated observables: the inverse participation ratio, the Shannon entropy, the many-body hybridization parameter, and the mean level-spacing ratio. These quantities capture complementary aspects of localization, entanglement, and spectral correlations, and are used to train a Kolmogorov--Arnold Network (KAN) classifier on eigenstates deep in the weak and strong disorder regimes. The resulting KAN achieves a validation accuracy exceeding $99.9\%$, comparable to that of convolutional neural networks trained directly on high-dimensional wave-function data, while requiring substantially reduced input dimensionality and significantly shorter training time. Applying the trained classifier across the full energy spectrum yields energy-resolved phase diagrams that reveal a clear many-body mobility edge and provide a consistent estimate of the critical disorder strength. The approach is inherently extensible: additional physically relevant observables can be incorporated into the feature space in a systematic manner without altering the overall architecture. Our results demonstrate that feature-based learning with KAN provides an efficient, scalable, and interpretable methodology for identifying many-body localization transitions, offering a practical alternative to raw-data-based neural network approaches.

### [217] [Semiclassical picture of the Heisenberg spin glass in two dimensions: from weak localization to hydrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22077)
*Giacomo Bracci-Testasecca,Jacopo Niedda,Aldo Coraggio,Roderich Moessner,Antonello Scardicchio*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过半经典展开方法分析二维海森堡自旋玻璃模型，发现自旋波激发性质取决于重整化群意义下相关性的关联性：磁有序态的低能激发是退局域化的，而自旋玻璃有序态的低能激发是弱局域化的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维海森堡自旋玻璃模型中自旋波激发的局域化性质，探讨在存在无序的情况下自旋波激发是流体动力学模式还是局域化模式，以及这些性质如何与底层经典序的对称性破缺相关联。

Method: 采用围绕经典态的半经典展开方法，在领头阶获得有效的二次自旋波哈密顿量，并研究其谱和本征函数的局域化性质，分析重整化群意义下相关性对自旋波哈密顿量矩阵元的影响。

Result: 发现自旋波激发的性质取决于底层经典序在自旋波哈密顿量矩阵元中诱导的相关性的关联性：磁有序态的低能激发是退局域化的，而自旋玻璃有序态的低能激发是弱局域化的。值得注意的是，在磁有序情况下，自旋波退局域化对无序的存在具有鲁棒性，即使在二维空间维度也是如此。

Conclusion: 通过将原始海森堡模型中自旋转动对称性的自发破缺与所得二次自旋波哈密顿量的对称性和普适类相关联来解释这一现象学。推测通过在半经典展开的高阶包含自旋波激发之间的相互作用，可以恢复流体动力学图像，促进遍历行为的出现。

Abstract: The two-dimensional Heisenberg spin-glass model is investigated by means of a semiclassical expansion around classical states. At leading order, we obtain an effective quadratic spin-wave Hamiltonian and study the localization properties of its spectrum and eigenfunctions. We find that the nature of the spin-wave excitations, whether they are hydrodynamic or localized modes, depends crucially on the relevance/irrelevance - in the renormalization group sense - of the correlations induced by the underlying classical order in the spin-wave Hamiltonian matrix elements: low-energy excitations around magnetically ordered states are delocalized, whereas those around spin-glass ordered states are localized, albeit weakly. Remarkably, in the magnetically ordered case, spin-wave delocalization is robust with respect to the presence of disorder, even in two spatial dimensions. We interpret this phenomenology by relating the spontaneous breaking of spin-rotation symmetry in the original Heisenberg model to the symmetry and universality class of the resulting quadratic spin-wave Hamiltonian. We conjecture that the hydrodynamic picture can be recovered through the inclusion of interactions among the spin-wave excitations at higher order in the semiclassical expansion, favoring the onset of ergodic behavior.

</details>


### [218] [Probing the Spacetime Structure of Entanglement in Monitored Quantum Circuits with Graph Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22244)
*Javad Vahedi,Stefan Kettemann*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究使用图神经网络（GNN）从监控量子电路中的局部测量数据重构全局纠缠熵，发现预测精度随可访问时空区域的增大而提高，且所需信息按时空尺度组织。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体系统中的全局纠缠本质上是非局域的，这引发了一个核心问题：是否能够从局部观测中推断全局纠缠。本研究旨在探索在监控量子电路中，仅通过局部测量数据重构全局纠缠的可能性。

Method: 采用图神经网络（graph neural networks, GNNs）方法，将单个量子轨迹表示为有向时空图（directed spacetime graphs），仅从局部测量数据重构半链纠缠熵（half-chain entanglement entropy）。通过改变网络深度和分层时空粗粒化（hierarchical spacetime coarse-graining）来系统调控可访问的时空尺度。

Result: 研究发现，预测精度随着可访问时空区域的增大而提高。当以结合深度和粗粒化的有效时空尺度（effective spacetime scale）表示时，不同架构的结果呈现一致性。这表明重构全局纠缠所需的信息是按时空尺度组织的。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了重构全局纠缠所需的信息在时空尺度上具有组织结构。基于图的学习架构为探索全局量子关联如何从局部测量数据中涌现提供了一个可控的操作框架。

Abstract: Global entanglement in quantum many-body systems is inherently nonlocal, raising the question of whether it can be inferred from local observations. We investigate this problem in monitored quantum circuits, where projective measurements generate classical records distributed across spacetime. Using graph neural networks (GNNs), we represent individual quantum trajectories as directed spacetime graphs and reconstruct the half-chain entanglement entropy from local measurement data alone. Because information propagates through the network via local message passing, the architecture directly controls the spacetime region over which correlations can be aggregated. By systematically varying this accessible scale -- through network depth and hierarchical spacetime coarse-graining -- we probe how much measurement information is required to reconstruct global entanglement. We find that prediction accuracy improves as the accessible spacetime region grows and that results from different architectures collapse when expressed in terms of an effective spacetime scale combining depth and coarse-graining. These results demonstrate that the information required to reconstruct global entanglement is organized in spacetime scales and show that graph-based learning architectures provide a controlled operational framework for probing how global quantum correlations emerge from local measurement data.

</details>

### [219] [Gravitational scattering amplitudes from curved space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20261)
*Carl Jordan Eriksen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文开发了弯曲背景下的引力微扰理论，计算了康普顿振幅（Compton amplitude）的前两阶后闵可夫斯基（post-Minkowskian）贡献，并与平直空间结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于对极端质量比双星系统的探索，特别是弯曲背景在经典引力振幅计算中的应用。虽然这些研究关注双星质量比的自力展开，但弯曲背景的使用本身具有独立的理论价值。

Method: 方法包括：回顾广义相对论和点质量生成的d维度规（施瓦西-坦格利尼解）；在任意背景上量子化广义相对论并推导费曼规则；建立世界线量子场论；开发弯曲背景下世界线耦合引力的配分函数微扰理论；重新表述描述引力子与致密天体散射的康普顿振幅的微扰展开。

Result: 计算了康普顿振幅的第一和第二阶后闵可夫斯基贡献，两者均与平直空间计算结果匹配。此外，二阶振幅显示出预期的红外行为，并与早期无质量引力散射结果一致。

Conclusion: 成功建立了弯曲背景下引力计算的微扰理论框架，验证了该框架在计算康普顿振幅后闵可夫斯基展开中的有效性，为极端质量比双星系统的引力波建模提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Motivated by the study of extreme mass-ratio binary systems, recent work has explored the use of curved backgrounds in computations of classical gravitational amplitudes [arXiv:2308.15304, arXiv:2308.14832, arXiv:2406.14770]. While these investigations concern the self-force expansion in the ratio of masses of the binaries, the use of curved backgrounds is interesting in its own right. In this thesis, I examine how gravitational computations can be done in a curved background. After having reviewed aspects of general relativity and the $d$-dimensional metric generated by a point mass (known as the Schwarzschild-Tangherlini solution), I quantize general relativity on an arbitrary background and compute Feynman rules for gravity in two cases: when the background is flat, and when it is a Schwarzschild-Tangherlini background. I then outline worldline quantum field theory. Using this newly-developed perturbation theory for the partition function of a worldline coupled to gravity in a curved background, I reformulate the perturbative expansion of the Compton amplitude, which describes the scattering of a graviton off a compact object. Having established this framework, I compute the first and second post-Minkowskian contributions to the Compton amplitude. Both are shown to match the results obtained from a flat-space computation. In addition, the second-order amplitude displays the expected infrared behavior and agrees with earlier results on massless gravitational scattering.

</details>


### [220] [White Dwarf Structure in $f(Q)$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20350)
*Rajasmita Sahoo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在对称远平行f(Q)引力框架下研究白矮星平衡结构，发现非度量性修正显著改变高密度区域性质，导致最大质量低于钱德拉塞卡极限，并与超重白矮星观测约束一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探索对称远平行f(Q)引力理论中的白矮星平衡结构，其中引力由非度量性标量Q而非时空曲率描述。研究动机是检验f(Q)引力在强场区域的可观测效应，特别是通过白矮星这一天体物理探针。

Method: 采用静态球对称恒星构型，考虑由冷、完全简并电子物质组成的白矮星。使用二次形式的引力拉格朗日量f(Q)=Q+αQ²，其中α量化与广义相对论的偏离。数值求解修正的恒星结构方程，并结合钱德拉塞卡状态方程。

Result: 非度量性修正在高密度区域产生显著偏离广义相对论的预测。增大α值会改变平衡构型，导致最大质量相对于钱德拉塞卡极限降低，并伴随恒星半径和内部剖面的相应变化。对于α=5×10¹⁸ cm²，获得最大质量M_max=1.3519 M⊙和半径R=2228.85 km，与超重白矮星ZTF J1901+1458的观测约束一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，白矮星可以作为测试f(Q)引力在强场区域可行性的补充天体物理探针。非度量性修正显著影响高密度白矮星的结构特性，为引力理论检验提供了新的观测约束。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the equilibrium structure of white dwarfs within the covariant formulation of symmetric teleparallel $f(Q)$ gravity, in which gravity is described by the nonmetricity scalar $Q$ instead of spacetime curvature. We consider static and spherically symmetric stellar configurations composed of cold, fully degenerate electron matter and adopt a quadratic form of the gravitational Lagrangian, $f(Q)=Q+αQ^{2}$, where $α$ quantifies deviations from general relativity. The corresponding modified stellar structure equations are solved numerically in conjunction with the Chandrasekhar equation of state. We examine the impact of the parameter $α$ on the internal structure and global properties of white dwarfs, including the radial profiles of the metric potentials, pressure, density, nonmetricity scalar, and enclosed mass, as well as the mass--radius relation. While negative values of $α$ were explored, they lead to unstable or nonphysical configurations at high densities; therefore, the analysis is restricted to non-negative values of $α$. Our results show that nonmetricity corrections produce significant deviations from the general relativistic predictions in the high-density regime. In particular, increasing $α$ modifies the equilibrium configurations and leads to a reduction in the maximum mass relative to the Chandrasekhar limit, accompanied by corresponding changes in the stellar radius and interior profiles. For $α= 5\times10^{18}\,\mathrm{cm^2}$, we obtain a maximum mass $M_{\max}=1.3519\,M_{\odot}$ and radius $R=2228.85\,\mathrm{km}$, which are consistent with the observational constraints of the ultra-massive white dwarf ZTF J1901+1458. These findings suggest that white dwarfs can provide a complementary astrophysical probe for testing the viability of $f(Q)$ gravity in the strong-field regime.

### [221] [Nonlinear tails in the Kerr black hole ringdown](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20379)
*Siyang Ling,Sam S. C. Wong*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究将广义相对论非线性效应引发的幂律尾迹（power law tails）从史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black holes）推广到克尔黑洞（Kerr black holes），通过Teukolsky方程分析证实了两种黑洞的非线性尾迹具有相同的幂律衰减行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究表明，广义相对论非线性效应产生的幂律尾迹主导了史瓦西黑洞准正模衰变（ringdown）的晚期波形。本研究旨在将这一分析结果从史瓦西黑洞扩展到克尔黑洞，探究旋转黑洞背景下的非线性尾迹特性。

Method: 采用Teukolsky方程进行研究，使用远场近似（far field approximation）处理径向格林函数（radial Green's function）。通过解析推导获得尾迹幂律表达式，并对β=0,1的情况进行数值验证。此外，通过数值求解Teukolsky方程展示了无质量标量场（massless scalar）非线性尾迹的动态形成过程。

Result: 解析推导得出尾迹幂律为t^{-ℓ-β-s}，其中s为自旋权重（spin-weight），(ℓ m)为谐波模式（harmonic mode），r^{-β}为源衰减率。数值结果证实了β=0,1情况下的理论预测，并显示克尔黑洞的非线性尾迹与史瓦西黑洞具有相同的幂律行为，这与远场区域时空的闵可夫斯基性质（Minkowski nature）一致。

Conclusion: 克尔黑洞的非线性尾迹表现出与史瓦西黑洞相同的幂律衰减特性，这一结果可由远场区域的闵可夫斯基时空性质解释。研究成功将广义相对论非线性尾迹的分析从非旋转黑洞扩展到旋转黑洞体系。

Abstract: Power law tails induced by nonlinearities of General Relativity (``sourced'' or ``nonlinear'' tails) were recently shown to dominate the late time waveform of Schwarzschild black hole ringdowns. We extend the analytical results regarding such nonlinear tails from Schwarzschild to Kerr black holes by studying the Teukolsky equation. Using a far field approximation to the radial Green's function, we analytically derived the tail power law to be $t^{-\ell-β-s}$ for spin-weight $s \neq 0$, harmonic mode $(\ell m)$ and source decay $r^{-β}$. We numerically confirmed these results for $β= 0, 1$. We also demonstrate the dynamical formation of such nonlinear tails for a massless scalar by numerically solving the Teukolsky equation. In all numerical results, Kerr black hole nonlinear tails have the same power laws as that for Schwarzschild black holes, as expected from the Minkowski nature of the spacetime in the far field region.

</details>


### [222] [Singular structures and causality of the Schwarzschild Green's function in the frequency domain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20490)
*Romeo Felice Rosato,Marina De Amicis,Paolo Pani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了史瓦西黑洞格林函数的两个奇异谱分量及其频域解释：低频分支割（branch cut）产生普赖斯定律尾迹的修正，准正规模（quasinormal-mode）谱产生红移响应。研究为基于灰体因子（greybody factors）的唯象振铃模型提供了首个解析证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于深入理解史瓦西黑洞格林函数的奇异谱分量及其物理意义，特别是低频分支割和准正规模谱在频域中的解释。这为最近基于灰体因子的唯象振铃模型提供理论基础。

Method: 研究方法包括分析史瓦西黑洞格林函数的频域特性，重点关注两个奇异谱分量：低频分支割和准正规模谱。通过解析方法研究这些分量与灰体因子的关系，并分析不同源定位情况下的响应特征。

Result: 研究发现：对于势垒峰值外的源，存在两个延迟激活的尾迹贡献，分别来自瞬时响应和振铃信号的后向散射；对于势垒峰值内的源，尾迹被抑制，信号由准正规频率主导。红移项不受背景时空几何特征屏蔽，持续到晚期。

Conclusion: 该研究为分支割贡献在中间时间的唯象建模提供了数学基础，这对未来观测尾迹具有重要意义。同时提供了从中期到晚期存在红移分量的强有力证据，深化了对黑洞扰动波形的理解。

Abstract: We study two singular spectral components of the Green's function of a Schwarzschild black hole and their interpretation in the frequency domain: (i) the low-frequency branch cut, which yields corrections to Price's law tails in the form of inverse power laws weighted by logarithmic terms; and (ii) the quasinormal-mode spectrum, which generates a redshifted response for sources extended toward the horizon. We show that the frequency-domain Green's function can be naturally interpreted in terms of greybody factors, providing the first analytical justification for recent phenomenological ringdown models based on these quantities. For sources localized outside the peak of the potential barrier, we identify two tail contributions activated with a time delay, arising from backscattering of the prompt response and of the ringdown signal. We show that corrections to Price's law can be relevant at intermediate times, when the ringdown still dominates the waveform. For sources localized inside the potential barrier peak, the tail is suppressed and the signal is instead dominated by quasinormal frequencies. In this regime, these spectral components produce both the ordinary quasinormal-mode ringdown and an infinite tower of exponentially decaying terms governed by the horizon surface gravity, the so-called redshift terms. We demonstrate that this component is not screened by geometric features of the background spacetime and persists up to late times, as supported by numerical investigations of perturbative waveforms. Our results provide a mathematical foundation for phenomenological modeling of the branch-cut contribution at intermediate times, which is relevant for prospective observations of tails, and strong evidence for the presence of redshifted components from intermediate to late times.

</details>


### [223] [Canonical and Grand-Canonical Singular Ensembles within a Thermodynamicized Gravity Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20571)
*Wen-Xiang Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文发展了一种针对两种具有奇异行为的系综结构（正则系综A和巨正则系综B）的引力-热力学解释框架，通过轮廓积分和留数分析统一处理其奇异结构，为自引力系统的系综理论扩展提供了数学上一致的途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在为具有奇异行为的两种系综结构（正则系综A和巨正则系综B）建立引力-热力学解释框架，以统一方式处理其奇异结构，并探索将系综理论扩展至自引力系统（self-gravitating systems）的数学一致路径。

Method: 采用轮廓积分（contour integration）和留数分析（residue analysis）统一处理两种系综的奇异结构；正则系综A被建模为恒星型系统，巨正则系综B被建模为星系型开放系统，在引力-热力学框架下分析其能量主导和粒子数参与的不同机制。

Result: 对于正则系综A，主导贡献与质能关系（mass-energy relation）及相应的能量驱动奇异区域相关；对于巨正则系综B，质能等效性和光速不变性的耦合影响导致更复杂的奇异构型，其中粒子交换和相对论运动学必须同时纳入考虑。

Conclusion: 引力-热力学表述为局部奇异行为与全局热力学可观测量之间提供了自然桥梁，使两种系综能在共同的变分和几何语言下进行比较；正则系综更适合封闭或准封闭天体物理系统，而巨正则系综更适合具有显著物质和能量交换的开放大尺度结构。

Abstract: This paper develops a gravitational-thermodynamic interpretation of two ensemble structures with singular behavior, denoted as canonical ensemble A and grand canonical ensemble B. Ensemble A is modeled as a stellar-type system in which energy plays the dominant thermodynamic role under an effectively fixed particle-number condition, whereas ensemble B is modeled as a galactic-type open system in which both energy and particle number participate nontrivially and relativistic effects become essential. Within this framework, the singular structures of the two ensembles are treated in a unified manner by contour integration and residue analysis. For ensemble A, the dominant contribution is associated with the mass-energy relation and the corresponding energy-driven singular sector. For ensemble B, the coupled influence of mass-energy equivalence and the invariance of the speed of light leads to a more intricate singular configuration in which particle exchange and relativistic kinematics must be incorporated simultaneously. We show that the gravitational-thermodynamic formulation provides a natural bridge between local singular behavior and global thermodynamic observables, allowing the two ensembles to be compared within a common variational and geometric language. The resulting description clarifies why the canonical sector is more suitable for closed or quasi-closed astrophysical systems, while the grand canonical sector is more appropriate for open large-scale structures with appreciable matter and energy exchange. This approach offers a mathematically coherent route for extending ensemble theory toward self-gravitating systems and suggests a broader singularity-based methodology for relativistic thermodynamics.

### [224] [Branch-dependent ringdown in black-bounce spacetimes: imprints of matter-source ambiguity on quasinormal modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20594)
*Hao Yang,Chen Lan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了在超越广义相对论的理论框架中，单一时空度规可由多种不等价物质源解释（如各向异性流体或非线性电动力学耦合标量场）支持的源模糊性问题。通过分析Simpson-Visser时空中的轴向引力扰动，发现不同物质源解释会在准正规模（QNMs）的阻尼特性上留下可观测的独特印记，引力波光谱学可系统性地打破这种源解释的简并性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在超越广义相对论的理论框架及广义相对论耦合非线性源中，正则黑洞（regular black holes）和黑洞反弹时空（black-bounce spacetimes）常出现源模糊性（source ambiguity）问题。单一时空度规可由多种不等价物质源解释支持，如各向异性流体（anisotropic fluid）或非线性电动力学（NED）耦合标量场，这构成了理论上的深刻复杂性。

Method: 研究在Simpson-Visser时空中分析轴向引力扰动（axial gravitational perturbations），该时空在临界反弹参数$a=2M$处平滑地从正则黑洞过渡到可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）。针对每种物质源解释推导精确主方程（master equations），通过时域数值演化（time-domain numerical evolutions）并利用Prony拟合提取准正规模（quasinormal modes）。

Result: 在黑洞分支（$a\le2M$）中，非线性电动力学（NED）解释比流体模型表现出更快的准正规模（QNMs）阻尼，这是由于耦合电磁通道增强的能量泄漏与视界吸收共同驱动。相反，在虫洞分支（$a>2M$）中，NED耦合系统产生更长寿命的基本模式，这种减弱的阻尼由类亚辐射（subradiant-like）干涉机制控制，该机制主动抑制向两个渐近平坦区域的辐射损失。

Conclusion: 这种分支依赖的动力学类似于开放非厄米量子系统（open non-Hermitian quantum systems）中的衰变宽度重新分布，表明物质源模糊性会在铃荡波形（ringdown waveforms）中留下独特且可观测的特征。研究证实引力波光谱学（gravitational-wave spectroscopy）可系统性地打破源解释的简并性，为探测奇异致密天体（exotic compact objects）的物理本质提供了新颖的经验途径。

Abstract: Regular black holes and black-bounce spacetimes frequently emerge in theoretical frameworks beyond general relativity, as well as in general relativity coupled to non-linear sources. A profound complication in these frameworks is source ambiguity: a single spacetime metric can often be supported by multiple, inequivalent matter-source interpretations, such as an anisotropic fluid or nonlinear electrodynamics (NED) coupled to a scalar field. We investigate how this fundamental degeneracy dynamically imprints on axial gravitational perturbations within the Simpson-Visser spacetime, which smoothly transitions from a regular black hole (BH) to a traversable wormhole (WH) at a critical bounce parameter $a=2M$. By deriving the exact master equations for each interpretation, we perform time-domain numerical evolutions to extract the quasinormal modes (QNMs) via Prony fitting. In the BH branch ($a\le2M$), the NED interpretation exhibits faster QNM damping than the fluid model, driven by enhanced energy leakage through the coupled electromagnetic channel alongside horizon absorption. Conversely, in the WH branch ($a>2M$), the NED coupled system produces longer-lived fundamental modes. This reduced damping is governed by subradiant-like interference that actively suppresses radiative losses to the two asymptotically flat regions. This branch-dependent dynamics, analogous to decay-width redistribution in open non-Hermitian quantum systems, demonstrates that matter-source ambiguity leaves distinct, observable signatures in ringdown waveforms. Our findings establish that gravitational-wave spectroscopy can systematically break the degeneracy of source interpretations, providing a novel empirical pathway to probe the physical nature of exotic compact objects.

### [225] [Breaking the degeneracy among regular black holes with gravitational lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20596)
*Hong Liu,Xiaolong Liao,Yi Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了Culetu、Bardeen和Hayward正则黑洞在引力透镜、阴影和准正规模三个观测体系中的参数简并性。研究发现，虽然事件视界望远镜观测能提供严格的参数约束，但主要几何可观测量仍存在高度简并，掩盖了非奇异核心的微观细节。研究提出高阶特征和吸积流动态观测是区分不同正则黑洞几何的关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探讨正则黑洞（regular black holes）在不同观测体系中的参数简并问题。具体关注Culetu、Bardeen和Hayward三种正则黑洞模型，分析其正则化参数q在引力透镜（lensing）、阴影（shadow）和准正规模（quasinormal mode）观测中的可区分性，以揭示宏观观测如何掩盖微观几何细节。

Method: 研究采用多观测体系综合分析，包括爱因斯坦环（Einstein ring）数据、强引力透镜（strong lensing）可观测量、事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope）观测、以及高阶特征如李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）和次级时间延迟（subleading time delays）。特别关注从透镜主导的静态流到动态主导的下落流转变过程中的亮度层次变化。

Result: 爱因斯坦环数据约束极弱（q > O(10^3)），且与强透镜观测结合无法改善参数估计。事件视界望远镜观测提供严格约束：Culetu模型q < 0.0466，Bardeen模型q < 0.5115，Hayward模型q < 1.0258。然而，主导阶几何可观测量仍高度简并，掩盖非奇异核心（non-singular cores）的微观细节。研究发现吸积诱导强度剖面的亮度层次在从透镜主导静态流到动态主导下落流转变时发生根本性反转。

Conclusion: 强场区域主导可用参数空间，但宏观观测存在"宏观普适性"问题。为打破这种简并，需要利用高阶特征（如李雅普诺夫指数和次级时间延迟）作为近视界曲率的敏感探针。高分辨率时间和强度剖面对于区分不同正则黑洞几何至关重要，特别是吸积流动态观测能提供关键区分特征。

Abstract: We examine parameter degeneracies in Culetu, Bardeen and Hayward regular black holes across lensing, shadow and quasinormal mode regimes. Our analysis reveals that while Einstein ring data yield extremely loose constraints, with the regularization parameter $q$ exceeding $\mathcal{O}(10^3)$, they fail to improve the parameter estimation when combined with strong lensing observables. In contrast, the Event Horizon Telescope observations provide remarkably tight limits: $0 \leq q < 0.0466 <0.0847$ for Culetu, $0 \leq q < 0.5115 <0.6682$ for Bardeen and $0 \leq q < 1.0258 <1.1881$ for Hayward, which shows that the strong field regime alone dominates the available parameter space. Despite these bounds, leading order geometric observables remain highly degenerate, which masks the microscopic details of non-singular cores. To break this ``macroscopic universality,'' we identify high order signatures, such as the Lyapunov exponent and subleading time delays, as sensitive probes of near horizon curvature. Crucially, we discover that the brightness hierarchy of accretion induced intensity profiles undergoes a fundamental inversion when transitioning from lensing dominated static flows to dynamics dominated infalling flows. These results demonstrate that high resolution temporal and intensity profiles are essential for distinguishing between regular black hole geometries.

### [226] [A Rigorous Jacobi-Metric Approach to the Gauss-Bonnet Lensing of Spinning Particles: Extension to Quadrupole Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20657)
*Hoang Van Quyet*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于高斯-博内定理（Gauss-Bonnet theorem）和雅可比度量（Jacobi metric），建立了研究自旋粒子引力偏转的广义几何框架，考虑了四极矩（quadrupole）效应，超越了传统的测地线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统测地线方法严格局限于极点-偶极子近似（pole-dipole approximation），无法处理自旋粒子四极矩效应。本文旨在建立包含完整Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon（MPD）方程的广义几何框架，研究自旋粒子在引力场中的偏转行为。

Method: 采用基于高斯-博内定理和雅可比度量的广义几何框架，纳入完整的MPD方程，包括Dixon四极矩项（Dixon-quadrupole term）。通过计算物理光线的测地曲率（geodesic curvature）$κ_g$，获得施瓦西时空（Schwarzschild spacetime）中偏转角的解析公式。

Result: 自旋诱导的四极矩（spin-induced quadrupole moment）与黎曼曲率张量梯度（gradient of the Riemann curvature tensor）的耦合产生非测地线力（non-geodesic force），使粒子轨迹偏离雅可比流形的测地线。偏转角的修正项为$δα\propto C_Q s^2 M / b^3$，其中$C_Q$为四极矩常数。

Conclusion: 该框架为通过强场区域（strong-field regime）的引力双折射（gravitational birefringence）探测致密天体（compact objects）内部结构提供了坚实的理论工具，揭示了自旋粒子内部结构对引力偏转的重要影响。

Abstract: In this paper, we establish a generalized geometric framework based on the Gauss-Bonnet theorem and the Jacobi metric to investigate the gravitational deflection of massive spinning particles up to the quadrupole order $\mathcal{O}(s^2)$. Deviating from conventional geodesic approaches that are strictly limited to the pole-dipole approximation, we incorporate the full Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon (MPD) equations, including the Dixon-quadrupole term. We rigorously demonstrate that the coupling between the spin-induced quadrupole moment and the gradient of the Riemann curvature tensor generates a non-geodesic force. This interaction significantly deviates the physical trajectory of the particle from the geodesics of the underlying Jacobi manifold. By explicitly calculating the geodesic curvature $κ_g$ of the physical ray, we obtain an analytical formula for the deflection angle in the Schwarzschild spacetime. Our results indicate that the internal structure of the spinning extended body, characterized by the quadrupole constant $C_Q$, induces a deflection correction $δα\propto C_Q s^2 M / b^3$. This formulation provides a robust theoretical tool for probing the internal structure of compact objects via gravitational birefringence in the strong-field regime.

Abstract: We construct a generalized class of Joshi-Malafarina-Narayan (JMN) naked singularity spacetimes that arise as equilibrium end states of gravitational collapse with non-vanishing tangential pressure. The observational properties of the spacetime are then examined through shadow formation and thin accretion disk emission. We find that when the photon sphere lies in the exterior Schwarzschild region, the shadow is identical to that of a Schwarzschild black hole. Accretion disk spectra show enhanced high-frequency emission compared to Schwarzschild, while deviations from the original JMN model remain small due to strong constraints on the inhomogeneity parameter.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非局域引力项在决定宇宙学动力学中具有重要作用。研究动机源于解释IceCube/KM3NeT实验观测到的高达220 PeV的高能天体物理中微子通量，同时考虑暗物质丰度问题，前提是宇宙学背景根据非局域引力场方程演化。

Method: 方法包括将曲率和挠率（torsion）基础上的非局域宇宙学模型中的非局域项"标量化"，并简化为标量-张量引力（scalar-tensor gravity）标准。采用四维算符$y_{αχ}\bar L_αHχ$来解释中微子率和暗物质丰度，并采用由非局域宇宙学模型中Noether对称性存在推断出的幂律解（power law solutions）。

Result: 研究显示，代表宇宙演化的不同动力学系统对IceCube/KM3NeT探测能量范围内的非局域引力参数高度敏感。通过非局域引力场方程演化宇宙学背景，可以同时解释中微子观测结果和暗物质丰度。

Conclusion: 非局域引力模型能够为高能中微子观测和暗物质问题提供统一的解释框架，且宇宙演化动力学对非局域引力参数表现出显著敏感性，这为通过实验数据约束引力理论提供了新途径。

Abstract: Non-local gravity terms have a relevant role in determining the cosmological dynamics. Here we consider curvature- and torsion-based cosmological models where non-local terms can be ``scalarised'' and then reduced under the standard of scalar-tensor gravity. In this context, we study the role of non-local cosmology with regards to the recent results reported by the IceCube/KM3NeT experiments, which revealed high-energy astrophysical neutrino fluxes up to energies of $220$\,PeV. Specifically, we consider the four-dimensional operator $y_{αχ}\bar L_αHχ$ in order to explain both the neutrino rate result and the abundance of dark matter in the Universe, provided that the cosmological background evolves according to non-local gravitational field equations. We show that different dynamical systems representing the evolution of the Universe can be highly sensitive to the parameters of non-local gravity at energies probed by IceCube/KM3NeT. In particular, we adopt power law solutions inferred by the existence of Noether symmetries in non-local cosmological models.

Abstract: We investigate the detectability of Gravitational Wave (GW) modes (emitted by black-holes and neutron stars) by third generation, ground-based gravitational wave detectors planned to be operational in the next decade. ### [232] [Second-Order Bi-Scalar-Vector-Tensor Field Equations Compatible with Conservation of Charge in a Space of Four-Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20979)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法基于变分原理，首先要求矢量场方程（被识别为电磁场的矢量势）与电荷守恒概念一致。其次要求在标量场为常数时，矢量方程在平直空间中简化为麦克斯韦方程（Maxwell's equations）。

Result: 即使施加了上述两个强有力的限制条件，作者仍未能构造出能产生所有可能场方程的拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）。这导致需要讨论其他限制场方程以获得可行双标量-矢量-张量场方程的方法。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明希格斯场（Higgs field）可以在早期宇宙中产生电磁场。同时，将双标量场与规范张量场（gauge-tensor fields）耦合以构建双标量-杨-米尔斯-张量场理论（bi-scalar-Yang-Mills-tensor field theory）在实践中不可行。

Abstract: The purpose of this paper is to explore, in a space of four-dimensions, the possible forms that second-order, bi-scalar-vector-tensor field equations derivable from a variational principle can assume. In order to restrict this enormous class of field equations I shall first require that the equations governing the vector field (which will be identified with the vector potential of an electromagnetic field) be consistent with the notion of conservation of charge. Secondly I shall require that these vector equations reduce to Maxwell's equations in a flat space when the scalar fields are constant. Unfortunately even with these two powerful restrictions on the form of the field equations I have not been able to construct a Lagrangian which yields all possible field equations of this nature. This situation will lead to a discussion of other ways in which the field equations can be restricted to obtain viable bi-scalar-vector-tensor field equations. Lastly I shall make a few remarks on how the results obtained can be used to show that the Higgs field can generate electromagnetic fields in the early Universe, and that it is not going to be practical to couple bi-scalar fields to gauge-tensor fields to construct a bi-scalar-Yang-Mills-tensor field theory.

Abstract: We consider a broad class of static, spherically symmetric generalized Schwarzschild-like solutions with multiple non-interacting anisotropic fluid sources and derive the coordinate transformation from Schwarzschild-like (curvature) to isotropic coordinates with conformally flat spatial slices. Because the local orthogonal planes determined by these new tetrads, which happen to be the local planes of symmetry will tilt under local perturbations. Abstract: A central issue in the thermodynamics of nonsingular black holes is the apparent violation of the first law. In this work, we use 2D dilaton gravity as a simple theoretical setting to study this issue. We systematically construct a broad class of nonsingular black hole solutions with metric function $A(x)=f(x)+c$, through a procedure that is considerably simpler than in higher-dimensional theories. Using the Iyer-Wald covariant phase space formalism, we derive the correct energy formula and establish a consistent first law for this entire class of solutions. The apparent first-law violation in a previous work is caused by an incorrect choice of energy. Our energy formula agrees, up to a normalization factor for the asymptotic Killing vector, with the Casimir function in 2D dilaton gravity, confirming its interpretation as the physical black hole energy. Our results clarify the correct first law for 2D nonsingular black holes and may provide insights into the first law of nonsingular black holes in higher dimensions.

### [237] [Causal Structure of Spacetime Singularities and Their Observable Signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21187)

Result: JMN-1时空奇点经历从类时（timelike）到类光（null）的转变，而JNW始终保持类时奇点；光子球存在于史瓦西和JNW时空，但在JMN-1中仅出现在类光奇相阶段；径向类时测地线在特定参数范围内出现转向点，表明强场区域存在有效排斥行为。

Abstract: We analyze the causal structure of horizonless compact objects via the light-cone geometry and conformal compactification of the Joshi-Malafarina-Narayan (JMN-1) and Janis-Newman-Winicour (JNW) spacetimes. We show that photon spheres exist in Schwarzschild and JNW, but arise in JMN-1 only in the null singularity phase, establishing a direct link between causal character and null geodesic trapping. We further demonstrate that radial timelike geodesics develop turning points for certain parameter regimes in both JMN-1 and JNW spacetimes, indicating the emergence of effective repulsive behavior in the strong field region. These features lead to distinct strong field lensing and shadow signatures, potentially testable by very long baseline interferometric observations such as those of the Event Horizon Telescope.

Method: 方法包括：在平坦FLRW背景下推导广义熵导致的暗能量密度；使用Hayward-Kodama形式主义获得几何状态方程；进行临界性分析；通过宇宙计时器、PantheonPlus Ia型超新星和DESI重子声学振荡数据进行联合统计分析。

Result: 结果显示：广义熵导致包含H^{-2}红外修正的有效暗能量密度；临界分析揭示了范德瓦尔斯型结构，具有反转的一级相变和非物理的燕尾行为；动态扩展中非传统临界行为持续存在；联合统计分析支持模型的观测可行性。

Conclusion: 结论表明Kaniadakis全息宇宙学（Kaniadakis holographic cosmology）是一个一致的理论框架，成功连接了广义熵、引力热力学和观测可行的暗能量动力学。

Abstract: We study the cosmological and thermodynamic implications of holographic dark energy derived from the Kaniadakis deformation of the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy. Within a spatially flat FLRW background, the generalized entropy leads to an effective dark energy density containing an infrared correction proportional to $H^{-2}$, modifying the dynamics of the apparent horizon. Using the Hayward Kodama formalism, we obtain a geometric equation of state and perform a criticality analysis, revealing a Van der Waals type structure with an inverted first order phase transition and a non physical swallowtail behavior in the Gibbs free energy, indicative of unstable thermodynamic branches. We further examine a dynamical extension including a $\dot{H}$ contribution and show that the unconventional critical behavior persists. The phenomenological viability of the model is tested through a joint statistical analysis with cosmic chronometers, PantheonPlus Type Ia supernovae, and DESI baryon acoustic oscillation data. These results establish Kaniadakis holographic cosmology as a consistent framework linking generalized entropy, gravitational thermodynamics, and observationally viable dark energy dynamics.

### [240] [Quasi-local thermodynamics of Kerr-Newman black holes: Pressure, volume, and shear work](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21258)
*Thiago Campos*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过建立克尔-纽曼黑洞的准局域热力学框架，将热力学相空间扩展至包含几何偏心率参数Y及其共轭热力学剪切张力X。旋转贡献通过剪切功项X dY纳入第一定律，并推导了内能和焓表示下的广义第一定律与斯马尔（Smarr）公式。

Result: 该框架通过勒让德变换（Legendre transformations）将准局域能量与旋转能量分离，从而获得热力学势。旋转贡献被纳入第一定律的剪切功项，几何变形被整合到准局域描述中。

Conclusion: 该研究为旋转黑洞热力学提供了新视角，将视界的几何变形整合到准局域描述框架中，解决了旋转时空热力学描述的难题。

Abstract: While the quasi-local thermodynamics of spherically symmetric black holes is well described by pressure and volume, extending this framework to rotating spacetimes poses a significant challenge. Rotation induces an oblate deformation of the horizon, breaking the direct functional dependence between geometric volume and area. In this work, we resolve this difficulty by establishing a quasi-local thermodynamic framework for Kerr-Newman black holes. We demonstrate that accommodating this kinematic deformation requires extending the thermodynamic phase space to include a geometric eccentricity parameter $Y$ and its conjugate, a thermodynamic shear tension $X$. Consequently, the rotational contribution is incorporated into the first law with a shear work term $X dY$. We derive the generalized first laws and Smarr formulas (Euler relations) for both the internal energy and enthalpy representations, showing that these thermodynamic potentials can be obtained through Legendre transformations that isolate the quasi-local energy from the rotational energy. Thus, this framework provides a novel perspective on the thermodynamics of rotating black holes, integrating the geometric deformation of the horizon into a quasi-local description.

### [241] [Polytropes, logotropes, the universal value of the surface density of dark matter halos, and the value of the cosmological constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21302)
*Pierre-Henri Chavanis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文探讨了天体物理学和宇宙学中对数物态方程（logotropic EoS）与多方物态方程（polytropic EoS）之间的理论联系，并展示了其对暗物质晕结构、宇宙常数等问题的解释潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立对数物态方程与多方物态方程之间的理论联系，并探索其对天体物理和宇宙学现象的解释能力，特别是暗物质晕的普遍表面密度、有效NFW密度尖峰以及宇宙常数等问题。

Method: 方法包括：1）证明对数物态方程是多方物态方程在γ→0极限下的退化形式；2）从Lynden-Bell暴力弛豫理论出发，通过特定的χ²分布相级分布推导多方和对数分布函数；3）分析对数分布函数的能量尾部和密度轮廓特性。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）对数物态方程对应指数γ=0的多方分布函数，其密度有限但压力对数发散；2）对数分布函数呈现ε^{-5/2}的幂律能量尾，与基于粗粒化Vlasov方程和长期修饰扩散方程的碰撞弛豫理论预测一致；3）引力耦合下产生r^{-1}密度轮廓，可解释暗物质晕的普遍表面密度和有效NFW尖峰。

Conclusion: 对数模型为暗物质晕结构、Tully-Fisher关系、宇宙常数等问题提供了统一的理论框架，可作为牛顿动力学修正（MOND）理论的替代方案，并能精确推导出宇宙常数Λ=1.36×10^{-52} m^{-2}的表达式。

Abstract: We discuss the connection between logotropes and polytropes in astrophysics and cosmology. The logotropic equation of state $P=A\ln(ρ/ρ_P)$ may be seen as a degenerate form of the polytropic equation of state $P=Kρ^γ$ in the limit $γ\rightarrow 0$, $K\rightarrow\infty$ with $A=Kγ$ fixed. The logotropic distribution function corresponds to the polytropic distribution function of index $γ=0$ for which the density is finite but the pressure diverges logarithmically. We show that the polytropic and logotropic distribution functions can be obtained in the nondegenerate limit of the Lynden-Bell theory of violent relaxation for a particular distribution of phase levels given by the $χ$-squared distribution. This provides a justification of the Tsallis entropy from the Lynden-Bell entropy. The logotropic distribution function presents a power-law energy tail decreasing as $ε^{-5/2}$. Interestingly, this ``universal'' power-law tail is predicted by recent kinetic theories of collisionless relaxation based on the coarse-grained Vlasov equation and on the secular dressed diffusion equation. When coupled to gravity, the associated density profile decreases as $r^{-1}$. This may explain the universal surface density of dark matter halos, or account for an effective NFW density cusp. This also accounts for the universal gravitational acceleration felt by a test particle and for the Tully-Fisher relation. The logotropic model can thus provide an alternative to the modification of Newtonian dynamics (MOND) theory. We recall how the logotropic model leads to a very accurate expression of the cosmological constant $Λ={G^2m_e^6}/{α^6\hbar^4}=1.36\times 10^{-52}\, {\rm m^{-2}}$ in terms of the mass of the electron and the fundamental constants of physics.

### [242] [Weakly birefringent screening disfavors fast Hawking-Ellis Type I warp drives via low-velocity cubic tilt scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21352)
*José Rodal*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究霍金-埃利斯I型曲速驱动背景的经向屏蔽是否能在受限的6变量弱双折射变形框架内实现。通过将问题构建为微扰可容许性问题，发现最小成功的容器是一个对称的经向3×3双矢量块，而非简单的秩一单轴本构变形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探究运动学上无旋的霍金-埃利斯I型（Hawking-Ellis Type I）曲速驱动背景的经向屏蔽（meridional screening）是否能在受限的6变量弱双折射（weakly birefringent）变形框架内实现。这本质上是一个微扰可容许性（perturbative admissibility）问题。

Method: 采用Schneider、Schüller、Stritzelberger和Wolz提出的弱双折射面积-度量闭合框架（weakly birefringent area-metric closure framework）。在受限的ansatz类中，首先测试了简单的秩一单轴本构变形（rank-one uniaxial constitutive deformation），然后发现最小成功的容器是一个对称的经向3×3双矢量块（symmetric meridional 3×3 bivector block）。

Result: 在受限的ansatz类中，简单的秩一单轴本构变形无法作为运动学屏蔽机制。成功的最小容器是一个对称的经向3×3双矢量块，其在17变量参数化中占据六个弱双折射变量。在基准角度θ=0,π/4,π/2下进行探索性积分，混合扇区倾斜（mixed-sector tilt）在对称轴上消失。

Conclusion: 研究证据不支持在简化微扰模型（reduced perturbative model）中存在快速壁（fast walls），而较小的亚光速（subluminal velocities）受简化可容许条件（reduced admissibility conditions）的约束较小。该简化弱双折射模型被视为一个导出的探索性特化，而非定理层面的不可行性或存在性证明。

Abstract: We investigate whether meridional screening of the kinematically irrotational Hawking-Ellis Type I warp-drive background can be accommodated within a restricted 6-variable reduced weakly birefringent deformation. The problem is posed as a perturbative admissibility question: whether the weakly birefringent area-metric closure framework of Schneider, Schüller, Stritzelberger, and Wolz can absorb the residual mixed-sector transport generated by that background while remaining within the locally hyperbolic weakly birefringent regime. Within the restricted ansatz class studied here, a naive rank-one uniaxial constitutive deformation fails as a kinematic screening mechanism. The minimal successful container is instead a symmetric meridional $3\times 3$ bivector block, whose sparse image in the 17-variable Schneider-Schüller-Stritzelberger-Wolz parametrization occupies six weakly birefringent variables. This yields a derived reduced working model coupled to the exact background transport system. Exploratory integration, using the irrotational profile together with a shear-based lift envelope, is reported at the benchmark angles $θ=0,π/4,π/2$. The mixed-sector tilt vanishes on the symmetry axis. In the representative coupled case $θ=π/4$, it is approximately cubic only for mild velocities $v\lesssim 1$; at higher velocity it departs strongly from that trend and the signed variable $φ_{17}$ changes sign between $v=2$ and $v=3$. At $θ=π/2$, by contrast, the benchmark values follow the decoupled reduced-model cubic law. The resulting evidence disfavors fast walls within the reduced perturbative model, while smaller subluminal velocities are less strained by the reduced admissibility conditions. Throughout, the reduced weakly birefringent model is treated as a derived exploratory specialization rather than a theorem-level no-go or existence proof.

Abstract: We investigate the influence of boundary terms in gravitational field theories, by considering that in the Einstein-Hilbert action the boundary can be described by a non-metric Weyl-type geometry. The gravitational action and the the field equations, are thus generalized to include new geometrical terms, coming from the non-metric nature of the boundary, and depending on the Weyl vector, and its covariant derivatives. The field equations obtained within this framework generalize the standard Einstein equations by including in their mathematical structure the Weyl vector, and its covariant derivatives. As an applications of the general formalism we investigate the cosmological evolution in a flat FLRW geometry. We obtain the generalized Friedmann equations, which contain extra terms depending on the Weyl vector and its derivatives, arising due to the presence of the Weylian boundary, and which describe an effective, time dependent dark energy. By imposing to the dark energy an equation of state parameter of the Barboza-Alcaniz type, the Friedmann equations can be solved numerically. We compare the predictions of the Weylian boundary gravitational theory with late-time observational data and the predictions of the $Λ$CDM paradigm. Our results show that the Weylian boundary cosmological models give a good description of the observational data, and they can reproduce almost exactly the predictions of the $Λ$CDM paradigm. Hence, the extension of gravitational theories through the addition of Weylian boundary terms, in which dark energy has a purely geometric origin, emerges as a viable alternative to standard general relativity.

### [244] [Entanglement degradation in regular and singular spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21857)
*Orlando Luongo,Stefano Mancini,Sebastiano Tomasi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究计算了在正则黑洞、Reissner-Nordström黑洞和Schwarzschild-de Sitter黑洞视界附近的量子纠缠退化，通过纠缠负性（entanglement negativity）分析标量场在两个Unruh-like模式间的纠缠特性，发现不同几何背景对纠缠保护程度存在差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 除Reissner-Nordström度规外，所有几何结构的纠缠负性$\mathcal{N}$均随区分参数单调增加；Reissner-Nordström度规在特定电荷值处呈现浅局部最小值，且是唯一使负性低于Schwarzschild情况的背景；Schwarzschild-de Sitter时空提供最强的纠缠保护；高频模式在所有背景中均经历较少的退化。

Conclusion: 量子纠缠可作为区分Schwarzschild时空与其他几何结构的有效探针，不同黑洞背景对纠缠退化的影响存在显著差异，其中Schwarzschild-de Sitter时空对纠缠的保护最强，而Reissner-Nordström度规表现出独特的非单调行为。

Abstract: We study entanglement degradation near the horizons of regular, Reissner-Nordström, and Schwarzschild-de Sitter black holes, considering the Bardeen, Hayward, and generalized Hayward metrics as regular black holes. To this end, we compute the entanglement negativity, $\mathcal{N}$, for two Unruh-like modes of a scalar field shared by Alice, who is inertial, and Rob, who hovers at a fractional offset $ρ$ outside the horizon of the backgrounds under consideration. For each geometry, we locally approximate the metric by a Rindler patch characterized by Rob's proper acceleration $a_0$. Because this Rindler approximation breaks down near the extremal limit, we also compute a near-extremal cutoff. Tracing over the inaccessible Rindler wedge yields a mixed Alice-Rob state, from which we evaluate $\mathcal{N}$ as a function of the mode frequency $ω$ and the acceleration $a_0$. In all geometries considered, except for one, $\mathcal{N}$ increases monotonically with the parameter distinguishing that geometry form the Schwarzschild one. The exception is the Reissner-Nordström metric, for which $\mathcal{N}$ exhibits a shallow local minimum at a particular value of the charge. We also find that the Reissner-Nordström metric is the only background for which the negativity falls below that of the Schwarzschild case. Among all cases studied, the Schwarzschild-de Sitter spacetime provides the strongest protection of entanglement. Finally, across all backgrounds, high-frequency modes undergo less degradation than low-frequency modes. These results suggest that entanglement may serve as a useful probe for distinguishing Schwarzschild spacetime from other geometries.

We select a noncoincident connection that naturally follows from the general framework of cosmological models with nonzero spatial curvature. ### [246] [Adiabatic renormalization for modified dispersion relations in cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21995)
*Christian Durán-Romero,Luis J. Garay,Mercedes Martín-Benito,Rita B. Neves*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了修正色散关系下宇宙学背景中标量量子场的行为，重点分析紫外渐近行为如何影响场量子化。研究发现超光速修正色散关系总产生幺正等价量子化，而渐近亚光速行为可能导致不等价的物理描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解修正色散关系（modified dispersion relations）下宇宙学背景中标量量子场的行为，特别是紫外渐近行为（ultraviolet asymptotics）如何影响场量子化（field quantization）。这涉及检验绝热近似（adiabatic approximation）的有效性和不同时间变量定义的量子化之间的幺正等价性（unitary equivalence）。

Method: 通过建立绝热近似有效性的条件，分析不同时间变量定义的量子化之间的幺正等价性。应用绝热正则化（adiabatic regularization）到两点关联函数（two-point correlation function），研究紫外标度（ultraviolet scaling）如何决定所需的减除阶数（subtraction order）。

Result: 研究发现超光速修正色散关系（superluminal modified dispersion relations）始终产生幺正等价量子化，而渐近亚光速行为（asymptotically subluminal behaviors）可能导致不等价的物理描述。紫外频率标度（ultraviolet scaling of the frequency）唯一决定了绝热正则化所需的减除阶数。

Conclusion: 修正色散关系的紫外渐近行为对量子场论在宇宙学背景中的描述具有关键影响。超光速修正保持量子化的幺正等价性，而亚光速修正可能导致物理描述的不等价性，这一结果通过标准、超光速Corley-Jacobson和Unruh色散关系的应用得到验证。

Abstract: We investigate the behavior of scalar quantum fields in cosmological backgrounds under modified dispersion relations, specifically focusing on how ultraviolet asymptotics influence field quantization. We establish the conditions for both the validity of the adiabatic approximation and the unitary equivalence between quantizations defined via different time variables. Our analysis reveals that while superluminal modified dispersion relations consistently yield unitarily equivalent quantizations, asymptotically subluminal behaviors can lead to inequivalent physical descriptions. By applying adiabatic regularization to the two-point correlation function, we demonstrate that the ultraviolet scaling of the frequency uniquely dictates the required subtraction order. These results are illustrated through applications to standard, superluminal Corley--Jacobson, and Unruh dispersion relations.

</details>


### [247] [Exceptional Points in Quasinormal Spectra of Hairy Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22261)
*Lang Cheng,Xiaobo Guo,Yuhan Li,Jun Tao,Peng Wang*

TL;DR: 本文研究了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中有毛黑洞（hairy black holes）准正规模谱中的例外点（exceptional points），并分析了其对铃荡信号（ringdown signals）的影响。研究发现，在例外点处，包含时间线性项的共振贡献模型比标准阻尼模式叠加模型能更稳健地描述铃荡过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准正规模（quasinormal mode）谱中的例外点是量子力学中的非厄米简并点，其特征值和特征函数同时简并。本文旨在识别有毛黑洞标量准正规模谱中的例外点，并研究其对黑洞铃荡信号的影响。

Method: 通过扫描参数空间识别爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中有毛黑洞标量准正规模谱中的例外点。从时域波形中提取准正规模，并比较例外点模型与标准模型对铃荡信号的描述能力。

Result: 在标量准正规模谱中成功识别出例外点。研究表明，包含时间线性项共振贡献的例外点模型比基于独立阻尼模式叠加的标准模型能更稳健地描述例外点处的铃荡过程。该模型能更自然地捕捉与谱简并相关的共振贡献，并能从铃荡信号中实现更可靠的提取。

Conclusion: 例外点模型为描述黑洞铃荡信号提供了更优越的框架，特别是在准正规模谱简并的情况下。该模型能更准确地捕捉与谱简并相关的共振行为，对引力波数据分析具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Exceptional points (EPs) in quasinormal mode (QNM) spectra are non-Hermitian degeneracies at which both the eigenvalues and eigenfunctions coalesce. In this paper, we identify an EP in the scalar QNM spectrum of hairy black holes in the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory by scanning the parameter space. We then investigate its implications for ringdown signals by extracting QNMs from time-domain waveforms. Our results show that an EP ansatz, which includes a resonant contribution containing a term linear in time, provides a more robust description of ringdown at the EP than the standard ansatz based on a superposition of independent damped modes. In particular, it captures the resonant contribution associated with spectral coalescence more naturally and enables a more reliable extraction from the ringdown signal.

Abstract: Based on nucleons ($p$, $n$) and hyperons ($Λ$, $Ω^-$) formed at kinetic freeze-out from a quark combination model, we systematically study the production of light nuclei and hyper-nuclei in the hadronic coalescence picture. We present the analytical formula of the nucleus momentum distribution of two-body coalescence and that of three-body coalescence. We explain the experimental data of the transverse momentum spectra of deuteron ($d$), triton ($t$), helium-3 ($^3$He) and hypertriton ($^3_Λ$H) measured in Au-Au collisions from the RHIC Beam Energy Scan I and II, and also provide the corresponding predictions of different $Ω-$hypernuclei $H(pΩ^-)$, $H(nΩ^-)$ and $H(pnΩ^-)$. Our results are obtained from an open-source implementation of this model in C++, publicly available as a module within the MUSES Framework. This code includes a new numerical method to extract thermodynamic quantities from near-boundary asymptotics in holographic models, introduced here for the first time, which greatly improves numerical stability and performance in comparison to earlier implementations. Thanks to this improved technique, we are able to compute results for many realizations of our holographic model, sampled from a Bayesian posterior distribution constrained by lattice QCD results at zero chemical potential. This allows us to propagate lattice QCD error bars to predictions of transport coefficients in a wide window of temperature and baryon chemical potential, covering the crossover region, the neighborhood of the predicted critical point, and the line of first-order phase transition. An ensemble of boosted decision trees is trained to discriminate between signal and backgrounds, paired with a genetic algorithm optimizer to combine the final classifier outputs. ### [253] [Hyperbolic form factors for Yukawa interactions, and applications to the Earth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21275)
*Pierre Fayet*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文定义了密度分布的双曲形状因子（hyperbolic form factor），即其双边拉普拉斯变换，用于计算地球内部密度分布对新型力（new force）耦合常数限制的影响，并提供了简化密度分布的解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于精确计算地球密度分布对新型力（new force）耦合常数限制的影响，这对于通过MICROSCOPE等实验测试新物理至关重要。密度分布的双曲形状因子（hyperbolic form factor）是确定由新电荷诱导的外部汤川势（Yukawa potential）的关键参数。

Method: 方法包括定义密度分布的双曲形状因子（hyperbolic form factor）作为其双边拉普拉斯变换（bilateral Laplace transform），并与形状因子（form factor）通过对偶性或解析延拓（analytic continuation）关联。对于球体，该因子表示为$\Phi(x = kR) =\langle \cosh \vec k.\vec r\rangle=\langle\sinh kr /kr\rangle$，并展开为矩（moments）的级数。还提出了从$\Phi(x)$的解析延拓恢复$\rho(r)$的反演公式（inversion formula）。

Result: 研究结果表明，简化的密度分布（如$\rho= \rho_0\ 2R/3r$或$\rho= \rho_0\, (\frac54-\frac{r}{R}+ \frac{R}{3r})$）能提供$\Phi(x)$和$\bar{\rho}(x)$的解析表达式，其值与5壳层模型（5-shell model）的结果几乎相同。对于地球，$\Phi(x)=(\sinh\frac{x}{2}/\frac{x}{2})^2$在$x=4$以内精度约为1%；$\Phi(x)= [7x^2\cosh x-24\cosh x+9x\sinh x -4x^2+24]/(4x^4)$在$\lambda > 100$ km（或$m< 2\times 10^{-12}$ eV/$c^2$）时精度在1%以内。

Conclusion: 结论指出，对于$m=10^{-12}$ eV/$c^2$的媒介子（mediator），与无质量媒介子相比，耦合常数限制增加了34倍：对于自旋1媒介子（spin-1 mediator），$|g_{B-L}|< 3.6 \times 10^{-24}$，$|g_B|<2.6\times 10^{-23}$；自旋0情况（spin-0 case）的限制略有不同。双曲形状因子（hyperbolic form factor）是确定地球密度分布对新力耦合限制影响的关键工具。

Abstract: We define the hyperbolic form factor of a density distribution as its bilateral Laplace transform, related by duality or analytic continuation to its form factor. For a sphere it is given by $Φ(x = kR) =\langle \cosh \vec k.\vec r\rangle=\langle\sinh kr /kr\rangle $, expanded as $\sum \frac{x^{2n}}{(2n+1)!} \frac{\langle r^{2n}\rangle}{R^{2n}} $, and similarly for the form factor $ \langle \sin kr/kr\rangle$. It is also obtained from the bilateral Laplace transform of $2πr\,ρ(|r|)$, and enters in the determination of the outside Yukawa potential induced by a new charge for a mediator of mass $m=k=1/λ$. $Φ(x)$ may be expressed as $\frac{3}{x^3}\,(x \cosh x - \sinh x)\ \barρ(x)/ρ_0$, where $\barρ(x)$ is an effective density decreasing, for $dρ/dr<0$, from the average $ρ_0$ at small $x$, down to $ρ(R)$. An inversion formula allows one to recover $ρ(r)$ from an analytic continuation of $Φ(x)$, as $ρ(r) =ρ_0\,(2R/3πr)\intΦ(ix) \sin (x\frac{r}{R})\,x\,dx$.
  $Φ(x)$ for the Earth is essential to determine limits on a new force, as tested by MICROSCOPE, depending on the density distribution within the Earth. Quite remarkably, much simplified density profiles, such as $ρ= ρ_0\ 2R/3r $ or $ρ= ρ_0\, (\frac54-\frac{r}{R}+ \frac{R}{3r})$, provide analytic expressions of $Φ(x)$ and $\barρ(x)$ giving almost the same values as in a 5-shell model. $\,Φ(x)=(\sinh\frac{x}{2}/\frac{x}{2})^2$ is valid to within $\simeq 1\,\%$ up to $x=4$. $\,Φ(x)= [7x^2\cosh x-24\cosh x+9x\sinh x -4x^2+24]/(4x^4)$ is valid to within 1 % for $λ> $ 100 km (or $m< 2\times 10^{-12}$ eV/$c^2$). For $m=10^{-12}$ eV/$c^2$ the coupling limits are increased by 34 as compared to a massless mediator, to $|g_{B-L}|< 3.6 \times 10^{-24} $ and $|g_B|<2.6\times 10^{-23}$ for a spin-1 mediator, with slightly different limits in the spin-0 case.

</details>


### [254] [Recoil corrections to pentaquark molecules with an SU(3) anti-triplet heavy baryon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21572)
*Xiao Chen,Li Ma*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究发现反冲修正（recoil corrections）对重味五夸克分子态的形成具有关键影响，显著降低某些系统的结合能，挑战了传统认为反冲修正可忽略的观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上认为反冲修正对重分子态形成可忽略，但本研究旨在揭示其在重味五夸克分子态中的重要性，特别是对可能的重子-介子束缚态谱系的影响。

Method: 采用单玻色子交换（one-boson-exchange, OBE）模型，研究包含Ξ_cD̅^(*)、Λ_cD̅^(*)等系统的双重重味和隐重重味五夸克态，同时考虑S-D波混合效应和反冲修正。

Result: 反冲修正会削弱某些同位旋单态通道中束缚态的稳定性，显著降低结合能；在Ξ_cD̅^*和Ξ_cD^*系统中尤为突出，尽管有无反冲修正都能找到束缚态解。

Conclusion: 反冲修正对重味五夸克分子态的形成具有不可忽略的影响，会削弱分子态吸引力，这一发现修正了传统对重分子态中反冲修正作用的认知。

Abstract: Recoil corrections, which appear at order $\mathcal{O}(\frac{1}{M})$, turn out to be crucial for the pentaquark molecules with heavy flavor. In the past, such corrections were typically regarded as negligible for the formation of heavy molecules. However, our research manifests the important impacts on the spectra of possible baryon-meson bound states. In certain cases, the binding energy sharply decreases after considering the recoil corrections. Using the one-boson-exchange (OBE) model, we have studied a series of double heavy and hidden heavy pentaquark states with an SU(3) anti-triplet baryon, including $Ξ_{c}\bar{D}^{(*)}$, $Λ_{c}\bar{D}^{(*)}$, $Ξ_{c}D^{(*)}$, $Λ_{c}D^{(*)}$, along with their bottom analogues. Considering both the $S$\--{}$D$ wave mixing effect and the recoil corrections, we find that recoil corrections, working against the stability of bound states in certain isospin-singlet channels, which cannot be ignored. For the $Ξ_{c}\bar{D}$ and $Ξ_{c}D$ systems with $I(J^P)=0(\frac{1}{2}^{-})$, the $Ξ_{c}\bar{D}^{*}$ and $Ξ_{c}D^{*}$ systems, as well as their bottom counterparts, with $I(J^P)=0(\frac{1}{2}^{-})$ and $0(\frac{3}{2}^{-})$, and the $Λ_{b}\bar{B}^{*}$ system with $I(J^P)=\frac{1}{2}(\frac{1}{2}^{-})$ and $\frac{1}{2}(\frac{3}{2}^{-})$, although the bound state solution can be found both with and without considering the recoil corrections, the inclusion of recoil corrections weakens the attraction of the molecules. This phenomenon arising from recoil corrections is especially prominent in the $Ξ_{c}\bar{D}^{*}$ and $Ξ_{c}D^{*}$ systems.

### [255] [Isospin-breaking effects of the double-charm molecular pentaquarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21667)

TL;DR: 该研究在单玻色子交换势框架下，分析了双粲分子五夸克态$D^{(*)}Σ_c^{(*)}$的同位旋破缺效应，发现其对结合能贡献约10%-30%的显著修正，特别在弱束缚分子候选态中尤为明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于精确分析双粲分子五夸克态的同位旋破缺效应，这些效应来自强相互作用（表现为同位旋多重态中$D^{(*)}Σ_c^{(*)}$组分的阈值差异及交换介子质量劈裂）和电磁相互作用，为理论计算匹配快速发展的实验项目提供必要精度。

Method: 采用单玻色子交换势（one-boson-exchange potential）框架，计算$D^{(*)}Σ_c^{(*)}$系统的结合性质及$I=1/2$与$I=3/2$态之间的同位旋混合角，同时考虑强相互作用和电磁相互作用的同位旋破缺来源。

Result: 计算结果表明同位旋破缺效应对结合能贡献约10%-30%的显著修正，该效应在弱束缚分子候选态（具有小结合能和大均方根半径特征）中尤为明显，对理论计算精度具有重要影响。

Conclusion: 明确包含同位旋破缺效应对于实现理论计算精度至关重要，以匹配快速发展的实验项目，研究结果为未来类氘分子态的高精度实验研究提供了有价值的指导。

Abstract: We investigate isospin-breaking effects in double-charm molecular pentaquarks with the $D^{(*)}Σ_c^{(*)}$ configuration, using the one-boson-exchange potential framework. In these systems, the isospin-breaking effects arise from two sources: the strong interaction, which manifests as the threshold difference of the $D^{(*)}Σ_c^{(*)}$ components in the same isospin multiplet and the mass splittings of the exchanged isovector mesons ($π$ and $ρ$); and the electromagnetic interaction between charged $D^{(*)}$ and $Σ_c^{(*)}$ components. We calculate the binding properties and the isospin mixing angle between the $I=1/2$ and $I=3/2$ states of the $D^{(*)}Σ_c^{(*)}$ system. Our results show that the isospin-breaking effect contributes a significant correction of roughly $10\%-30\%$ to the binding energy. This effect is particularly pronounced in loosely bound molecular candidates, which are characterized by small binding energies and large root-mean-square radii. We therefore conclude that the explicit inclusion of isospin-breaking effects is essential for achieving the precision in theoretical calculations necessary to match rapidly advancing experimental programs. Our results are expected to provide valuable guidance for future high-precision experimental studies of deuteron-like molecular states.

</details>


### [256] [Jet quenching and its substructure dependence due to color decoherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22014)
*Xiang-Pan Duan,Lin Chen,Guo-Liang Ma,Carlos A. Salgado,Bin Wu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出一个结合真空样发射（vacuum-like emissions）和介质诱导辐射（medium-induced radiation）的理论框架，用于描述QCD介质中的喷注淬火（jet quenching）现象及其对喷注锥角大小和子结构的依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于QCD介质中的颜色相干（color coherence）和退相干（decoherence）效应，旨在建立一个能够描述喷注淬火及其对喷注锥角大小和子结构依赖性的理论框架。

Method: 方法结合了真空样演化（使用双对数近似下的生成函数方法）和介质诱导能量损失（采用BDMPS-Z形式体系）。QCD体介质通过OSU (2+1)维粘性流体力学建模，将红外动量标度Q₀和流体力学演化初始时刻的喷注淬火参数作为自由参数。

Result: 该方法很好地描述了ATLAS实验在√s_NN=5.02 TeV的0-10% PbPb碰撞中测量的大半径喷注的包容喷注修正因子R_AA及其对喷注子结构的依赖性。

Conclusion: 提出的理论框架成功结合了真空演化和介质诱导辐射，为理解QCD介质中喷注淬火现象及其对喷注几何特征的依赖性提供了有效的描述工具。

Abstract: Motivated by color coherence and decoherence effects in the QCD medium, we propose a theoretical framework that combines vacuum-like emissions and medium-induced radiation to study jet quenching and its dependence on jet cone sizes and substructure. In our approach, a jet produced at a hard scale $Q$ first undergoes vacuum-like evolution, as described by the well-established generating-function method in the double logarithmic approximation. These vacuum-like emissions generate subjets at an infrared momentum scale $Q_0$. Each subjet then experiences medium-induced energy loss as described by the BDMPS-Z formalism. By modeling the QCD bulk medium using OSU (2+1)-dimensional viscous hydrodynamics and treating $Q_0$ together with the jet-quenching parameters at the initial proper time of the hydrodynamic evolution as free parameters, our approach provides a very good description of the inclusive jet modification factor $R_{AA}$ for large-radius jets and its dependence on jet substructure in 0-10% PbPb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}} = 5.02~\rm{TeV}$, as measured by the ATLAS experiment.

### [257] [Spacelike and timelike structure functions: a dispersive crossing relation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21779)
*Aniruddha Venkata*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新的色散方法（dispersive proposal）用于分析延拓（analytic continuation）强子张量（hadronic tensor），建立了连接深度非弹性散射（deep inelastic scattering）和半包含电子-正电子湮灭（semi-inclusive electron-positron annihilation）的减除色散关系（subtracted dispersion relations）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Drell、Levy和Yan先前的研究表明，交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）暗示深度非弹性散射和半包含电子-正电子湮灭由单一前向振幅（forward amplitude）的解析延拓所支配。他们识别了电流关联子（current correlator）解析延拓的障碍，但未完全解决该问题。

Method: 作者提出了一种新的色散方法用于关联子的解析延拓，假设多项式有界性（polynomial boundedness）并推导了连接类空（spacelike）和类时（timelike）截面的减除色散关系。引入了一个新的因子化函数（factorized function）来量化交叉障碍，并计算了其最低阶硬核（hard kernel）。

Result: 建立的色散关系将深度非弹性散射中的分布函数（distribution functions）与湮灭过程中的碎裂函数（fragmentation functions）联系起来。该恒等式为连接这两种不同物理过程的分布函数提供了数学框架。

Conclusion: 该工作补充了Drell-Levy-Yan的观察，通过新的色散方法实现了关联子的解析延拓，建立了连接类空和类时截面的理论关系，为理解深度非弹性散射和电子-正电子湮灭之间的交叉对称性提供了更完整的理论框架。

Abstract: Crossing symmetry suggests that deep inelastic scattering and semi inclusive electron-positron annihilation are governed by analytic continuations of a single forward amplitude. Drell, Levy, and Yan proposed that the hadronic tensor admits analytic continuation and demonstrated, in reasonable models, that connected contributions to the cross-section continue. They also identified obstructions to continuation of the current correlator. In this work we supplement their observation with a new dispersive proposal for analytic continuation of the correlator and, assuming polynomial boundedness, derive subtracted dispersion relations relating spacelike and timelike cross sections. We introduce a new factorized function that quantifies the obstruction to crossing and compute its hard kernel at lowest order. The resulting identity connects distribution functions in deep inelastic scattering to fragmentation functions in annihilation.

</details>


### [258] [Kinky vortons in the 2HDM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22040)
*Richard A. Battye,Steven J. Cotterill,Adam K. Thomasson*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Z₂对称全局双希格斯二重态模型（2HDM）中构建并分析了二维载流环状解，称为扭结涡旋子（kinky vortons），证明了其在非轴对称扰动下的动态稳定性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索标准模型（Standard Model）现象学扩展中的涡旋子（vorton）解可行性，并为U(1)对称2HDM中的涡旋子提供计算上可处理的代理模型。

Method: 采用薄弦近似（thin string approximation）和弹性弦形式体系（elastic string formalism）来描述扭结涡旋子解，这些方法能准确捕捉其平衡半径和动态振荡频率。

Conclusion: Z₂对称理论中的扭结涡旋子确立了标准模型现象学扩展中涡旋子解的可行性，并提出了三维环境中可能产生类似扭结涡旋子缺陷的机制。

Abstract: We construct and analyse two-dimensional, current-carrying ring solutions, known as kinky vortons, in the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric global two-Higgs-doublet model (2HDM). We demonstrate the existence of multiple dynamically stable configurations that persist under non-axially symmetric perturbations. These solutions are described with high accuracy by the thin string approximation and elastic string formalism, which correctly capture both their equilibrium radii and dynamical oscillation frequencies. Kinky vortons in the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric theory establish the viability of vorton solutions in a phenomenologically motivated extension of the Standard Model, and should provide a computationally tractable proxy for vortons in the $U(1)$-symmetric 2HDM. In addition, we identify a composite domain wall configuration in which localized condensates are supported on secondary domain walls existing on a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ wall, suggesting a mechanism by which kinky-vorton-like defects could arise in a three dimensional setting.

### [259] [Theoretical Ion Sputtering Yields from Loose Powders using a Multiscale Monte Carlo Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20251)
*Sebastien Verkercke,Deborah Berhanu,Caixia Bu,Benjamin Clouter-Gergen,Francois Leblanc,Jesse R. Lewis,Liam S. Morrissey,Daniel W. Savin*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 该研究开发了多尺度蒙特卡洛模型模拟松散粉末的离子溅射，发现粉末溅射与平坦表面存在显著差异，并推导出两种拟合函数来描述粉末溅射产额和角分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 松散粉末的离子溅射（ion sputtering）在行星科学和工业应用中具有重要意义，但目前对其理解仍然不足。现有研究主要关注平坦表面或粗糙表面的溅射行为，缺乏对粉末材料溅射特性的系统认识。

Method: 研究开发了多尺度蒙特卡洛（multiscale Monte Carlo）模型来模拟粉末溅射，采用比基于体素（voxel-based）方法更高保真度的靶材几何结构。模拟了Kr+离子轰击Cu粉末和平坦铜板的溅射过程。

Result: 研究发现粉末溅射与平坦表面存在四个主要差异：1）入射角α>0°时，逃逸溅射产额（escaping sputtering yield）在所有离子能量下都以后向喷射物（backward-directed ejecta）为主；2）α<60°时，产额峰值朝向离子束源，类似于无大气天体光学观测中的冲效应（opposition effect）；3）角分布峰值仅为平坦表面的一半或更少；4）离子能量增加时，喷射物角分布中未出现从初级到次级碰撞溅射的演化。这些行为归因于粉末的相互连接空隙（interconnected voids）。

Conclusion: 研究推导出两种拟合函数：1）将粉末逃逸溅射产额与平坦表面产额相关联，仅取决于孔隙率、入射角、平均局部入射角及相应的平坦表面产额；2）提供孔隙率>0.49时逃逸喷射物的双微分角分布（double-differential angular distribution）。这些函数为松散粉末的绝对双微分逃逸溅射产额提供了潜在的普适拟合函数。

Abstract: Ion sputtering from loose powders remains poorly understood despite its relevance to planetary science and industry. We developed a multiscale Monte Carlo model to simulate sputtering from powders, using a higher-fidelity approach for the target geometry compared to voxel-based methods. Simulating Kr+ ions impacting Cu powders and flat slabs, we show that sputtering from loose powders differs markedly from that of flat slabs or rough surfaces. The main differences are: (1) for incident angles a > 0 degree relative to the bulk normal, the escaping sputtering yield is dominated by backward-directed ejecta for all ion energies; (2) for a < 60 degrees, the yield peaks toward the ion-beam origin, similar to the opposition effect seen in optical observations of airless bodies; (3) the angular distribution peak is half or less than that of a flat slab; (4) as ion energy increases, no evolution occurs from primary to secondary knock-on sputtering in the ejecta angular distribution. We attribute these behaviors to the powders interconnected voids. Ions penetrate these voids and sputter underlying grains; the ejecta then preferentially escape toward the ion-beam origin, where shadowing is minimal. We derive two fitting functions: 1) relating the escaping sputtering yield of a powder to that of a flat surface, depending only on porosity, incident angle, mean local incidence angle, and the corresponding flat slab yield; 2) providing the double-differential angular distribution of the escaping ejecta for porosities > 0.49. These provide a potentially universal fitting function of the absolute doubly-differential escaping sputtering yield from loose powders.

</details>
